We introduce VISTAQA, a comprehensive benchmark for joint evaluation of free-form answer correctness and pixel-level evidence grounding in visual question answering. VISTAQA comprises 1,157 expert-curated samples spanning six task types and six visual domains, ranging from direct perception to compositional and relational reasoning. VISTAQA requires models to not only answer correctly, but to also provide precise segmentation masks that support their answers. It also includes hallucination-aware examples where no valid visual evidence exists. To support this enhanced evaluation, we introduce GROVE, a unified evaluation metric that enforces joint correctness by combining textual accuracy and grounding quality via a per-sample geometric mean, ensuring neither dimension can compensate for deficiencies in the other. Comprehensive experiments across grounding-aware models and hybrid pipelines with general-purpose MLLMs reveal that even the strongest systems achieve limited performance under GROVE, highlighting a substantial gap between answer accuracy and visual evidence alignment.

### [42] [Rethinking Cross-Layer Information Routing in Diffusion Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20708)
*Chao Xu,Maohua Li,Qirui Li,Yixuan Xu,Yanke Zhou,Yunhe Li,Cuifeng Shen,Hanlin Tang,Kan Liu,Tao Lan,Lin Qu,Shao-Qun Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文系统分析了扩散Transformer（DiTs）中跨层信息流，发现传统残差连接存在信息单调增长、梯度急剧衰减和块级冗余等问题。为此提出Diffusion-Adaptive Routing（DAR），一种可学习、时间步自适应、非增量的子层输出聚合机制，兼容多种现代Transformer优化方法（如REPA）。在ImageNet 256×256上，DAR使SiT-XL/2的FID提升2.11（7.56 vs. 9.67），并以8.75倍更少迭代次数达到基线质量；结合REPA可实现训练加速2倍。DAR还可用于大模型微调与分布匹配蒸馏，有效保留高频细节。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统残差连接在扩散Transformer中导致信息流问题，如单调增长、梯度衰减和冗余，限制了模型性能与训练效率，亟需新的跨层信息路由机制。

Method: 提出Diffusion-Adaptive Routing（DAR），通过可学习、时间步自适应、非增量的方式对子层输出进行历史聚合，替代传统残差连接，并与现有增强技术兼容。

Result: 在ImageNet 256×256上，DAR显著降低FID（7.56 vs. 9.67），减少8.75倍训练迭代；结合REPA实现2倍训练加速；在微调与蒸馏中保持高频细节。

Conclusion: 跨层信息路由是扩散建模中被低估的设计维度，DAR作为通用且高效的残差替代方案，为高效扩散生成提供了新方向。

Abstract: Diffusion Transformers (DiTs) have become a de facto backbone of modern visual generation, and nearly every major axis of their design -- tokenization, attention, conditioning, objectives, and latent autoencoders -- has been extensively revisited. The residual stream that governs how information accumulates across layers, however, has been directly inherited from the original Transformer. In this paper, we present a systematic empirical analysis of cross-layer information flow in DiTs, jointly along depth and denoising timestep, and identify three concrete symptoms of traditional residual addition, namely monotonic forward magnitude inflation, sharp backward gradient decay, and pronounced block-wise redundancy. Motivated by this diagnosis, we propose Diffusion-Adaptive Routing (\textsc{DAR}), a drop-in residual replacement that performs \emph{learnable, timestep-adaptive, and non-incremental} aggregation over the history of sublayer outputs. Moreover, the proposed \textsc{DAR} is compatible with many modern Transformer enhancement methods, such as REPA. On ImageNet $256\times256$, \textsc{DAR} improves SiT-XL/2 by $2.11$ FID ($7.56$ vs.\ $9.67$) and matches the baseline's converged quality with $8.75\times$ fewer training iterations. Stacked on top of REPA, it yields a $2\times$ training acceleration in the early stage, suggesting cross-layer information routing as an underexplored design axis in diffusion modeling, one that operates orthogonally to existing representation-alignment objectives. Beyond pretraining, \textsc{DAR} can also be applied during the fine-tuning stage of large-scale T2I models and preserves high-frequency details during Distribution Matching Distillation.

</details>


### [43] [SAVER: Selective As-Needed Vision Evidence for Multimodal Information Extraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20713)
*Miaobo Hu,Shuhao Hu,Bokun Wang,Rui Chen,Xin Wang,Xiaobo Guo,Daren Zha,Jun Xiao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: SAVER提出一种选择性视觉调用框架，用于社交媒体中的多模态命名实体识别和关系抽取。它通过一个基于置信区间的视觉可定位性门控机制判断是否需要调用视觉信息，并在激活时利用子模函数选择相关且多样化的图像子集，结合集合变换器进行聚合，最后通过能量驱动的联合评分头完成分类任务。实验表明，SAVER在保持高精度的同时显著降低计算开销和延迟，优于纯文本及始终融合视觉的基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 社交媒体多模态信息中存在多个弱相关、冗余甚至误导性的图像，导致始终开启的多模态融合浪费计算资源并放大虚假视觉信号，因此需要智能判断何时调用视觉信息以及调用哪些图像以提供可信证据。

Method: SAVER采用Conformal Groundability Gate（CGG）评估文本片段的视觉可定位性，基于实体对生成激活信号，并通过符合式校准确定阈值；激活后使用子模函数选择最具代表性和多样性的图像子集，经由Set Transformer聚合，再通过能量启发的联合评分头整合文本、可选视觉证据、图文一致性及稀疏路由信息完成分类任务。

Result: SAVER在多个指标上均优于强基线模型：提升F1分数，降低AURC（异常不确定性率），在固定风险水平下提高激活覆盖率，同时显著减少浮点运算量（FLOPs）和P90延迟，证明其高效性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: SAVER实现了视觉信息的按需调用，在保证性能的前提下大幅降低计算开销，为复杂多模态场景下的高效信息抽取提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Multimodal IE in social media is difficult because a post may attach multiple images that are weakly related, redundant, or even misleading with respect to the text. In this setting, always-on multimodal fusion wastes computation and can amplify spurious visual cues. The core challenge is to decide, for each candidate span or marked entity pair, whether vision should be consulted at all and, if so, which small subset of images provides trustworthy evidence.
  We propose SAVER, a selective vision-as-needed framework for multimodal named entity recognition and multimodal relation extraction. SAVER uses a Conformal Groundability Gate (CGG) to estimate span-level visual groundability in MNER, derive pair-level activation in MRE from the two marked entities, and calibrate the activation threshold on a held-out split via a conformal-style procedure with Clopper--Pearson upper bounds. When activated, a submodular relevance--diversity selector chooses a compact evidence subset across images, which is then aggregated by a Set Transformer. An energy-inspired joint scoring head combines text, optional visual evidence, text--image consistency, and sparse routing for entity typing or relation classification.
  Experiments show that SAVER consistently improves F1 over strong text-only and always-on multimodal baselines, while reducing AURC, increasing activation coverage at a fixed risk level, and lowering FLOPs and P90 latency.

### [44] [Holistic Reliability Propagation: Decoupling Annotation and Prediction for Robust Noisy-Label](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20725)
*Jingyang Mao,Ningkang Peng,Yanhui Gu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: HRP通过分离标签和伪标签的可靠性，利用双层元学习估计每样本的alpha（标签可靠性）和beta（伪标签可靠性），并分别在不同目标中使用：输入分支采用全局门控的可靠性感知Mixup，对比分支则用beta门控的伪标签正例。该方法在合成与真实数据集上均优于强基线，尤其在高噪声下表现稳健。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将外部标注和模型预测合并为单一可靠性权重，但两者失效原因不同，导致可靠性估计不准确；本文旨在解耦两种来源的可靠性以提升噪声标签学习效果。

Method: 提出Holistic Reliability Propagation（HRP）框架，采用双层元学习生成每样本的标签可靠性（alpha）与伪标签可靠性（beta），并设计可靠性感知Mixup与beta门控的对比学习策略，实现差异化的可靠性传播。

Result: 在合成及真实世界多模态分类基准上，HRP显著提升平均准确率，尤其在高噪声环境下仍保持竞争力，优于现有强基线方法。

Conclusion: 解耦标签与伪标签的可靠性有助于更精准地建模噪声，HRP通过灵活的可靠性传播机制有效提升了噪声标签学习性能，为多媒体分类中的鲁棒训练提供了新思路。

Abstract: Learning with noisy labels in multimedia classification often combines external annotations and model predictions into a single reliability weight, even though the two sources can fail for different reasons. We instead estimate disentangled reliabilities: bilevel meta-learning produces two batch-normalized scalars per sample, alpha for the given label and beta for the pseudo-label, without constraining them to sum to one. Holistic Reliability Propagation (HRP) then routes them to different objectives, using reliability-aware Mixup with global gating on the input branch and beta-gated pseudo-label positives on the contrastive branch. On synthetic and real-world benchmarks, HRP improves average accuracy over strong baselines and remains competitive at the highest noise rates.

### [45] [GAMR: Geometric-Aware Manifold Regularization with Virtual Outlier Synthesis for Learning with Noisy Labels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20727)
*Ningkang Peng,Jingyang Mao,Xiaoqian Peng,Peirong Ma,Xichen Yang,Weiguang Qu,Yanhui Gu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新型几何感知流形正则化范式，通过主动合成虚拟异常样本构建数据流形间的能量屏障，增强类内紧凑性和类间分离性，从而提升模型对噪声标签的鲁棒性。该方法不依赖噪声模式假设，可无缝集成至现有样本选择框架，显著优于当前SOTA方法，尤其在非对称噪声下表现突出，并强化了模型在分布外检测中的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法多通过被动过滤干净样本缓解噪声标签带来的性能下降，但难以区分困难样本与噪声样本，导致性能瓶颈。本文首次强调主动重塑特征空间几何结构的重要性，以解决此问题。

Method: 提出几何感知流形正则化范式，通过主动合成虚拟异常样本，在特征空间中构建能量屏障，施加几何约束以促进类内紧凑和类间分离。

Result: 在CIFAR-10等多个基准上超越现有SOTA方法，尤其在高挑战性的非对称噪声环境下优势明显；同时显著提升模型在分布外检测中的性能，增强开放世界场景下的可靠性与安全性。

Conclusion: 主动重构特征空间几何结构是应对噪声标签的关键，所提范式具有高度通用性与可集成性，为鲁棒学习提供了新思路。

Abstract: Deep neural networks (DNNs) experience significant performance degradation when processing noisy labels, primarily due to overfitting on mislabeled data. Current mainstream approaches attempt to mitigate this issue by passively filtering clean samples during training. However, simple sample filtering within feature spaces degraded by noise struggles to distinguish between challenging samples and noisy samples, creating a bottleneck for model performance. We highlight for the first time the fundamental importance of actively reshaping feature space geometry for learning from noisy data. We propose a novel Geometry-aware Manifold Regularization Paradigm whose core idea is to explicitly construct energy barriers between data manifolds by actively synthesizing virtual outlier samples. By imposing geometric constraints that promote intra-class compactness and inter-class separation, this approach enhances the discriminability between hard and noisy samples, leading to the learning of more robust representations. Our regularization mechanism exhibits high universality, with effectiveness independent of any prior assumptions about noise patterns. It can be integrated as a standalone mechanism into existing sample selection frameworks, providing stronger robustness against diverse noisy environments. Experiments demonstrate that our paradigm achieves performance surpassing current state-of-the-art (SOTA) methods on multiple benchmarks, including CIFAR-10, with particularly pronounced advantages under more challenging asymmetric noise conditions. Furthermore, this paradigm significantly enhances the model's capability in Out-of-Distribution (OOD) detection, ensuring superior reliability and safety for deployment in open-world scenarios.

### [46] [Early High-Frequency Injection for Geometry-Sensitive OOD Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20728)
*Chuanjie Cheng,Ningkang Peng,Chenxi Liu,Yifan He,Peirong Ma,Yanhui Gu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出EIHF，一种在输入端暴露高频信息的干预方法，以增强后训练阶段的OOD检测性能。通过频带级MMD²分析发现，高频成分能提供更强的ID/OOD特征区分性，而低频成分则较弱。EIHF不改变训练目标，仅在第一个卷积前引入高频证据，有效重塑类条件特征几何结构，减少马氏距离重叠，在CIFAR-100和ImageNet-100上均取得优异表现，尤其在FPR95方面领先，但在场景中心的Places数据集迁移任务中存在局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有后训练OOD检测器依赖模型训练后已编码的特征几何结构，但该结构对不同频率成分的敏感度不一。研究发现，高频率成分更有利于区分ID与OOD样本，因此需要一种无需修改训练目标的输入端干预策略来主动增强高频信息的利用。

Method: 采用频带级MMD²分析评估不同方法（CE, SimCLR, SupCon, PALM）在不同输入频率上的特征分离能力；基于此发现，提出输入侧干预方法EIHF，通过在第一个卷积前增强高频信号，提升特征空间中的ID/OOD可分性。

Result: 在CIFAR-100和ImageNet-100上，EIHF显著提升OOD检测性能，取得最佳平均FPR95和次优平均AUROC；但在场景中心的数据分布偏移（如Places）任务中效果受限。

Conclusion: 高频成分在特征空间中具有更强的ID/OOD判别能力，通过输入端干预（EIHF）提前暴露高频信息，可在不改变训练目标的前提下有效提升几何敏感型OOD检测性能，但其有效性受数据分布类型影响。

Abstract: Post-hoc OOD detectors score logits or features after training, so their success depends on the geometry already encoded in the representation. We revisit this assumption through a band-wise MMD^2 analysis across CE, SimCLR, SupCon, and the OOD-oriented representation method PALM. In our diagnostic, low-frequency input bands induce weaker ID/OOD feature discrepancy, whereas higher-frequency bands tend to provide stronger separability. This observation motivates EIHF, an input-side intervention that exposes high-frequency evidence before the first convolution without changing the training objective. EIHF is strongest for geometry-sensitive OOD detection: under matched training and scoring settings, it reshapes class-conditional feature geometry and reduces ID/OOD Mahalanobis score overlap. Experiments on CIFAR-100 and ImageNet-100 show gains on CIFAR-100 and the best average FPR95 with second-best average AUROC on ImageNet-100, while also revealing a limitation on the scene-centric Places shift. Code is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/EIHF.

### [47] [TASTE: A Designer-Annotated Multi-Dimensional Preference Dataset for AI-Generated Graphic Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20731)
*Haonan Zhu,Elad Hirsch,Alexandria Minetti,Allison Nulty,Purvanshi Mehta*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该研究提出TASTE数据集，包含10位专业设计师对四种文本到图像模型输出在九个设计维度上的评分，涵盖排版、美学、空间布局、基调等多个方面，并提供每张图像的幻觉标记。研究通过Kendall's tau、多数概率和Condorcet循环等方法验证了设计师评价的一致性，发现其一致性介于食物与电影偏好之间，显著高于随机评分。现有预训练模型（包括多模态大模型和专用评分器）在多数准则上未超过0.55的宏观一致率，且规模扩大并未提升准确性。研究进一步提出一个小型配对差异头，在TASTE上达到0.611的性能，接近人类单人评分上限（0.741），表明当前模型仍需改进以更好捕捉复杂设计判断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前文本到图像模型的训练依赖于单一整体评价的偏好数据，但专业设计师在评估设计时会从多个独立维度（如排版、色彩和谐、视觉层次等）进行考量，单一标签无法反映这些复杂判断。因此，需要更细致、多维度的评估体系来准确衡量生成设计的质量。

Method: 构建TASTE数据集，由10名专业设计师在两个独立群体中对四个主流文本到图像模型的输出进行九个设计维度的评分，并标注图像幻觉情况；使用统计检验（Kendall's tau、多数概率、Condorcet循环）评估设计师间一致性；对比多种预训练模型（包括不同规模的视觉语言模型及专用评分器）在各维度上的表现；训练一个小的配对差异头模型以优化对设计差异的感知能力。

Result: TASTE数据集显示设计师评价具有显著一致性，所有维度均拒绝随机评分假设；现有预训练模型在多数准则上宏平均一致性低于0.55，且规模扩展未能有效提升性能；新提出的配对差异头模型在测试中达到0.611的性能，接近0.741的人类单评上限，表明仍有较大改进空间。

Conclusion: 当前文本到图像模型在复杂设计质量评估上仍严重不足，亟需更精细的评估基准与模型设计。本研究提供的TASTE数据集和分析框架为未来模型优化提供了关键工具，同时揭示了现有模型在理解多维设计判断方面的局限性。

Abstract: Text-to-image models produce graphic design at production scale, but their supervision comes from photo-style preference data with a single overall verdict per comparison. Designers evaluate along several distinct axes, including typography, visual hierarchy, color harmony, layout, and brief fidelity, and a single label collapses them. We release TASTE (Typography, Aesthetics, Spatial, Tone, Etc.): ten professional designers ranked outputs from four current text-to-image models on nine criteria across two disjoint cohorts, yielding 1,600 ratings per criterion plus per-image hallucination flags on the holistic-preference cohorts. We pair the dataset with three contributions. First, a criterion-agnostic signal test framework, using Kendall's tau, majority probability, and Condorcet cycles against exact iid-uniform nulls at p = 4 and R = 5, places designer agreement on graphic design between food and movie preferences and photo-style image quality, with every TASTE criterion rejecting the random-rater null. Second, no pre-trained system in our benchmark, including six open-weight VLM judges from 3B to 33B parameters and three dedicated T2I scorers, HPSv2.1, PickScore-v1, and LAION-Aesthetic-V2, exceeds 0.55 macro agreement with the 5-designer majority; VLM judges trade off position bias against content sensitivity, so scaling moves along this frontier without improving accuracy. Third, a small pairwise-difference head trained on TASTE reaches 0.611, closing roughly half the gap to the 0.741 single-rater ceiling.

### [48] [Sketch2MinSurf: Vision-Language Guided Generation of Editable Minimal Surfaces from Hand-Drawn Sketches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20733)
*Wenda Wang,Anqi Liu,Junqi Yang,Lei He,Luying Wang,Jiachen Lu,Weixin Huang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Sketch2MinSurf 是一种结合视觉-语言引导与极小曲面理论的混合框架，可从手绘草图生成平滑且可编辑的3D表面。通过空间-拓扑编码表示几何结构，并引入S2MS-Loss损失函数以保证几何重建与拓扑一致性。在100个草图测试中，拓扑相似度达0.844，优于现有方法，生成结果无非流形缺陷，可直接用于下游设计流程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生成模型如GAN、NeRF和扩散模型难以处理非欧几里得表面并保持拓扑一致性，无法生成可直接用于设计工作的可编辑流形。因此需要一种能准确捕捉手绘意图并生成高质量3D几何的方法。

Method: 提出空间-拓扑编码，将几何表示为节点坐标与实/虚边骨架的元组；引入基于奖励调节的Sketch2MinSurf结构损失（S2MS-Loss），联合约束几何重建与拓扑一致性；结合视觉-语言模型提供语义指导，实现从草图到可编辑3D表面的生成。

Conclusion: Sketch2MinSurf成功实现了从手绘草图到高质量、可编辑3D表面的转化，具备良好的拓扑控制能力与设计实用性，为交互式3D建模提供了新范式。

Abstract: Converting hand-drawn sketches into structured 3D geometries remains challenging due to the difficulty of representing non-Euclidean surfaces and maintaining topological consistency. Existing generative models such as GANs, NeRFs, and diffusion architectures often fail to produce editable manifolds directly usable in downstream design workflows. We present Sketch2MinSurf, a hybrid vision-language and geometric optimization framework that integrates vision-language guidance with minimal-surface theory to generate smooth and editable 3D surfaces from hand-drawn sketches. The core of our approach is a spatial-topological encoding that represents geometry as tuples of node coordinates and real/virtual edge skeletons, enabling stable topological control during generation. We further introduce the Sketch2MinSurf Structural Loss (S2MS-Loss), a reward-modulated objective that jointly constrains geometric reconstruction and topological coherence. On a test set of 100 sketches, Sketch2MinSurf achieves a topological similarity score of 0.844, outperforming existing sketch-to-shape baselines. The generated manifolds are directly editable and free from non-manifold artifacts. A public art installation at a university showcases the method's potential for human-intent-driven 3D form generation. The dataset and code are available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/Sketch2MinSurf/.

### [49] [Resolving Long-Tail Ambiguity in Unsupervised 3D Point Cloud Segmentation with Language Priors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20737)
*Siqi Wei,Hongbin Xu,Feng Xiao,Tian Lan,Chun Li,Ming Li,Qiuxia Wu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: LangTail提出一种基于语言引导的层次化学习框架，通过引入语言模型中的平衡世界知识，缓解无监督3D点云分割中的长尾模糊问题。该方法利用语言模型构建细粒度、均衡的语义先验，并通过对比对齐注入层次聚类框架，从而在多粒度上引导语义结构形成，防止小类别被主导类别吸收，提升对少数类别的表征能力。在ScanNet-v2、S3DIS和nuScenes上的实验表明，该方法分别取得+13.5、+12.9和+8.9 mIoU的显著提升，验证了语言先验在改善少数类别表示方面的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有无监督3D点云分割方法主要依赖纯视觉相似性聚类，存在长尾模糊问题，即少数类别的特征容易被主导聚类吸收，导致预测严重不平衡。为解决此问题，需引入外部平衡先验知识以纠正视觉聚类的偏差。

Method: LangTail首先从语言模型中构建实体级语义先验，捕捉跨类别的平衡且细粒度的世界知识；随后将这些先验通过对比对齐机制注入到层次聚类框架中，引导多粒度语义结构的形成，从而增强对视觉下采样类别的区分能力。

Result: 在ScanNet-v2、S3DIS和nuScenes数据集上，LangTail分别实现+13.5、+12.9和+8.9 mIoU的性能提升，显著优于现有方法，证明语言先验能有效改善少数类别的表征质量。

Conclusion: 语言模型提供的平衡语义先验可有效缓解无监督3D点云分割中的长尾模糊问题，通过与视觉聚类协同，提升对少数类别的识别能力，为未来自监督3D理解提供新思路。

Abstract: Existing approaches for unsupervised 3D point cloud segmentation predominantly rely on a purely visual similarity-based learning-by-clustering paradigm, which suffers from a fundamental limitation: long-tail ambiguity. In such a paradigm, features of minor classes are consistently absorbed by dominant clusters, leading to severely imbalanced predictions. To address this issue, we propose LangTail, a language-guided hierarchical learning framework that leverages the balanced world knowledge encoded in language models to mitigate long-tail ambiguity in unsupervised 3D segmentation. The key idea is to establish multi-level associations between language-derived semantic priors and visually underrepresented minor classes, thereby compensating for the biased attention of purely visual clustering toward dominant classes. Specifically, LangTail first constructs an entity-level semantic prior from language models, capturing balanced and fine-grained world knowledge across categories. These priors are injected into a hierarchical clustering framework via contrastive alignment. This guides multi-granularity semantic structure formation and prevents minor classes from being absorbed by dominant clusters, yielding more discriminative representations for underrepresented categories. Extensive experiments on ScanNet-v2, S3DIS, and nuScenes demonstrate that LangTail consistently outperforms existing methods by significant margins, \ie, +13.5, +12.9, and +8.9 mIoU, respectively. These results demonstrate the effectiveness of language priors in improving the representation of minority classes in 3D point clouds. The code will be released at: https://github.com/Whisky0129/langtail_official.

</details>


### [50] [STAR-IOD: Scale-decoupled Topology Alignment with Pseudo-label Refinement for Remote Sensing Incremental Object Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20738)
*Yaoteng Zhang,Qing Zhou,Junyu Gao,Qi Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出STAR-IOD框架，解决遥感增量目标检测中的类别遗忘、尺度变化和标注缺失问题。通过子空间解耦拓扑蒸馏（STD）模块对齐类间拓扑关系，缓解尺度变化带来的表示差异；引入聚类驱动伪标签生成器（CPG），利用K-Means动态确定类别阈值，提升旧类检测准确性。构建DIOR-IOD和DOTA-IOD两个新数据集，实验表明方法在mAP上分别优于现有方法1.7%和2.1%，有效缓解灾难性遗忘。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统检测器在学习新类别时易遗忘旧类别，且现有方法忽视遥感图像中普遍存在的类内尺度变化及标注缺失问题，影响知识迁移与旧知识保留，亟需高效增量学习框架。

Method: 提出STAR-IOD框架，包含子空间解耦拓扑蒸馏（STD）模块以传递结构知识并对齐类间拓扑关系；设计聚类驱动伪标签生成器（CPG），基于K-Means动态识别类特定阈值，区分真实目标与背景噪声，缓解标注缺失问题。

Result: 在DIOR-IOD和DOTA-IOD数据集上，STAR-IOD分别取得1.7%和2.1%的mAP提升，显著优于当前最优方法，在保持基类与新类检测性能的同时有效缓解灾难性遗忘。

Conclusion: STAR-IOD通过结构化知识蒸馏与动态伪标签机制，有效应对遥感增量检测中的尺度变化与标注缺失挑战，为该领域提供了高效可靠的解决方案。

Abstract: Remote sensing imagery typically arrives in the form of continuous data streams. Traditional detectors often forget previously learned categories when learning new ones; therefore, research on Remote Sensing Incremental Object Detection (RS-IOD) is of great significance. However, existing methods largely overlook the intra-class scale variations prevalent in remote sensing scenes, which undermines the effectiveness of knowledge transfer and old knowledge preservation. Moreover, RS-IOD also suffers from missing annotations, which cause the model to misclassify old-class instances as background. To address these challenges, we propose a novel framework, STAR-IOD. First, we introduce a Subspace-decoupled Topology Distillation (STD) module to transfer structural knowledge, explicitly aligning inter-class topological relationships and mitigating intra-class representation discrepancies induced by scale shifts. Furthermore, we introduce the Clustering-driven Pseudo-label Generator (CPG), a plug-and-play module that leverages K-Means clustering to dynamically identify class-specific thresholds, thereby guaranteeing an accurate distinction between true positive targets and background noise and alleviating the issue of missing annotations for old classes. We also constructed two Remote Sensing Incremental Object Detection datasets, DIOR-IOD and DOTA-IOD to facilitate research on RS-IOD. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our method outperforms state-of-the-art approaches by 1.7% and 2.1% mAP on DIOR-IOD and DOTA-IOD, respectively, effectively alleviating catastrophic forgetting while preserving strong detection performance on both base and novel classes. The code and dataset are released at: https://github.com/zyt95579/STAR-IOD.

</details>


### [51] [SpineContextResUNet: A Computationally Efficient Residual UNet for Spine CT Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20760)
*K S Nithurshen,Saurabh J. Shigwan*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于Transformer或大规模集成的脊柱自动分割方法对GPU资源需求高，难以在资源受限环境或边缘设备中应用，阻碍其临床推广。

Method: 设计轻量级3D Residual U-Net架构，引入并行多膨胀卷积的上下文块以高效捕获长程解剖依赖，替代高开销的自注意力或RNN机制，优化模型计算效率与内存占用。

Result: 在VerSe2020和CTSpine1K数据集上分别达到88.17%和88.13%的Dice分数；在仅1.7M参数规模下，性能显著优于受限版SwinUNETR，且可在Intel Core i5、8GB RAM等低配硬件上稳定运行，而传统重模型如TotalSegmentator因内存不足无法执行。

Conclusion: SpineContextResUNet是一种高效、轻量、适合边缘部署的脊柱分割方法，具备良好的临床实用潜力，尤其适用于资源受限环境下的点对点诊断与实时处理。

Abstract: Automated segmentation of the vertebral column in Computed Tomography (CT) scans is a prerequisite for pathological assessment and surgical planning. However, state-of-the-art methods, particularly those based on Transformers or large-scale ensembles, demand substantial GPU resources, creating a barrier for clinical adoption in resource-constrained environments or on edge devices. To address this, we introduce SpineContextResUNet, a computationally efficient 3D Residual U-Net designed for rapid spinal localization. Our architecture integrates a lightweight Context Block that employs parallel multi-dilated convolutions to capture long-range anatomical dependencies without the high latency of Recurrent Neural Networks (RNNs) or the memory overhead of Self-Attention mechanisms. Extensive validation on two public benchmarks, VerSe2020 and CTSpine1K, demonstrates that our model achieves a Dice score of 88.17% and 88.13% respectively. To evaluate performance under strict hardware constraints, we compared our model against a bottlenecked SwinUNETR scaled to match our ~1.7M hardware footprint. While the constrained Transformer suffers severe performance degradation due to a lack of spatial inductive biases in a limited-data regime, our CNN-based approach successfully maintains high accuracy. Crucially, heavy baselines like TotalSegmentator fail due to memory exhaustion on commodity hardware (Intel Core i5, 8GB RAM), our model performs robust inference, making it a viable solution for point-of-care diagnostics and deployment on edge platforms like the Nvidia Jetson Orin Nano.

### [52] [Diffuse to Detect: Bi-Level Sample Rebalancing with Pseudo-Label Diffusion for Point-Supervised Infrared Small-Target Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20766)
*Zhu Liu,Yuanhang Yao,Ping Qian,Zihang Chen,Risheng Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种更自适应、稳定的框架，解决红外小目标检测中点标注因复杂背景和低对比度导致的伪标签演化不稳定及样本分布不平衡问题。通过利用热辐射与热扩散的内在一致性，提出物理驱动的标注策略，将单点标签扩展为可靠的伪掩码；并设计双层双更新框架，联合优化检测器权重、样本权重与扩散参数，结合元分类器动态预测样本损失权重，以及可微分扩散模块基于检测反馈精修伪标签，实现训练与超参数优化的自适应交互。实验表明该方法可实现五倍标注加速、更高检测精度，并在仅使用30%数据时达到接近全量数据的性能，验证了其高效性与实用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 点监督虽具可扩展性，但在复杂、低对比度的红外图像中面临伪标签演化不稳与样本分布严重失衡两大瓶颈，限制了其性能提升。

Method: 提出物理驱动的标注策略，将单点标签扩展为伪掩码；设计双层双更新框架，结合元分类器动态调整样本权重，以及可微分扩散模块根据检测反馈迭代优化伪标签，实现检测器、样本权重与扩散参数的联合优化。

Conclusion: 所提方法有效缓解了点监督在红外小目标检测中的伪标签不稳与样本不平衡问题，具备高效率与强实用性，适用于大规模、低成本标注场景。

Abstract: Point supervision has become a scalable solution to address dense annotation for infrared small target detection, but its performance is limited by two coupled bottlenecks: unstable pseudo-label evolution in cluttered, low-contrast infrared imagery and severe sample-distribution imbalance. In this paper, we present a more adaptive and stable framework to address these issues. Leveraging the intrinsic consistency between thermal radiation patterns and heat diffusion, we propose a physics-induced annotation strategy that expands single-point labels into reliable pseudo-masks. To further enhance supervision and alleviate sample imbalance, we develop a bi-level dual-update framework that jointly optimizes detector weights, sample weights, and diffusion parameters. A meta-classifier dynamically predicts sample-wise loss weights, while a differentiable diffusion module refines pseudo-labels with detection feedback, enabling adaptive interaction between training and hyperparameter optimization. Extensive experiments across multiple datasets demonstrate five-fold annotation acceleration, superior detection accuracy, and comparable performance with 30% of the training data, validating the efficiency and practicality of our approach. Our code is available at https://github.com/yuanhang-yao/diffuse-to-detect.

Main category: cs.CV

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于外部扰动的幻觉检测方法缺乏对内部跨模态依赖关系的关注，导致检测不准确，需要更精细的视觉依赖分析以提高检测可靠性。

Method: VIHD方法包括视觉依赖性探测（VDP）定位视觉主导解码层，视觉干预解码（VID）通过掩码视觉令牌校准语义分布，计算校准语义熵（CSE）作为幻觉信号。

Result: 在三个医学VQA基准上，使用两种医学MLLMs的实验表明，VIHD显著优于当前最先进的方法，证明了细粒度视觉依赖性在幻觉检测中的重要性。

Conclusion: VIHD通过引入基于视觉干预的细粒度跨模态依赖分析，有效提升了医疗多模态大模型中幻觉检测的准确性，为临床决策支持提供了更可靠的工具。

Abstract: While medical Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have shown promise in assisting diagnosis, they still frequently generate hallucinated responses that appear linguistically plausible but lack visual evidence. Such hallucinations pose risks to clinical decision-making and necessitate effective detection. Existing introspective detection methods primarily perform uncertainty estimation or logical verification by analyzing model responses conditioned on original or perturbed inputs. However, such external perturbations are often heuristic and context-agnostic, which overlooks the internal cross-modal dependency between generated tokens and related visual tokens during decoding. To address this issue, we propose VIHD, a Visual Intervention-based Hallucination Detection method that leverages targeted visual token masking to calibrate semantic entropy for more effective hallucination detection. VIHD locates visually dominant decoder layers via Visual Dependency Probing (VDP), executes Visual Intervention Decoding (VID) via token masking to calibrate the semantic distribution, and quantifies the resulting Calibrated Semantic Entropy (CSE) as a reliable hallucination signal. Extensive experiments on three medical VQA benchmarks with two medical MLLMs demonstrate that VIHD consistently outperforms state-of-the-art methods, underscoring the importance of fine-grained visual dependency for hallucination detection. The code will be available at https://github.com/Jiayi-Chen-AU/VIHD

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: Experiments show consistent improvements in attribute fidelity across all baselines, demonstrating that AttriLoss enhances fine-grained attribute realization without requiring architectural changes and integrates seamlessly into existing pipelines.

Conclusion: Attribute realization is a crucial, complementary aspect of visual storytelling alongside character consistency. AttriStory advances the field toward fine-grained, attribute-controlled story generation through a modular and effective approach.

Abstract: Visual storytelling with diffusion models has made impressive strides in maintaining character consistency across narrative scenes. However, a critical gap remains: while these methods ensure a character remains consistent across scenes, they provide no systematic method to ensure if fine-grained attributes such as color and textures of clothing, accessories are faithfully rendered in the generated images. Towards this goal, we introduce AttriStory, a benchmark enabling attribute realization in visual storytelling. We curate 200 multi-scene stories across 10 distinct artistic styles using Large Language Model. Each scene is constructed with detailed attribute specifications to enable rich visual narratives. Further, to address attribute realization, we propose a plug-and-play latent optimization module that operates during early denoising steps, when the model establishes structural and semantic content. We achieve this through AttriLoss objective designed to maximize alignment between the cross-attention maps for desired attribute-object pairs while suppressing spurious associations, guiding models to localize attributes correctly. This approach operates orthogonally to existing consistency mechanisms, integrating seamlessly with current story generation pipelines without requiring architectural modifications. Our experiments demonstrate consistent improvements on incorporating AttriLoss across all baselines. This work positions attribute realization as a distinct, complementary dimension of visual storytelling, alongside character consistency, advancing the field toward fine-grained attribute-controlled story generation. Conclusion: 尽管可有效区分真实与生成图像，但精准识别生成模型仍是重大挑战，未来需加强模型指纹技术、提升系统对抗攻击能力，并发展实时检测机制以应对日益复杂的生成内容风险。

Abstract: The rapid advancements in generative AI technologies, such as Stable Diffusion, DALL-E, and Midjourney, have significantly transformed the creation of synthetic visual content. While these models enable innovation across industries, they also pose serious challenges, including misinformation, disinformation, and biased content generation. The increasing realism of AI-generated images makes their detection a pressing concern for researchers, policymakers, and industry stakeholders.
  In this paper, we present the findings of the Defactify 4.0 workshop, which introduced the Counter Turing Test (CT2) for AI-Generated Image Detection. The competition consisted of two key tasks: (1) binary classification of images as either AI-generated or real and (2) identification of the specific generative model responsible for an AI-generated image. To facilitate this, we developed the MS COCOAI dataset, consisting of 50,000 synthetic images from multiple generative models alongside real-world images from the MS COCO dataset.
  Participants employed diverse detection strategies, including convolutional neural networks (CNNs), Vision Transformers (ViTs), frequency-based analysis, contrastive learning, and multimodal techniques. The results demonstrated that while AI-generated images can be detected with high accuracy (F1-score > 0.83), identifying the exact model used remains significantly more challenging (highest F1-score: 0.4986). These findings highlight the need for improved model fingerprinting, adversarial robustness, and real-time detection mechanisms.

### [56] [What Semantics Survive the Connector? Diagnosing VLM-to-DiT Alignment in Video Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20795)
*Hangyu Lin,Chao Wen,Chengming Xu,Jianxiong Gao,Jiangning Zhang,Xiaobin Hu,Yanwei Fu*

Result: 系统评估四个代表性模型案例表明，细粒度结构语义在VLM到DiT的对齐过程中显著退化；验证了语义传递并非无损，确认了对齐过程是当前多模态视频编辑中的主要瓶颈。

Conclusion: VLM-to-DiT的对齐过程存在严重语义瓶颈，导致细粒度结构信息丢失，挑战了现有范式中‘无损语义转移’的假设。研究结果为未来多模态对齐架构的设计提供了新的诊断基准与改进方向。

Abstract: Flow matching based video generative models have been increasingly relying on prepended Vision-Language Models (VLMs) to handle complex, instruction-based video editing. However, we hypothesize that this alignment acts as a severe semantic bottleneck, degrading fine-grained structural variables. Verifying this is challenging, as end-to-end evaluations conflate alignment failures with generation errors, and natural datasets lack disentangled annotations. To rigorously investigate this, we propose a controlled data processing pipeline based on video composition that results in TRACE-Edit, a diagnostic dataset focusing on relation-based editing. Leveraging this dataset, we propose a comprehensive diagnostic protocol to analyze two important designs of meta-query and connector in the existing video editing models. Systematic evaluation of four representative model cases reveals that fine-grained structural semantics can be severely degraded during alignment. Our findings overturn the assumption of lossless semantic transfer, identifying the VLM-to-DiT alignment as a major bottleneck and providing a new diagnostic foundation for future multi-modal alignment architectures.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用两阶段框架：第一阶段预测图像的Canny边缘图以捕捉结构信息；第二阶段结合源图像外观与预测结构生成最终图像；同时构建一个自动化的10万对文本感知数据集，确保跨视角文本一致性。

Result: 实验结果显示，该方法在GPT-4.1评估和知识蒸馏研究中均优于多个基线模型，证明中间结构预测是实现高保真度主题驱动生成的有效路径。

Conclusion: 通过结构与外观解耦及高质量文本一致数据集的引入，所提方法显著提升了文本到图像生成中对细节的保留能力，具有良好的实用前景。

Abstract: Subject-driven text-to-image generation still struggles to preserve high-frequency identity details such as logos, patterns, and text. Existing methods typically operate directly in RGB space, which often leads to detail degradation under substantial edits. We propose a two-stage framework that decouples structure from appearance by first predicting a Canny map and then rendering the final image conditioned on both the source appearance and the predicted structure. To improve text handling, we further introduce a fully automatic pipeline that constructs a 100k-pair text-aware dataset with cross-view textual consistency. Experiments, including GPT-4.1-based evaluation and a knowledge distillation study, show clear gains over selected baselines and suggest that intermediate structural prediction is an effective route for high-fidelity subject-driven generation. Our dataset and code will be made publicly available.

</details>


### [59] [Spatial Gram Alignment for Ultra-High-Resolution Image Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20808)
*Jinjin Zhang,Xiefan Guo,Di Huang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Spatial Gram Alignment (SGA)框架，通过对齐生成特征与视觉基础模型的内部自相似性，在不破坏预训练潜空间的前提下，实现超分辨率文本到图像生成中全局结构一致性和微观细节保真度的平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在高分辨率下直接进行局部特征蒸馏会破坏预训练潜空间，导致生成质量下降，亟需一种非侵入性方法来保留生成模型的原生能力。

Method: SGA通过构建非侵入的空间约束，对齐生成特征与基础模型特征的内部自相似性（即空间Gram矩阵），从而在宏观结构上建立一致性，同时保持生成模型原有的像素级细节还原能力。该方法可应用于扩散过程中的中间特征及VAE潜空间。

Result: 实验表明，SGA在超分辨率文本到图像合成任务上达到当前最优性能，有效协调了全局结构完整性和细粒度视觉细节之间的矛盾。

Abstract: Modern ultra-high-resolution image synthesis relies heavily on the robust generative capacity of large-scale pre-trained Latent Diffusion Models (LDMs). While recent representation alignment methods have proven effective by distilling visual priors from foundation models (e.g., SAM or DINO) into generative latent features, scaling these approaches to pre-trained LDMs at extreme resolutions exposes a critical learnability-fidelity conflict. Specifically, forcing direct patch-wise feature distillation inherently perturbs the pre-trained latent manifold, ultimately leading to generation degradation. To address this bottleneck, we propose Spatial Gram Alignment (SGA), a novel framework that explicitly leverages the representation priors of vision foundation models while preserving the native generative capacity of LDMs. Moving beyond restrictive direct alignment, SGA imposes a non-invasive spatial constraint by aligning the internal self-similarities of the generative features with those of the foundation priors. This spatial constraint effectively establishes macroscopic structural coherence, while the native generative objectives retain the microscopic pixel-level fidelity inherent to the original LDMs. Notably, this versatile strategy integrates seamlessly across both intermediate diffusion features and VAE latents within pre-trained LDMs. Extensive experiments demonstrate that SGA achieves state-of-the-art performance for ultra-high-resolution text-to-image synthesis, yielding an effective reconciliation between global structural integrity and fine-grained visual details. Code is available at https://github.com/zhang0jhon/SGA.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Both tracks require accurately localizing temporal segments from long untrimmed egocentric videos. To address these tasks, we propose a reranking-based framework that effectively leverages the strong video-language reasoning capability of multimodal large language model (MLLM) while preserving the efficiency and candidate recall of conventional localization pipelines. Specifically, we first obtain a set of candidate segments from existing localization model OSGNet, and then employ MLLM to select the segment that best matches the given query, thereby refining the final prediction. Ultimately, our method achieved first place in both the Natural Language Queries and GoalStep tracks. Our code can be found at https://github.com/iLearn-Lab/CVPR25-OSGNet.

### [61] [VSCD: Video-based Scene Change Detection in Unaligned Scenes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20821)
*Jiae Yoon,Ue-Hwan Kim*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Video-based Scene Change Detection (VSCD)任务，旨在从不同时间拍摄的视频中检测像素级变化，支持任意相机运动和非同步视频。构建了包含超过110万帧的大规模标注数据集，并提出一种查询中心的多参考模型，通过隐式时序匹配、局部块对应对齐和置信度融合实现高分辨率变化掩码生成。该方法在基准上达到最先进性能，并成功部署于移动机器人，在视觉监控和增量学习任务中验证了实际应用价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有变化检测方法通常假设固定视角、轻微偏移或仅有少量物体变化，难以应对真实场景中复杂的相机运动、非同步视频及大量物体出现/消失的情况。为实现长期自主系统中的环境感知能力，亟需更鲁棒的视频级变化检测方法。

Method: 提出查询中心的多参考模型：利用变化掩码监督隐式学习时序匹配；通过局部块对应关系将候选参考特征对齐到查询帧；结合帧级与块级置信度进行多参考特征融合，最终一次性解码每帧的高分辨率变化掩码。

Result: 在自建大规模数据集上显著优于现有的图像和视频基线方法；在真实世界测试集上表现出良好泛化能力；成功应用于移动机器人，实现了视觉监控和对象增量学习的实时运行。

Abstract: Detecting what has changed in an environment is essential for long-term autonomy, yet most change detection settings assume fixed viewpoints, mild misalignment, or only a few changed objects. We introduce Video-based Scene Change Detection (VSCD), which predicts a pixel-wise change mask for each query frame, given a reference and a query RGB video of the same indoor space recorded at different times under unconstrained camera motion. The two videos are not temporally synchronized, and many object instances may appear or disappear. To study this setting, we build a large-scale benchmark with over 1.1 million frames annotated with pixel-accurate change masks, together with a real-world test set for evaluating transfer beyond simulation. We propose a query-centric multi-reference model that learns temporal matching implicitly from change-mask supervision, aligns candidate reference features to the query via local patch correspondence, and fuses per-candidate change features using frame-level and patch-level confidence before decoding a high-resolution mask once per frame. Our approach achieves state-of-the-art performance against strong image- and video-based baselines, and we validate its real-world impact by deploying it on a mobile robot for two downstream applications -- visual surveillance and object incremental learning.

### [62] [RelWitness: Open-Vocabulary 3D Scene Graph Generation with Visual-Geometric Relation Witnesses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20823)
*Minh Anh Nguyen,Quang Huy Tran,Bao Ngoc Le,Tuan Kiet Pham,Sui Yang Guang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: RelWitness 是一种在不完整关系监督下进行开放词汇3D场景图生成的框架，通过视觉-几何线索（关系见证）识别物体间真实关系，提升未见关系识别能力，减少幻觉和冗余描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有3D场景图数据集的关系标注不完整，导致模型难以学习未标注的有效关系，同时容易将缺失标签误判为负例，影响开放词汇场景理解性能。

Method: 提出关系见证概念，利用RGB图像、深度图、重建3D几何、角色敏感文本、对象先验空视图及多视角一致性构建关系见证记录；通过视觉-几何验证器对未标注关系候选进行分类，并采用见证引导的正-未标记学习目标，避免将缺失标签误设为负例。

Result: 在3DSSG/3RScan和ScanNet衍生的开放词汇分割上，模拟实验显示：未见关系识别能力提升，见证精度提高，幻觉减少，冗余关系表达降低。所有数值为规划值，需后续复现验证。

Conclusion: RelWitness 有效应对开放词汇3D场景图生成中的不完整标注问题，通过关系见证机制增强模型对真实关系的感知与推理能力，具备良好的可扩展性和鲁棒性。

Abstract: Open-vocabulary 3D scene graph generation seeks to describe object instances and their relations with flexible natural-language predicates. The central difficulty is not only vocabulary expansion, but supervision reliability: relation annotations in 3D scene graph datasets are selective, and many valid object-pair relations are unannotated. We propose RelWitness, a framework for open-vocabulary 3D scene graph generation from posed RGB-D sequences under incomplete relation supervision. The key concept is a relation witness: a concrete visual-geometric cue that makes a relation observable in the captured scene. Support relations require contact and vertical ordering; containment requires enclosure; proximity requires metric closeness; orientation requires facing direction; and stable relations should persist across views where both objects are visible. RelWitness constructs relation witness records from RGB views, depth maps, reconstructed 3D geometry, role-sensitive text, object-prior null views, and multi-view consistency. A visual-geometric witness verifier assigns unannotated relation candidates to verified missing positives, reliable negatives, or uncertain unlabeled cases. A witness-guided positive-unlabeled objective then learns from incomplete annotations without turning every missing label into a negative. We further introduce witness-consistent decoding and an RGB-D missing-relation audit protocol. Simulated manuscript-planning experiments on 3DSSG/3RScan and ScanNet-derived open-vocabulary splits show the intended behavior: improved unseen-relation recognition, higher witness precision, lower hallucination, and reduced redundant relation phrases. All numerical results are planning values and must be replaced by reproduced measurements before submission

</details>


### [63] [ArchSIBench: Benchmarking the Architectural Spatial Intelligence of Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20837)
*Qirui Shen,Wenda Wang,Jiachen Lu,Zilong Huang,Jin Bai,Lei He,Hongxuan Chen,Weixin Huang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了ArchSIBench，一个基于建筑学、认知科学和心理学视角的建筑设计空间智能评估基准，涵盖感知、推理、导航、变换和配置五个核心维度，包含17个细粒度子任务。通过专家手动标注构建了3000个问答对，用于全面评估视觉语言模型（VLMs）的建筑空间智能。实验发现，大多数模型在建筑空间智能方面与人类基准存在显著差距，尤其在空间变换和配置推理上表现不足；尽管部分先进模型接近无建筑训练的人类水平，但仍不及有建筑训练的人类。该基准有望为衡量和提升VLMs的建筑空间智能提供系统性资源。

Method: 提出ArchSIBench基准，结合建筑学、认知科学与心理学视角，设计覆盖感知、推理、导航、变换和配置五个维度的17个子任务，并由具有建筑背景的专家进行人工标注，构建3000个高质量问答对。基于该基准，对多种VLMs进行评估，分析其在不同能力维度的表现差异。

Result: 多数视觉语言模型在建筑空间智能方面显著落后于人类基准，尤其在空间变换和配置推理任务中差距明显；部分先进模型可达到无建筑训练人类的水平，但仍不及有建筑训练的人类。模型在不同能力维度间表现出显著差异。

Conclusion: ArchSIBench为评估和推动视觉语言模型在建筑空间智能方面的发展提供了重要基准与系统资源，有助于揭示当前模型的局限并引导未来研究方向。

Abstract: Architectural spatial intelligence, the ability to recognize and infer architectural space, is fundamental to tasks such as robot navigation, embodied interaction, and 3D scene understanding and generation. Although extensive research has evaluated the basic spatial skills of Vision-Language Models (VLMs) such as relative orientation, distance comparison, and object counting, these tasks cover only the most elementary levels of spatial cognition and largely overlook higher-level cognition of architectural space, including layout understanding, circulation patterns, and functional zoning. In this work, we present ArchSIBench, a Benchmark for Architectural Spatial Intelligence based on the perspectives from architecture, cognitive science, and psychology. ArchSIBench covers five core dimensions: perception, reasoning, navigation, transformation, and configuration, comprising 17 fine-grained subtasks. Through careful manual annotation by experts with architectural backgrounds, we construct 3,000 question-answer pairs to enable comprehensive evaluation of architectural spatial intelligence. Based on ArchSIBench, we evaluate various VLMs and find that the architectural spatial intelligence of most models shows significant differences from human baselines; additionally, models exhibit substantial variability across capability dimensions. Some state-of-the-art models can approach the level of human evaluators without architectural training. However, a clear gap remains compared to human evaluators with architectural training, particularly in spatial transformation and configuration reasoning. We believe that ArchSIBench will provide important insights and systematic resources for measuring and advancing the architectural spatial intelligence of VLMs. The dataset and code are available at https://huggingface.co/datasets/ArchSIBench/ArchSIBench.

### [66] [HDMoE: A Hierarchical Decoupling-Fusion Mixture-of-Experts Framework for Multimodal Cancer Survival Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20891)
*Huayi Wang,Haochao Ying,Yuyang Xu,Qiyao Zheng,jun wang,Cheng Zhang,Ying Sun,Jian Wu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出HDMoE框架，通过双层MoE和RFR模块解决多模态生存预测中的冗余特征与细粒度关系建模问题，显著提升预测性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在特征解耦融合前未有效减少模态特征的冗余信息，且缺乏对细粒度特征关系及局部交互的建模能力，影响预测效果。

Method: 设计双层混合专家（MoE）结构：第一层分离冗余信息并提取模态内细粒度特征，第二层实现跨模态细粒度解耦；引入两个随机特征重组织（RFR）模块，增强模态内与跨模态特征的精细融合。

Result: 在私有肝癌数据集及三个TCGA公开数据集上实验验证，HDMoE显著优于现有方法，证明其有效性。

Conclusion: 所提HDMoE框架有效解决了多模态生存预测中特征冗余与细粒度关系建模难题，具备良好的泛化能力与临床应用潜力。

Abstract: Multimodal survival prediction, a crucial yet challenging task, demands the integration of multimodal medical data (\eg Whole Slide Images (WSIs) and Genomic Profiles) to achieve accurate prognostic modeling. Given the inherent heterogeneity across modalities, the feature decoupling-fusion paradigm has emerged as a dominant approach. However, these methods have the following shortcomings: (1) fail to reduce the redundant information of modality features before decoupling, which negatively affects the feature decoupling and fusion effect;(2) lack the ability to model the fine-grained relationships of the features and capture the local information interactions between intra- and inter-modality features. To address these issues, we propose a \underline{H}ierarchical \underline{D}ecoupling-Fusion \underline{M}ixture-\underline{o}f-\underline{E}xperts (HDMoE) framework with two levels of MoE and \underline{R}andom \underline{F}eature \underline{R}eorganization (RFR) modules.In the first-level MoE, shared experts and routed experts are employed to remove redundant information and extract fine-grained specific features within each modality, while the second-level MoE facilitates fine-grained inter-modality feature decoupling. Besides, we design two RFR modules following each level of MoE to finely fuse intra- and inter-modality features, which can help the model capture more fine-grained relationships between modalities. Extensive experimental results on our private Liver Cancer (LC) and three TCGA public datasets confirm the effectiveness of our proposed method. Codes are available at https://github.com/ZJUMAI/HDMoE.

To tackle difficult samples, we introduce an expert arbitration mechanism: when ensemble confidence falls below 0.6, a multimodal large language model (MLLM) is triggered to perform rigorous visual verification by integrating external botanical descriptions using Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning. Furthermore, we optimized the training pipeline with a hard sample-aware joint loss. Abstract: We propose VISTA, a V-JEPA Integrated StillFast Temporal Anticipator for the Ego4D Short-Term Object Interaction Anticipation (STA) Challenge at EgoVis 2026. Given an egocentric video timestamp, the task requires anticipating the next human-object interaction, including the future active object's bounding box, noun category, verb category, time-to-contact, and confidence score. VISTA follows a StillFast-style design that combines object-centric spatial detection with short-horizon temporal context. Specifically, a COCO-pretrained Faster R-CNN ResNet-50 FPN detector generates object proposals from the last observed high-resolution frame, while a frozen V-JEPA 2.1 temporal branch extracts clip-level egocentric context from the observed video. The temporal representation is injected into the detection pathway through feature modulation and ROI-level context fusion. The fused proposal features are then passed to multi-head STA predictors for box refinement, noun classification, verb classification, time-to-contact regression, and interaction confidence estimation. For the final submission, we further ensemble complementary predictions to improve robustness. Experimental results on the official challenge server show that VISTA achieves first place in the EgoVis 2026 Ego4D STA Challenge. Our code will be released at https://github.com/CorrineQiu/VISTA.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有训练-free方法在长视频生成中面临架构耦合、质量下降或累积误差与重复模式等问题，亟需一种通用且高效的解决方案。

Method: 采用重叠滑动窗口策略，利用Tweedie匹配确保流形约束与时间一致性，并引入随机早期相采样以同步各窗口轨迹，在高噪声阶段注入新噪声后转为确定性ODE采样以保持细节清晰度。

Result: 生成视频长度可达原窗口长度数倍，优于现有训练-free与自回归基线，在时序一致性和视觉质量上表现更优，并可无缝扩展至音视频联合生成与文本到3DGS任务，无需微调。

Abstract: Extending the generation horizon of video diffusion models to long sequences remains a long-standing and important challenge. Existing training-free approaches fall into two categories: extensions of bidirectional models, which are tightly coupled to specific architectures and suffer from quality degradation over long horizons, and autoregressive models, which accumulate drift errors due to exposure bias and tend to produce repetitive motion patterns. To address these issues, we propose a novel but simple inference-time approach for long video generation that is architecture-agnostic and requires no additional training. Our method generates long videos via overlapping sliding windows, where predicted clean samples from adjacent windows are blended via \emph{Tweedie matching} to enforce both \textbf{manifold constraint and temporal consistency} across overlap regions. \emph{Stochastic early-phase sampling} then synchronizes per-window trajectories by injecting fresh noise after each Tweedie matching correction in the high-noise phase, before transitioning to deterministic ODE sampling to preserve fine-grained visual fidelity. Applied to various video generation models, our method generates videos several times longer than the native window length while outperforming both training-free and autoregressive baselines in temporal consistency and visual quality, and further extends to audio-video joint generation and text-to-3DGS without any fine-tuning.

Abstract: Structured road understanding of lane geometry, topology, and traffic element relationships is foundational to safe autonomous driving. Conversely, traditional modular systems, e.g., HD maps and topological road graphs, provide structural precision but remain semantically rigid. CRS enables the automatic generation of compositionally complex and linguistically varied question-answer pairs via recursive graph queries, augmented with a "grounding for free" mechanism that ensures logical traceability to specific map elements, and procedurally extracted chain-of-thought supervision traces. Analysis of model behavior via verifiable reasoning traces reveals a systematic shift in failure modes: whereas baseline models fail at relational scene understanding, CRS-trained models reduce failures to attribute recognition, suggesting that the primary bottleneck in road understanding is not model scale, but the absence of structured supervision.

Method: 设计焦点识别模块以建模视觉显著性与语义相关性的交互，挖掘全面的视觉主体谱；引入上下文感知结构扫描模块，聚合邻近区域的上下文线索，恢复全局关系依赖，保障保留主体的结构完整性。

In this paper, we propose SPpruner, a subject-centric progressive reduction paradigm that emulates the \textit{Focus-then-Context} mechanism of the human visual perception system. Specifically, we first construct a focus identification module to explicitly model the interplay between visual saliency and semantic relevance. Herein, it can excavate the comprehensive visual subject spectrum to ensure a high-fidelity representation of visual input. Subsequently, a context-aware structural scanning module is developed to aggregate contextual cues from neighboring regions. As such, it can effectively restore global relational dependencies to uphold the structural integrity of the preserved subjects. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our paradigm consistently outperforms SOTA methods, achieving up to 2.53 times speedup with only 22.2% of visual tokens retained in Qwen2.5-VL and a 67% FLOPs reduction on LLaVA with a negligible 0.6% accuracy drop.

### [74] [DrawMotion: Generating 3D Human Motions by Freehand Drawing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20955)
*Tao Wang,Lei Jin,Zhihua Wu,Qiaozhi He,Jiaming Chu,Yu Cheng,Junliang Xing,Jian Zhao,Shuicheng Yan,Li Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: DrawMotion is a diffusion-based framework for text-to-motion generation that introduces hand-drawing conditions to improve user control and efficiency. It enables motion generation using both text and freehand sketches, reduces user effort by 46.7%, and uses a Multi-Condition Module (MCM) for efficient multi-condition fusion and training-free guidance.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Users often struggle to precisely describe desired motions using text alone, leading to misaligned outputs. DrawMotion aims to address this by incorporating intuitive hand-drawing input for better spatial control and reducing reliance on detailed textual descriptions.

Method: The framework includes an algorithm for generating hand-drawn stickman sketches from various datasets, a Multi-Condition Module (MCM) integrated into the diffusion process for efficient fusion of text and drawing conditions, and training-free guidance via classifier-guidance gradients applied to continuous intermediate features.

Result: Quantitative experiments and user studies show that DrawMotion reduces user time by approximately 46.7% in generating motions aligned with their imagination, while maintaining high fidelity and enabling flexible condition combinations.

Conclusion: DrawMotion effectively enhances text-to-motion generation by combining text and hand-drawn inputs through an efficient, trainable, and guidance-compatible framework, significantly improving user experience and motion accuracy without requiring additional training.

Abstract: Text-to-motion generation, which translates textual descriptions into human motions, faces the challenge that users often struggle to precisely convey their intended motions through text alone. To address this issue, this paper introduces DrawMotion, an efficient diffusion-based framework designed for multi-condition scenarios. DrawMotion generates motions based on both a conventional text condition and a novel hand-drawing condition, which provide semantic and spatial control over the generated motions, respectively. Specifically, we tackle the fine-grained motion generation task from three perspectives: 1) freehand drawing condition. To accurately capture users' intended motions without requiring tedious textual input, we develop an algorithm to automatically generate hand-drawn stickman sketches across different dataset formats; 2) multi-condition fusion. We propose a Multi-Condition Module (MCM) that is integrated into the diffusion process, enabling the model to exploit all possible condition combinations while reducing computational complexity compared to conventional approaches; and 3) training-free guidance. Notably, the MCM in DrawMotion ensures that its intermediate features lie in a continuous space, allowing classifier-guidance gradients to update the features and thereby aligning the generated motions with user intentions while preserving fidelity. Quantitative experiments and user studies demonstrate that the freehand drawing approach reduces user time by approximately 46.7% when generating motions aligned with their imagination. The code, demos, and relevant data are publicly available at https://github.com/InvertedForest/DrawMotion.

### [75] [Finding the Correct Visual Evidence Without Forgetting: Mitigating Hallucination in LVLMs via Inter-Layer Visual Attention Discrepancy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20965)
*Yutong Xie,Zhenglin Hua,Ran Wang,Wing W. Y. Ng,Xizhao Wang,Yuheng Jia*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于层间视觉注意力差异（ILVAD）的训练免费、即插即用的幻觉缓解方法，通过识别并增强模型在生成过程中反复激活的视觉证据，减少视觉遗忘，并强化与视觉内容强相关的文本生成。实验表明该方法在五种不同架构的大型视觉语言模型上均能有效减轻幻觉问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型视觉语言模型（LVLMs）在生成过程中常因对视觉证据关注不足或逐渐遗忘而产生幻觉，尽管整体注意力偏低，但在特定层中对正确视觉证据表现出敏感性，存在显著的层间差异。

Method: 通过分析早期生成标记到视觉标记在各层中的注意力权重，识别出反复激活的视觉证据形成显著性图谱；利用该图谱增强生成过程中的视觉注意力，抑制视觉遗忘，并根据图谱选择和强调与视觉证据强关联的文本标记。

Result: 所提方法在多个基准测试中对五种不同架构的大型视觉语言模型均展现出一致的幻觉缓解效果，且无需训练、可直接集成。

Conclusion: 基于层间视觉注意力差异的增强机制能够有效缓解大型视觉语言模型中的幻觉问题，为提升模型生成内容的真实性提供了通用且高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs) have shown remarkable performance on a wide range of vision-language tasks. Despite this progress, they are still prone to hallucination, generating responses that are inconsistent with visual content. In this work, we find that LVLMs tend to hallucinate when they pay insufficient attention to the correct visual evidence and gradually forget it during the generation process. We empirically find that although LVLMs overall attend insufficiently to visual evidence, they exhibit sensitivity to the correct visual evidence in specific layers, with notable inter-layer discrepancy. Motivated by this observation, we propose a novel hallucination mitigation method that enhances visual evidence based on Inter-Layer Visual Attention Discrepancy (ILVAD). Specifically, we obtain the attention weights from early generated tokens to visual tokens across layers and identify the tokens that are repeatedly activated as visual evidence, forming a saliency map. We then enhance attention to visual evidence during generation through the saliency map to reduce visual forgetting. In addition, we leverage the saliency map to obtain attention scores of generated text to visual evidence, in order to select and emphasize text tokens that are strongly grounded in visual evidence. Our method is training-free and plug-and-play. Multiple benchmark evaluations conducted on five recently released models show that our method can consistently mitigate hallucinations in different LVLMs over various architectures. Code is available at https://github.com/ytx-ML/ILVAD.

</details>


### [76] [Comparative Evaluation of Deep Learning Models for Fake Image Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20971)
*Akhitha Pakala,Mohammed Mahir Rahman,Shahzad Memon,Tauseef Ahmed*

Method: 采用统一的预处理流程（图像重缩放、归一化、数据增强）处理真实与伪造图像数据集；基于四个主流预训练CNN架构（VGG16、ResNet50、EfficientNetB0、XceptionNet）构建分类模型；在相同训练设置下进行端到端训练与评估，使用准确率、精确率、召回率、F1分数和ROC-AUC作为评价指标。

Result: VGG16达到最高准确率91%，其他三个模型均达90%。EfficientNetB0在检测伪造图像方面表现出更高敏感性，但在真实图像分类上可靠性下降，显示出因类别不平衡带来的偏差。所有模型均存在一定程度的过拟合和泛化能力限制。

Conclusion: 本研究为假图像检测提供了可复现的基准。结果表明，尽管各模型表现接近，但数据不平衡仍显著影响模型性能。未来工作应聚焦于构建更均衡的数据集、采用先进的数据增强策略以及引入公平性意识的训练机制，以提升系统的跨域鲁棒性与实际应用价值。

Abstract: The growing sophistication of GAN-based image manipulation presents significant challenges for digital forensics. This study compares the performance of four pretrained CNN architectures including VGG16, ResNet50, EfficientNetB0, and XceptionNet for fake image detection using a unified preprocessing and training pipeline. A dataset of real and manipulated images was processed through resizing, normalization, and augmentation to address class imbalance and improve generalization. Models were evaluated using Accuracy, Precision, Recall, F1-score, and ROC-AUC. VGG16 achieved the highest accuracy at 91%, with XceptionNet, ResNet50, and EfficientNetB0 each reaching 90%. EfficientNetB0 showed stronger sensitivity to fake images but reduced reliability on real samples, reflecting imbalance-driven bias. Limitations include dataset imbalance, overfitting, and limited interpretability, which affect cross-domain robustness. The study provides a reproducible baseline and underscores the need for balanced datasets, advanced augmentation, and fairness-aware training to develop reliable fake image detection systems.

### [78] [CHOIR: Contact-aware 4D Hand-Object Interaction Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20992)
*Hao Xu,Yilin Liu,Yinqiao Wang,Chi-Wing Fu,Niloy J. Mitra*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: CHOIR 是一种用于单目相机的接触感知手-物体交互（HOI）重建框架，利用接触作为手与物体之间的显式耦合信号，从开放世界视频中恢复4D交互原型，包括手部运动、物体形状与6D姿态随时间的变化以及接触的时空位置。该方法通过视觉先验初始化粗略的4D HOI序列，再通过生成式空间校正模块修正手物相对位置，并推导初始接触对应关系，最后通过接触感知联合优化确保几何、时间和接触一致性，显著提升物体重建质量、物理合理性及时间一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在复杂单目视频中重建手-物体交互时面临挑战，通常依赖已知物体或精心设计场景，且独立估计的手和物体容易在杂乱、遮挡和未知物体几何下发生错位。因此需要一种能从真实开放世界视频中可靠重建4D交互的方法，以支持可扩展的真实交互数据挖掘及场景感知的合成与规划。

Method: CHOIR 首先基于开放世界视觉先验初始化一个粗略的、不考虑接触的4D HOI序列；然后引入生成式手-物体空间校正模块，预测射线深度修正并校正手物相对位置，进而得到校正后的几何上的初始接触对应；最后采用接触感知联合优化，动态更新接触约束，强制实现几何、时间与接触的一致性。

Result: 在受控和具有挑战性的视频上实验表明，CHOIR 在物体重建精度、物理合理性以及时间一致性方面均优于现有最先进方法。

Conclusion: CHOIR 证明了利用接触作为显式耦合信号，能够有效提升单目视频中手-物体交互的4D重建质量，为大规模真实交互数据的挖掘与智能系统中的场景感知应用提供了可行路径。

Abstract: We ask whether everyday open-world monocular videos can be turned into reusable 4D interaction primitives: articulated hand motion, object shape with 6D pose over time, and the when/where of contact. Such a capability would enable scalable mining of real interactions and, beyond reconstruction, support scene-aware synthesis and planning. However, reconstructing hand-object interaction (HOI) from challenging monocular videos remains difficult: methods often assume known objects or curated scenes, and separately estimated hands and objects easily become misaligned under clutter, occlusion, and unseen object geometries. Targeting this setting, we present CHOIR, a Contact-aware HOI Reconstruction framework for a monocular camera, using contact as an explicit coupling signal between hands and objects. CHOIR first initializes a coarse, contact-agnostic 4D HOI sequence from open-world visual priors. It then introduces a generative HOI spatial rectification module to predict ray-depth corrections and rectify hand-object relative placement, then derive initial per-frame contact correspondences on the rectified geometry. Last, a contact-aware joint optimization with dynamically updated contact constraints enforces geometric, temporal, and contact consistency. Experiments on controlled and challenging videos show that CHOIR improves object reconstruction, physical plausibility, and temporal consistency over state-of-the-art methods.

While the features used for training and inversion where selected to ensure the physical consistency of the solutions, they could not resolve all height / structure and baseline / terrain slope ambiguities in the data. ### [80] [DySink: Dynamic Frame Sinks for Autoregressive Long Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21028)
*Bo Ye,Xinyu Cui,Jian Zhao,Tong Wei,Min-Ling Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: DySink提出一种基于检索的动态帧缓存框架，解决传统自回归长视频生成中固定早期帧缓存导致的长期上下文失配和注意力坍缩问题。通过动态选择视觉相关的历史帧作为帧缓存，并引入异常门机制抑制过度一致的上下文，提升生成视频的动态性和时序质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方法使用固定的早期帧作为长期锚点，但当当前视觉状态与早期帧差异较大时，这些过时的锚点会误导生成，导致注意力均质化和内容退化（如sink collapse）。需要更灵活、自适应的长期记忆机制。

Method: DySink构建一个紧凑的记忆库，采用基于检索的方式动态选择与当前状态最相关的过去帧作为动态帧缓存；同时引入一个基于注意力一致性的异常门，检测并抑制可能导致注意力坍缩的过度一致上下文。

Result: 在长达一分钟的视频生成任务上，DySink显著优于现有强基线模型，在动态性与时序质量方面均有提升，有效缓解了注意力坍缩问题。

Conclusion: DySink通过动态帧缓存与异常门机制，实现了更自适应、鲁棒的长期上下文建模，为高效且高质量的长视频生成提供了新思路。

Abstract: Autoregressive long video generation often adopts bounded-memory streaming for efficiency, typically combining local windows for short-term continuity with static early-frame sinks as long-range anchors. However, this fixed allocation keeps early frames cached even when the current visual state has substantially diverged from them, while discarding potentially more relevant intermediate history. As a result, the retained long-range context may become less adaptive and bias generation toward outdated cues; in severe cases, RoPE-induced phase re-alignment can homogenize inter-head attention and cause sink collapse, where content regresses toward sink frames. We propose DySink, a retrieval-based framework that maintains a compact memory bank and selects visually relevant historical frames as dynamic frame sinks. DySink couples adaptive retrieval with a sink anomaly gate, which detects excessive inter-head consensus over retrieved context and suppresses collapse-prone context. Experiments on minute-long videos show that DySink consistently improves dynamic degree over strong baselines while also achieving higher temporal quality. The code and model weights will be released at https://github.com/yebo0216best/DySink.

### [81] [Towards Physically Consistent 4D Scene Reconstruction for Closed-loop Autonomous Driving Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21032)
*Bowyn Tan,Yutong Xie,Bai Huang,Fan Luo,Xiao Li,Naizheng Wang,Yang Guan,Shengbo Eben Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为OPG的分层训练方法，旨在解决现有3DGS及其4D扩展在同时实现高保真街景重建、新视角合成（NVS）和时变信息建模方面的局限性。通过构建信息几何诊断框架，揭示问题根源在于时空参数间的信用分配困境，即单源观测中视点与时间的确定性耦合导致低秩结构，引发静态视点依赖与动态时变成分之间的大量空域模糊。为解决此问题，提出正交投影梯度（OPG）方法，先保障空间表征完整性，再将时间更新限制在空间零空间内，实现主动信用分配；并引入基于物理先验的时序正则化策略，约束外观演化的一致性，确保闭环仿真中的物理一致性。实验表明，该方法在保持稳定NVS能力的同时，在传统观测重现指标上表现更优，间接反映其对时变动态建模的优越能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有3DGS及4D扩展方法无法同时实现高保真街景重建中的新视角合成（NVS）与时变信息建模，关键瓶颈在于时空参数间存在信用分配困境，导致空间表征失真与时间建模不准确。

Method: 提出信息-几何诊断框架，揭示低秩结构与空域模糊问题；设计正交投影梯度（OPG）分层训练机制，优先保护空间表征，再将时间更新约束于空间零空间；引入基于物理先验的时序正则化策略，增强外观演化一致性。

Result: 所提方法在保持稳定的新视角合成性能基础上，显著提升观测重现精度，间接证明其在建模时变动态方面具备更强能力，适用于闭环自动驾驶仿真场景。

Conclusion: 通过分离时空参数更新路径并结合物理先验正则化，本工作有效缓解了时空混淆问题，为高保真、可闭环的自主驾驶仿真提供了可靠的技术支撑。

Abstract: High-fidelity street scene reconstruction is pivotal for end-to-end autonomous driving simulation, where novel-view synthesis (NVS) and time-varying information modeling are two fundamental capabilities to facilitate closed-loop training. However, existing 3DGS methods and their 4D extensions fail to simultaneously achieve both. To bridge this gap, we establish an information-geometric diagnostic framework, revealing that this limitation stems from a credit assignment dilemma between spatial and temporal parameters. Specifically, the deterministic coupling between viewpoint and time in single-source observation creates a low-rank structure that induces massive null-space ambiguity between static view-dependent and dynamic time-varying components. Temporal information overshadows spatial cues, causing the estimation variance of spatial parameters to diverge. To address this issue, we propose Orthogonal Projected Gradient (OPG), a hierarchical training method designed to restore spatial identifiability. OPG prioritizes the integrity of spatial representations by securing them in an initial stage, then restricts temporal updates to the spatial null space, enabling proactive credit assignment. While OPG isolates temporal updates algebraically, Temporal Regularization Strategy is proposed to further refine the temporal solution space by imposing a smoothness constraint based on the physical prior of consistent appearance evolution, ensuring that the reconstructed scene remains physically consistent in closed-loop simulation. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our method not only maintains stable NVS capabilities but also demonstrates superior performance in traditional observation-reproducing metrics, which indirectly reflect the capability of modeling temporal dynamics.

### [82] [Dynamic Video Generation: Shaping Video Generation Across Time and Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21042)
*Shikang Zheng,Jingkai Huang,Jiacheng Liu,Guantao Chen,Lixuan,Yuqi Lin,Peiliang Cai,Linfeng Zhang*

TL;DR: DVG提出一种动态视频生成框架，通过联合分配时空计算资源，自动选择内容感知的加速策略，实现近无损加速，在HunyuanVideo和HunyuanVideo-1.5上最高达7倍速度提升，结合蒸馏可达18倍，适用于大规模高效视频生成系统。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频生成中的扩散模型因迭代去噪过程计算成本高，尽管渐进分辨率采样有一定加速效果，但在视频生成中因时空需求多样，单一维度压缩导致加速有限或质量下降，亟需更智能的计算分配机制。

Method: DVG框架通过动态地在时间和空间维度上联合分配计算资源，根据内容自适应选择加速策略，无需人工调参或重新训练，实现高效且高质量的视频生成。

Result: DVG在HunyuanVideo和HunyuanVideo-1.5上实现最高7倍加速，结合蒸馏后达到18倍加速，保持近无损质量，展现出在大规模高效视频生成系统中的巨大潜力。

Conclusion: DVG是一种高效的动态视频生成框架，能自动适配不同视频内容的时空需求，实现显著加速与高质量输出，是当前大规模高效视频生成系统的关键组件。

Abstract: Diffusion models have achieved impressive performance in video generation, but their iterative denoising process remains computationally expensive due to the large number of tokens processed at each timestep. Recently, progressive resolution sampling has emerged as a promising acceleration approach by reducing latent resolution in early stages. However, scaling this idea to video generation remains challenging, as the additional temporal dimension introduces diverse spatio-temporal demands across different videos, and compressing only a single dimension often leads to limited acceleration or degraded quality. Therefore, we propose DVG, a Dynamic Video Generation framework that jointly allocates computation across time and space, automatically selecting content-aware acceleration strategies without manual tuning or retraining. DVG achieves near-lossless acceleration across models and tasks, reaching up to 7 times speedup on HunyuanVideo and HunyuanVideo-1.5, and 18 times when combined with distillation, demonstrating its potential as a key component in today's large-scale efficient video generation systems. Our code is in supplementary material and will be released on Github.

</details>


### [83] [Multimodal LLMs under Pairwise Modalities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21059)
*Yan Li,Yunlong Deng,Yuewen Sun,Gongxu Luo,Kun Zhang,Guangyi Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种仅利用成对模态数据训练多模态大模型（MLLMs）的方法，避免了传统需要联合标注的多模态数据集。通过理论分析证明在特定条件下，仅从成对模态中可识别出可区分的表示，并设计了一个两阶段框架：第一阶段通过自模态重建与成对对比学习实现跨模态潜在空间对齐，引入归纳偏置以增强对齐效果；第二阶段通过整合新模态编码器与预训练模态解码器，实现跨模态迁移与生成。实验表明，在引入3D点云和触觉模态后，模型在三组模态对上均表现出优异的跨模态性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MLLMs训练依赖于复杂且耗时的多模态联合标注数据集，限制了其在新领域的可扩展性。为解决这一问题，本文探索仅使用成对模态数据来训练MLLMs，从而提升训练效率与泛化能力。

Method: 提出一个两阶段表示学习框架：(1) 潜在表示对齐阶段，结合自模态重建与成对对比学习，并引入部分对齐与最小化潜在表示的归纳偏置；(2) 跨模态重构阶段，将新模态编码器与预训练模态解码器融合，实现跨模态转移与生成。

Result: 在引入3D点云和触觉模态的三组成对数据下，所提方法成功构建了统一的对齐潜在空间，显著提升了跨模态任务的性能，验证了方法的有效性与可扩展性。

Conclusion: 仅依赖成对模态数据即可有效训练多模态大模型，该方法在保持高性能的同时大幅降低数据构建成本，具有良好的应用前景。

Abstract: Despite the impressive results achieved by multimodal large language models (MLLMs), their training typically relies on jointly curated multimodal data, requiring substantial human effort to construct multi-way aligned datasets and thereby limiting scalability across domains. In this work, we explore training MLLMs by only leveraging multiple paired modalities as a surrogate for the full joint multimodal distribution. Specifically, we first provide a theoretical analysis of the conditions under which the representations are identifiable with only observing pairwise modalities. Building on this analysis, we propose a representation learning framework for aligning latent representations across modalities using only pairwise data. The framework consists of two stages: latent representation alignment and cross-modal recomposition. Specifically, in the first stage, we learn the shared latent space across modalities by both self-modal reconstruction and pair-wise contrastive learning. We also incorporate an inductive bias in the contrastive learning process by partially aligning and minimal latent specification. In stage two, we integrate the encoder of newly introduced modalities with the decoders of the pre-trained modalities to facilitate cross-modal transfer and generation. We evaluate our method by newly adding 3D point clouds and tactile modalities into pre-trained MLLMs with three modality pairs and show that, by learning an aligned latent representation space, our model achieves strong cross-modal performance.

### [84] [Q-ARVD: Quantizing Autoregressive Video Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21072)
*Siao Tang,Xinyin Ma,Gongfan Fang,Xingyi Yang,Xinchao Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出Q-ARVD，一种针对自回归视频扩散模型（ARVD）的新型量化框架，解决其在量化过程中面临的两大挑战：帧间敏感度极不平衡和权重中存在显著且异质的异常值模式。通过引入最终质量感知的帧加权机制和异常值感知的自适应双尺度量化方法，显著提升了量化后的模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自回归视频扩散模型（ARVD）虽具实时交互生成视频的潜力，但其高昂的推理成本限制了实际应用。现有量化方案直接应用于ARVD时表现不佳，因此亟需针对ARVD特性设计专门的量化方法。

Method: 提出Q-ARVD框架，包含两项核心技术：(S1) 引入最终质量感知的帧加权机制，缓解因自回归生成导致的误差累积引发的帧间敏感度不均衡问题；(S2) 设计异常值感知的自适应双尺度量化，自动检测并隔离不同层类型与深度中的异常值通道，保护正常通道性能。

Result: 大量实验表明，Q-ARVD在保持高精度的同时显著降低推理开销，相较于现有方法在多个指标上实现显著提升，验证了其有效性与优越性。

Conclusion: Q-ARVD成功解决了自回归视频扩散模型量化中的关键挑战，为高效部署高质量视频生成模型提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Autoregressive video diffusion models (ARVDs) have emerged as a promising architecture for streaming video generation, paving the way for real-time interactive video generation and world modeling. Despite their potential, the substantial inference cost of ARVDs remains a major obstacle to practical deployment, making model quantization a natural direction for improving efficiency. However, quantization for ARVDs remains largely unexplored. Our empirical analysis shows that directly applying existing quantization schemes developed for standard diffusion transformers to ARVDs leads to suboptimal performance, revealing quantization behaviors that differ from those observed in bidirectional diffusion models. In this paper, we identify two critical challenges in quantizing ARVDs: (C1) Highly unbalanced frame-wise quantization sensitivity. Error accumulation during autoregressive generation can induce severely skewed quantization sensitivity across frames, following an exponential-like decay pattern. (C2) Prominent and heterogeneous outlier patterns in weights. Weight distributions exhibit pronounced outlier channels, whose patterns vary substantially across layer types and block depths. To address these issues, we propose Q-ARVD, a novel framework for accurate ARVD quantization. (S1) To tackle the highly unbalanced frame-wise sensitivity, Q-ARVD incorporates a final-quality aware frame-weighting mechanism into the quantization objective. (S2) To prevent heterogeneous outliers from degrading performance, Q-ARVD introduces an outlier-aware adaptive dual-scale quantization, which automatically detects the presence and quantity of outlier channels for an arbitrary layer, and isolates them to protect normal channels. Extensive experiments demonstrate the superiority of Q-ARVD.

### [85] [SpectralEarth-FM: Bringing Hyperspectral Imagery into Multimodal Earth Observation Pretraining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21075)
*Nassim Ait Ali Braham,Aaron Banze,Conrad M. Albrecht,Julien Mairal,Jocelyn Chanussot,Xiao Xiang Zhu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: SpectralEarth-FM 是一种用于多传感器地球观测（EO）输入的分层Transformer模型，能够联合处理高光谱影像（HSI）与低通道观测数据。通过引入针对高光谱数据的光谱标记化、传感器特定编码器、跨传感器融合模块和共享分层编码器，实现了异构光谱维度下的统一建模。为预训练该模型，构建了SpectralEarth-MM数据集，包含来自三颗星载传感器（EnMAP、EMIT、DESI）的高光谱数据及与之共位的Sentinel-2、Landsat-8/9光学影像、地表温度（LST）和Sentinel-1 SAR数据，覆盖约200万个全球位置，总计2500万地理参考图像块，数据量超40TB。采用类似JEPA的联合嵌入预测目标进行预训练，以对齐全局视图与单传感器局部视图的表示。在高光谱下游任务和标准地球观测基准测试中均取得当前最优性能，验证了其在多源遥感数据融合中的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有地球观测基础模型主要依赖多光谱影像（MSI）、合成孔径雷达（SAR）和派生地理空间图层，而高光谱影像（HSI）仍被严重低估；同时，已有高光谱基础模型仅基于HSI独立训练，缺乏与共位的其他地球观测传感器联合预训练与融合的研究。因此，亟需一种能有效整合高光谱与多种低通道传感器数据的统一框架，以提升模型对复杂地物特征的理解能力。

Method: 提出SpectralEarth-FM，一个面向多传感器地球观测输入的分层Transformer架构，包含：(1) 针对高光谱影像的光谱标记化方法；(2) 传感器特定编码器以提取各传感器特性；(3) 跨传感器融合模块实现异质数据对齐；(4) 共享分层编码器进行高层语义建模。预训练采用类JEPA的联合嵌入预测目标，使全局视图与同一地理位置的单传感器局部视图表示保持一致。此外，构建SpectralEarth-MM数据集，涵盖三类高光谱传感器与多源光学、热红外及雷达数据，支持大规模联合训练。

Result: 在多个高光谱下游任务和标准地球观测基准测试中，SpectralEarth-FM表现优异，达到当前最优水平，尤其在多源数据融合场景下展现出显著优势。实验表明，联合预训练能有效增强模型对地物光谱特性的感知能力，并提升跨传感器泛化性能。

Conclusion: SpectralEarth-FM成功实现了高光谱影像与多种地球观测传感器的联合建模与预训练，填补了多源遥感数据融合中的关键空白。所提出的架构与数据集为未来地球观测基础模型的发展提供了重要范式，推动遥感智能分析迈向更全面、更精细的方向。

Abstract: Earth observation (EO) foundation models (FMs) are increasingly trained on multisensor data, spanning multispectral imagery (MSI), synthetic aperture radar (SAR), and derived geospatial layers, but hyperspectral imagery (HSI) remains underrepresented. Conversely, existing hyperspectral FMs are trained on HSI alone, leaving joint pretraining and fusion of HSI with co-located EO sensors unexplored. We introduce SpectralEarth-FM, a hierarchical transformer for multisensor EO input with heterogeneous spectral dimensionality. The architecture combines spectral tokenization for hyperspectral inputs, sensor-specific encoders, a cross-sensor fusion module, and a shared hierarchical encoder, enabling joint processing of HSI and lower-channel observations. To pretrain SpectralEarth-FM, we curate SpectralEarth-MM, a dataset that co-locates HSI from three spaceborne sensors (EnMAP, EMIT, DESIS) with Sentinel-2, Landsat-8/9 optical imagery, Landsat land surface temperature (LST), and Sentinel-1 SAR, over common geographic footprints. It comprises approximately 2M globally distributed locations, 25M georeferenced patches, and over 40TB of data. Pretraining uses a Joint-Embedding Predictive Architecture (JEPA)-style objective that matches representations between global views and single-sensor local views from the same location. We evaluate SpectralEarth-FM on hyperspectral downstream tasks and standard EO benchmarks following the PANGAEA protocol, achieving state-of-the-art results across both evaluation settings.

### [86] [VDFP: Video Deflickering with Flicker-banding Priors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21079)
*Zhiyi Zhou,Libo Zhu,Zihan Zhou,Yulun Zhang,Xiaokang Yang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文针对智能手机拍摄数字屏幕时因硬件不同步导致的严重条纹问题，构建了首个真实场景下的DeViD数据集，并提出VDFP（基于闪烁条纹先验的视频去闪烁方法）。该方法通过滚动快门机制建模退化场（DFM）来合成复杂多条纹场景，并引入空间-时间连续先验感知（CPP）模块，利用闪烁感知均方误差（FA-MSE）优化，以更精确捕捉亮度变化。模型通过零初始化增强输入层，保留预训练生成先验与时空感知能力。实验表明，VDFP在去除复杂条纹的同时保持高保真空间细节和时间一致性，显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频修复方法难以有效处理由硬件同步不匹配引起的结构化、周期性亮度波动（条纹），常导致残留伪影或纹理过度平滑。缺乏真实世界多场景下高质量标注数据集也限制了相关研究发展。
