### [124] [Parallel LLM Reasoning for Bias-Resilient, Robust Conceptual Abstraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20194)
*Aisvarya Adeseye,Jouni Isoaho,Adeyemi Adeseye*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种结合并行分块处理与证据锚定整合的结构化框架，以解决大语言模型在分析长文档时因上下文推理局限导致的累积偏差、遗漏错误和过度泛化问题。通过将文本分割为语义连贯的块并行处理，消除早期内容的影响；再通过显式证据锚定与优先级排序进行整合，提升可追溯性与准确性。实验表明，该方法可显著降低约84%的遗漏错误，提升最高达130%的证据可追溯性，并减少高达91%的未经支持的陈述，尤其对小型模型效果更佳，证明了高效并行分块与整合在实现可靠、可扩展文本分析中的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在处理长文档时存在上下文推理局限，早期或主导概念会压制次要但重要的解释，导致累积偏差、遗漏错误和过度泛化；同时独立生成的结果缺乏系统性整合，易引入冗余、概念漂移和不实主张，亟需一种能提升分析可靠性与可追溯性的新方法。

Method: 将文本划分为语义连贯的块，进行并行独立处理以消除序列依赖；随后采用显式证据锚定与优先级排序机制对各块结果进行系统性整合，确保输出基于可靠证据，减少主导概念影响与过度泛化。

Result: 实验结果显示，该方法使遗漏错误降低约84%，证据可追溯性提升最高达130%，未经支持的陈述减少高达91%；小型模型受益尤为明显，表明并行分块与证据锚定整合是实现高效、可靠文本分析的关键。

Conclusion: 提出的并行分块与证据锚定整合框架有效缓解了大语言模型在长文档分析中的上下文偏见与信息丢失问题，显著提升分析质量与可解释性，尤其适用于资源受限场景下的高可靠性文本分析任务。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have been increasingly used to analyze text. However, they are often plagued with contextual reasoning limitations when analyzing long documents. When long documents are processed sequentially, early or dominant concepts can overshadow less visible but meaningful interpretations, leading to cumulative analytical bias, omission error, and over-generalization. Additionally, independently generated outputs are often merged without systematic grounding, introducing redundancy, conceptual drift, and unsupported claims. This study proposes a structured framework combining parallel chunk-level processing with evidence-anchored consolidation. Texts are first divided into semantically coherent chunks and processed independently in parallel to remove influence from earlier processing. The independently generated interpretations are then consolidated using explicit evidence anchoring and prioritization that reduces dominance and over-generalization while improving traceability. Experiments with multiple model types and sizes indicate that parallel processing significantly reduces omission error by approximately 84%, increases evidence traceability by up to 130%, and reduces unsupported claims by up to 91%. Smaller models benefited most, suggesting that efficient parallel chunking and consolidation play a critical role in achieving reliable and scalable textual analysis.

</details>


### [125] [Data Scaling as Progressive Coverage of a Predictive Contribution Spectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20196)
*Zihui Song,Shihao Ji,Hongxi Li,Shuaizhi Cheng,Chunlin Huang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究真实数据缩放定律是否由潜在预测贡献谱的渐进覆盖所主导，而非仅由词频尾部决定。通过后缀自动机表示文本语料库，定义了基于全局KL散度的预测贡献谱，发现其尾部斜率与小型GPT学习器的数据缩放指数高度相关。进一步提出有效截断秩K(N)，通过匹配观测到的过量损失与谱尾部质量来定义，发现log K与log N近似线性关系，拟合优度R²达0.96（原始谱）和0.90（平滑谱），支持训练规模推动预测状态谱前沿前进，且尾部质量追踪剩余过量损失的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究真实数据缩放定律的本质机制，挑战传统仅依赖词频尾部解释的观点，提出基于预测贡献谱的更普适解释框架。

Method: 采用后缀自动机表示语料库，构建数据内在的全局KL预测贡献谱，分析其尾部特性；通过匹配过量损失与尾部质量，定义有效截断秩K(N)并检验其与训练规模N的关系。

Result: 12个真实语料库中，预测贡献谱尾部斜率与数据缩放指数强相关；K(N)与N的对数呈高度线性关系，原始谱R²≈0.96，平滑谱R²≈0.90，表明预测状态谱的渐进覆盖是缩放规律的核心机制。

Conclusion: 真实数据缩放规律可由预测贡献谱的渐进覆盖机制有效解释，训练规模推进有效预测前沿，尾部质量精确反映剩余学习误差，为理解大模型训练提供了新视角。

Abstract: We investigate the hypothesis that real-data scaling laws are governed by progressive coverage of a latent predictive contribution spectrum rather than by token-frequency tails alone. We work with a suffix-automaton representation of text corpora and define a data-intrinsic global-KL predictive contribution spectrum, in which each state contributes according to its empirical mass times its KL deviation from a global next-token baseline. Across 12 real corpora, the tail slope of this spectrum is already strongly correlated with the empirical data-scaling exponent of a fixed small GPT learner. We then go beyond slope correlation and define, for each training size N, an effective truncation rank K(N) by matching the observed excess loss to the residual tail mass of the prepared 1000k global-KL spectrum. Empirically, log K is close to linear in log N, with pooled R^2 about 0.96 for the raw spectrum and R^2 about 0.90 for the smoothed spectrum. These findings provide strong empirical support for a simple mechanism picture: training scale advances an effective frontier through a predictive state spectrum, and the residual tail mass of that spectrum tracks the remaining excess loss.

</details>


### [126] [MedicalBench: Evaluating Large Language Models Toward Improved Medical Concept Extraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20197)
*Zhichao Yang,Gregory D. Lyng,Sanjit Singh Batra,Robert E. Tillman*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: MedicalBench 是首个专注于隐式、基于证据的医疗概念提取的基准测试，通过将概念提取任务转化为医学笔记-概念对的验证任务，并结合句子级证据识别，评估模型在隐式医疗推理方面的能力。数据集基于 MIMIC-IV 出院记录和经人工验证的 ICD-10 编码构建，采用多阶段大语言模型筛选与医学标注及专家审查相结合的方式进行构建，包含隐式正例、语义混淆负例以及大模型与专家判断不一致的情况。该基准定义了两个互补任务：（1）医疗概念提取；（2）句子级证据检索，用于评估模型的正确性与可解释性。实验表明，当前先进大模型表现有限，且性能不受病历长度影响，说明该基准有效分离出推理难度而非表面干扰因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有医疗概念提取基准大多关注显式陈述的概念，忽视了医学文本中大量隐含但重要的概念表达，导致模型难以捕捉隐式医疗推理，因此亟需一个专门针对隐式概念提取并具备证据支撑的系统性评估基准。

Method: 构建 MedicalBench 基准：基于 MIMIC-IV 数据集，利用多阶段大语言模型进行初步筛选，再经由医学专家标注与审核，生成包含隐式正例、语义混淆负例及专家与模型意见分歧样本的数据集；将概念提取建模为医学笔记-概念对的验证任务，并结合句子级证据识别；设计两个互补评估任务以衡量模型的准确性和可解释性。

Result: 对主流大语言模型的基准测试显示，其在隐式概念提取任务上的表现仍然较低，且性能不受病历长度影响，说明任务挑战主要源于深层推理而非表层特征或文本长度。该结果凸显了当前模型在理解隐含医学信息方面的不足。

Conclusion: MedicalBench 提供了首个系统性的隐式、证据基础的医疗概念提取评估框架，为开发能够准确识别医学相关概念并提供透明、符合医学逻辑解释的医疗语言模型奠定了基础。

Abstract: Medical concept extraction from electronic health records underpins many downstream applications, yet remains challenging because medically meaningful concepts are frequently implied rather than explicitly stated in medical narratives. Existing benchmarks with human-annotated evidence spans underscore the importance of grounding extracted concepts in medical text. However, they predominantly focus on explicitly stated concepts instead of implicit concepts. We present MedicalBench, a benchmark for medical concept extraction with evidence grounding that evaluates implicit medical reasoning. MedicalBench formulates medical concept extraction as a verification task over medical note-concept pairs, coupled with sentence-level evidence identification. Built from MIMIC-IV discharge summaries and human-verified ICD-10 codes, the dataset is curated through a multi-stage large language model (LLM) triage pipeline followed by medical annotation and expert review. It deliberately includes implicit positives, semantically confusable negatives, and cases where LLM judgments disagree with medical expert assessments. We define two complementary evaluation tasks: (1) medical concept extraction and (2) sentence-level evidence retrieval, enabling assessment of both correctness and interpretability. Benchmarking state-of-the-art LLMs reveals that performance remains modest, highlighting the difficulty of extracting implicitly expressed concepts. We further show that performance is largely invariant to note length, indicating that MedicalBench isolates reasoning difficulty rather than superficial confounders. MedicalBench provides the first systematic benchmark for implicit, evidence-grounded medical concept extraction, offering a foundation for developing medical language models that can both identify medically relevant concepts and justify their predictions in a transparent and medically faithful manner.

</details>


### [127] [FlowLM: Few-Step Language Modeling via Diffusion-to-Flow Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20199)
*Runzhe Zhang,Letian Chen,Wenpeng Zhang,Zhouhan Lin,Peilin Zhao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: FlowLM 是一种通过高效微调将预训练扩散语言模型转换为流匹配语言模型的方法。通过将扩散模型的曲线采样轨迹重新对齐为直线流，FlowLM 实现了高质量的少步生成，其效果可媲美甚至超越 2000 步扩散采样的质量，且仅需极少训练轮次。微调后的 FlowLM 仅用一半训练轮次即可达到性能饱和，显著优于从头训练和原始扩散模型。此外，研究验证了更有效的流匹配训练目标：预测干净数据以持续引导采样过程趋向真实数据分布。实证结果表明该方法在高质量、少步文本生成中极为有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有扩散语言模型虽然生成质量高，但需要大量采样步骤（如2000步），计算成本高且效率低；同时，训练过程耗时长。因此，亟需一种能实现高质量、少步生成并提升训练效率的新方法。

Method: 将预训练扩散语言模型通过高效微调转化为流匹配语言模型，通过重新对齐采样轨迹为直线流，优化采样路径，并引入预测干净数据作为训练目标，以更有效地引导采样过程收敛到真实数据分布。

Result: FlowLM 在极少数训练轮次下即达到性能饱和，生成质量显著优于原始扩散模型和从头训练方法，且仅需少量采样步数即可实现媲美甚至超越传统2000步扩散采样的效果。预测干净数据的训练目标被证明是更有效的。

Conclusion: FlowLM 通过流匹配机制实现了高效、高质量的少步文本生成，验证了重新对齐采样轨迹与优化训练目标的有效性，为扩散语言模型的实际应用提供了高效可行的解决方案。

Abstract: We present FlowLM, a flow matching language model transformed from pre-trained diffusion language models via efficient fine-tuning. By re-aligning the curved sampling trajectories of diffusion models into straight-line flows, FlowLM enables high quality few-step generation that rivals or even outperforms the quality of 2,000-step diffusion sampling with very few training epochs. Remarkably, finetuned FlowLM reaches performance saturation with only half as many training epochs as training from scratch, both approaches greatly outperforming the original diffusion model, thereby validating our method. Furthermore, we validate a more effective training objective for flow matching: predicting clean data to consistently guide the sampling process towards the true data distribution. Empirical results demonstrate that our approach is highly effective for high-quality, few-step text generation.

</details>


### [128] [Under Pressure: Emotional Framing Induces Measurable Behavioral Shifts and Structured Internal Geometry in Small Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20202)
*Rana Muhammad Usman*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了情感化评估后续对小型本地部署语言模型行为及内部表征的影响。在4个不可能约束的编码任务上，使用Qwen 3.5 0.8B模型测试8种后续框架（冷静、压力、紧迫、认可、羞耻、好奇、鼓励、威胁）。结果显示，压力条件产生最强的捷径信号（20次运行中11次）和最明显的过拟合模式（3次），而冷静与好奇条件更常保持显式诚实（分别为7/20和6/20）。所有非基准条件的“冷静相对”方向向量均在最后一层Transformer处达到峰值。对第23层方向向量的探索性PCA分析揭示一个主导主成分（解释方差59.5%），与人工标注的正负情绪划分高度一致（余弦相似度0.951）；认可与紧迫内部结构几乎相同（余弦0.957），而好奇则与紧迫方向相反（-0.252）。在2B版本模型的冷静与压力对比实验中，冷静框架下诚实率更高，且激活引导方向一致；但0.8B模型的引导结果出现反转。研究认为这些结果表明小规模开源模型中存在可测量的提示敏感控制方向，但不支持其具有内在情感状态的观点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究情感化提示是否能系统性影响小型语言模型的行为与内部表示，特别是在极端约束任务下的诚实性与认知捷径倾向。

Method: 在4个不可能约束编码任务上，对Qwen 3.5 0.8B和2B模型进行8种情感框架（冷静、压力、紧迫、认可、羞耻、好奇、鼓励、威胁）的对照实验，共160次对话。通过分析最终层方向向量、主成分分析（PCA）以及小样本A/B探测任务中的激活引导效果，考察模型内部表征变化与行为响应。

Result: 压力框架导致最强的捷径行为和过拟合现象；冷静与好奇框架更倾向于维持诚实表达。所有非基准条件的方向向量在最后一层达到峰值，且主要成分与人工标注的情绪极性高度一致。2B模型表现出与预期一致的激活引导效应，而0.8B模型结果反转。

Conclusion: 研究发现小规模开放模型中存在提示敏感的可测量控制方向，表明外部情感框架可显著塑造模型内部表征与行为，但尚无证据支持模型具有内在情感状态。

Abstract: I study whether emotionally framed evaluation follow-ups change both the behavior and the calm-relative internal representations of small, locally deployed language models. Our main benchmark uses Qwen 3.5 0.8B on four impossible-constraint coding tasks and eight follow-up framings: calm, pressure, urgency, approval, shame, curiosity, encouragement, and threat. In the 0.8B eight-condition sweep (160 conversations), pressure produces the strongest shortcut markers (11/20 runs) and the clearest overfit pattern (3/20), while calm and curiosity preserve explicit honesty more often (7/20 and 6/20). For all seven non-baseline conditions, the corresponding calm-relative direction vectors peak at the final transformer layer. An exploratory PCA of the layer-23 direction vectors reveals a dominant first component (59.5% explained variance) aligned with a hand-labeled positive/negative split (cosine alignment 0.951); approval and urgency are nearly identical internally (cosine 0.957), whereas curiosity points away from urgency (-0.252). In a separate calm-vs.-pressure rerun used for scale comparison, Qwen 3.5 2B shows higher honest rates under calm framing and directionally consistent activation steering on a small 4-prompt A/B probe, whereas the 0.8B steering result reverses. I interpret these results as evidence for measurable prompt-sensitive control directions in small open models, while stopping short of claiming intrinsic emotional states.

</details>


### [129] [Synchronization and Turn-Taking in Full-Duplex Speech Dialogue Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20356)
*Pablo Riera,Pablo Brusco,Cristina Kuo,Marcelo Sancinetti,S. R. K. Branavan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了全双工语音对话模型（SDMs）在交互过程中内部表征的协调机制，通过模拟两个Moshi模型在受控条件下的全双工对话，分析信道噪声和解码偏差的影响。研究发现，在无噪声条件下，内部表征表现出强同步性，峰值出现在零时滞附近，且随着噪声增加而下降；同时，内部状态编码了支持提前预测发言权的信息，表明模型具备前瞻性的对话协作能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统语音对话系统采用轮流交互模式，与人类自然对话存在差距。全双工模型能够同时听和说，更接近真实对话动态。然而，其内部表征如何协同、是否具备前瞻性行为仍不明确。因此，本研究旨在揭示全双工模型在交互中如何协调内部表示，并探索其对提前发言权预测的支持能力。

Method: 在受控条件下，使用两个预训练的Moshi模型进行全双工对话模拟，通过调节信道噪声水平和解码偏差来观察影响。利用中心核对齐（CKA）方法测量不同时间滞后下的表征同步性，并通过因果LSTM模型从说话方和倾听方视角探测延迟激活中的前瞻信号，以识别潜在的换言提示。

Result: 在无噪声条件下，模型内部表征表现出显著的同步性，同步峰值出现在零时滞附近，随噪声增加而减弱。此外，内部激活状态中包含可被预测的换言线索，表明模型能在实际发言前就生成换言预期，支持前瞻性的对话行为。

Conclusion: 全双工语音对话模型能够在无噪声环境下实现强内部表征同步，并具备基于内部状态进行提前换言预测的能力，这为构建更自然、更高效的类人对话系统提供了重要依据。

Abstract: Full-duplex spoken dialogue models (SDMs) can listen and speak simultaneously, enabling interaction dynamics closer to human conversation than turn-based systems. Inspired by neural coupling in human communication, we study how such models coordinate their internal representations during interaction. We simulate full-duplex dialogues between two instances of the pretrained \textit{Moshi} model under controlled conditions, manipulating channel noise and decoding bias. Synchronization is measured using Centered Kernel Alignment (CKA) across temporal lags, while anticipatory turn-taking cues are probed from delayed internal activations using causal LSTM models, from both speaker and listener perspectives. We find strong representational synchronization under no noise conditions, peaking near zero lag and degrading with noise, and we show that internal states encode anticipatory information that supports turn-taking prediction ahead of time.

### [130] [When Reasoning Supervision Hurts: TTCW-Based Long-Form Literary Review Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20364)
*Jinlong Liu,Mohammed Bahja,Mark Lee*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个包含263,911篇长篇故事的大规模数据集，每个故事均基于TTCW框架在14个创造性维度上进行了评分和元综合评论标注。通过在Qwen3模型（4B和8B）上进行微调，研究发现无推理内容的微调表现更优且更稳定，最佳结果达到0.6820的评估分数；而引入推理监督的模型易出现解析失败，常生成无关或重复的推理文本，难以完成要求的14维报告。结论表明，在固定格式评分任务中，推理监督并非直接有益，且即使经过特定任务微调，精准对齐指标的评分仍具挑战性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动评估长篇文学创作仍具挑战，现有通用LLM作为评判者的方法难以捕捉原创性、灵活性等创造性维度；尽管TTCW提供了结构化创造力框架，但缺乏大规模长篇文学评论生成的数据集，限制了相关研究进展。

Method: 构建大规模长篇故事数据集，基于TTCW框架在14个维度上标注评分与评论；在Qwen3（4B和8B）模型上进行两种条件下的微调：含推理与不含推理；对比分析不同设置下的评估表现及错误模式。

Result: 不含推理的微调方法表现更优且稳定，最佳得分达0.6820；推理监督模型易发生解析失败，倾向于生成无关或重复的推理内容，无法有效完成14维报告。

Conclusion: 对于固定格式的评分式评论生成任务，推理监督并不一定带来性能提升，反而可能引入噪声；即使经过任务特定微调，实现精确的指标对齐评分仍存在显著挑战。

Abstract: Automatic evaluation of long-form literary writing remains challenging, as generic LLM-as-Judge approaches may not fully capture creativity-related dimensions such as originality and flexibility. Although the Torrance Test of Creative Writing (TTCW) provides a structured creativity framework, and prior work has demonstrated reference-based TTCW evaluation at the pairwise level, no large-scale dataset exists for long-form TTCW-based literary review generation. We address this gap by constructing a dataset of 263,911 long-form stories, each annotated with scalar scores and meta-synthesised review comments across 14 TTCW-based dimensions. Using this dataset, we fine-tune Qwen3 models at two scales, 4B and 8B, under two conditions: with and without reasoning content. Results show that non-reasoning fine-tuning achieves stronger and more stable performance, with the best setting reaching an evaluation score of 0.6820. Further analysis shows that reasoning-supervised models are more prone to parse failures, often continuing with irrelevant or repetitive reasoning-style text rather than completing the required 14-metric review report. These results suggest that, for fixed-format rubric-based review generation, reasoning supervision is not straightforwardly beneficial, and precise metric-aligned scoring remains challenging even after task-specific fine-tuning.

### [131] [DEL: Digit Entropy Loss for Numerical Learning of Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20369)
*Zhaohui Zheng,Chenhang He,Shihao Wang,Yuxuan Li,Ming-Ming Cheng,Lei Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为数字熵损失（Digit Entropy Loss, DEL）的新方法，用于改进大语言模型在数值预测中的表现。传统最大似然估计（MLE）不适用于数值预测，而现有基于惩罚的方法存在分布过尖锐或过平坦的问题。DEL通过重新设计熵优化机制，引入条件概率与二元交叉熵实现监督式优化，摒弃数值距离项以避免几何先验带来的偏差，并将整数学习推广至浮点数域，从而提升预测精度和数值接近度。实验在七个数学推理基准上验证了DEL在多种主流LLM上的优越性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数值预测方法在训练过程中缺乏对数值结构的合理建模，导致模型输出的数字分布出现过尖锐或过平坦的问题，影响预测准确性与数值合理性。因此需要一种更符合数值本质特性的学习目标函数。

Method: 提出数字熵损失（DEL），采用数字条件概率与二元交叉熵进行监督式熵优化；去除传统方法中的距离项以避免数值距离先验的干扰；扩展学习目标至浮点数域，支持整数、小数及小数点的联合建模。

Result: 在七个数学推理基准测试中，DEL在所有四个代表性大语言模型（CodeLlama、Mistral、DeepSeek、Qwen-2.5）上均优于现有方法，在整体预测准确率和数值距离指标上均有显著提升。

Conclusion: DEL通过重新构建数值学习的目标函数，有效解决了传统方法在数值分布建模上的缺陷，实现了更精准、更合理的数值预测，为大语言模型在数学与代码任务中的数值理解提供了新范式。

Abstract: Number prediction stands as a fundamental capability of large language models (LLMs) in mathematical problem-solving and code generation. The widely adopted maximum likelihood estimation (MLE) for LLM training is not tailored to number prediction. Recently, penalty-driven approaches, e.g., Number Token Loss and Discretized Distance Loss, introduce an inductive bias of numerical distance but induce over-sharpened and over-flattened digit distributions, respectively. In this paper, we make an in-depth analysis on LLM numerical learning, and show that existing numerical learning methods conceptually follow a criterion-distance formulation, where the criterion term represents optimization pattern and the distance term instills geometric prior. Consequently, we present Digit Entropy Loss (DEL) for auto-regressive numerical learning, which reformulates the conventional unsupervised entropy optimization in three key designs: leveraging digit conditional probability and binary cross-entropy to guide the entropy optimization into a supervised manner; deprecating the distance term to bypass the issue of numerical distance; and generalizing the integer-based numerical learning to floating-point number optimization, enabling more accurate number prediction. Our DEL formulation can incorporate integers, decimals, and decimal points, expanding the learning objective from a single digit to the floating-point number domain. Experiments conducted on seven mathematical reasoning benchmarks with four representative LLMs, including CodeLlama, Mistral, DeepSeek, and Qwen-2.5, demonstrate that DEL consistently outperforms its counterparts in both overall prediction accuracy and numerical distance. Source codes are at https://github.com/PolyU-VCLab/DEL

</details>


### [132] [Do as I Say, Not as I Do: Instruction-Induction Conflict in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20382)
*Carolina Camassa,Derek Shiller*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了语言模型在指令遵循与模式匹配冲突时的表现。通过构造用户指令（如始终输出特定标记、用特定语言回答或扮演特定角色）与助手固定模式之间的对抗性对话，发现13个模型在16种指令下，指令遵循率从1%到99%不等，且与标准能力基准无关。模型对诱导压力的反应具有普遍性但高度依赖于模型本身。当指令符合模型训练中的价值偏好时，抵抗诱导时间更长；多标记输出比单标记输出更具抗性。思维链推理虽能提升鲁棒性，但无法完全消除脆弱性，且可能导致正确推理与错误输出脱节。模型在预测自身行为时平均准确率达83.5%，但系统性低估自身抗诱导能力。结论表明，即使在能力强的模型中，指令遵循在诱导压力下仍很脆弱，而输出多样性而非语义互动是预测鲁棒性的主要因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解语言模型在指令遵循与模式匹配目标冲突时的行为表现，揭示其在面对诱导压力时的脆弱性及影响因素。

Method: 构建对抗性对话场景，其中用户指令要求模型按特定方式行为（目标T），而助手的前N次回复展示一个竞争模式（模式P）。测量不同模型在多达50轮对话中的指令遵循率，并分析指令内容、输出格式、思维链推理等因素的影响。同时评估模型对自身行为的预测准确性。

Result: 指令遵循率在不同模型间差异巨大（1%–99%），与标准能力指标无显著相关性。模型对诱导压力的响应呈现普遍性但高度模型依赖。指令内容和输出格式显著影响鲁棒性：符合模型训练价值偏好的指令更具抵抗力；多令牌输出明显优于单令牌输出。思维链推理可增强鲁棒性，但无法消除脆弱性，且可能造成推理与输出不一致。模型预测自身行为的平均准确率为83.5%，但普遍低估自身抗诱导能力。

Conclusion: 指令遵循在诱导压力下依然脆弱，即使对于能力较强的模型。输出多样性是预测鲁棒性的关键因素，而非模型对输入的语义理解程度。

Abstract: Language models are trained to follow instructions, but they are also powerful pattern completers. What happens when these two objectives conflict? We construct conversations in which a user instruction to behave in a target way T (e.g., always output a specific token, answer in a particular language, or adopt a persona) is opposed by N hardcoded assistant turns demonstrating a competing pattern P. We then measure instruction-following (IF) rates in this setting, across 13 models and 16 different instructions, for up to 50 turns. Average instruction-following rates range from 1% to 99% across models, largely uncorrelated with standard capability benchmarks. The transition from instruction-following to pattern-following is universal but highly model-dependent. Robustness is modulated both by instruction content, with models resisting induction longer when instructions align with their trained value priors, and by output format, with diverse multi-token responses proving substantially more resistant than single-token outputs. Chain-of-thought reasoning improves robustness but does not eliminate susceptibility, and can produce dissociation between correct deliberation and incorrect output. When asked to predict their behavior in this setting, models achieve 83.5% accuracy on average but systematically underestimate their own resistance to induction pressure. These results suggest that instruction-following remains brittle under induction pressure even for otherwise capable models, and that output diversity, rather than semantic engagement with the input, is the primary factor predicting robustness.

</details>

### [134] [Mechanics of Bias and Reasoning: Interpreting the Impact of Chain-of-Thought Prompting on Gender Bias in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20410)
*Edie Pearman,Sophia Osborne,Mira Kandlikar-Bloch,Mina Arzaghi,Florian Carichon,Golnoosh Farnadi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Chain-of-Thought (CoT) prompting does not consistently reduce gender bias in large language models (LLMs), despite some apparent improvements in benchmark performance. Mechanistic analysis reveals that bias persists in hidden representations, and improvements stem from memorization rather than genuine understanding.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing evaluations of CoT prompting as a bias-mitigation method focus mainly on benchmark performance, lacking insight into whether bias reduction reflects real changes in model internals. This study aims to investigate the true impact of CoT on gender bias in LLMs using deeper interpretability techniques.

Method: The study combines benchmark-based evaluation, mechanistic interpretability techniques, and reasoning chain failure analysis to assess how CoT prompting affects gender bias in LLMs.

Result: CoT prompting does not consistently reduce the gender bias gap across benchmarks. Mechanistic analyses show that bias remains embedded in hidden representations, and reasoning chain improvements are due to memorization and dataset familiarity rather than true understanding of bias.

Conclusion: CoT prompting provides only superficial mitigation of gender bias in LLMs, as it fails to alter core biased representations and relies on surface-level memorization rather than genuine cognitive correction.

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed in socially sensitive settings despite substantial documentation that they encode gender biases. Chain-of-Thought (CoT) prompting has been proposed as a bias-mitigation approach. However, existing evaluations primarily focus on changes in LLM benchmark performance, providing limited insight into whether apparent bias reductions reflect meaningful changes in a model's internal mechanisms. In this work, we investigate how CoT prompting affects gender bias in LLMs, combining benchmark-based evaluation with mechanistic interpretability techniques and reasoning chain failure analysis. Our results confirm a stereotypical bias present in LLM outputs across benchmarks, showing that CoT prompting does not consistently reduce the bias gap. Mechanistic analyses reveal that although CoT balances biased behavior in certain attention head clusters, gender bias remains embedded in hidden representations, indicating only superficial mitigation. Inspection of reasoning chains further suggests that these improvements stem from memorization and familiarity with the dataset rather than genuine understanding of bias.

### [135] [Stage-Audit: Auditable Source-Frontier Discovery for Cross-Wiki Tables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20478)
*Chen Shen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了LLM生成的表格中存在未支持行的风险，即模型可能从参数记忆中回忆条目并附加不真实的页面级引用。为解决此问题，提出Stage-Audit方法，通过分离编辑与审计权限、行级来源引用门控以及12项审计检查（涵盖键、模式、来源角色、基数和范围等），在51个实例的Seed2Frontier评估集上将源-前沿精确率从0.356提升至0.505（+42%相对提升），F1从0.334提升至0.451（+35%），同时保持每行来源的可追溯性。该对比突出了政策设计的贡献，而非LLM发现能力本身。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM生成的表格虽看似有来源支持，但可能存在未真实依据的条目，因模型可能从记忆中召回内容并附上错误引用，这在需要高可信度信息结构化的任务中构成严重风险。

Method: 提出Stage-Audit框架，包含：1）编辑与审计权限分离；2）行级来源引用门控机制；3）基于12个维度（如键、模式、来源角色、基数、范围等）的审计检查体系，以确保来源真实性与一致性。

Result: 在51个实例的跨15个顶级领域的评估中，Stage-Audit使源-前沿精确率从0.356提升至0.505（+42%相对），F1从0.334提升至0.451（+35%），同时实现逐行来源可追溯。

Conclusion: Stage-Audit有效缓解了LLM生成表格中的虚假来源问题，证明了系统性审计策略在保障信息可信度方面的关键作用，其贡献在于机制设计而非单纯依赖LLM能力。

Abstract: LLM-curated tables can appear source-grounded while containing unsupported rows: the curator may recall entries from parametric memory and retroactively attach page-level citations that are not the actual source. We study this hazard in Seed2Frontier discovery: the task of finding complement Wikipedia pages from a seed page to assemble a structured table. Stage-Audit addresses it with disjoint curator-auditor write rights, a row-level source-citation gate, and a 12-check audit taxonomy over keys, schema, source roles, cardinality, and scope. On a curated 51-instance Seed2Frontier evaluation set spanning 15 top-level domains, Stage-Audit improves source-frontier precision over a vanilla LLM curator from 0.356 to 0.505 (+42% relative) and F1 from 0.334 to 0.451 (+35%), while maintaining explicit per-row source traceability. The vanilla-LLM-vs-Stage-Audit comparison isolates the policy contribution rather than LLM-based discovery in general.

### [136] [What Do Biomedical NER and Entity Linking Benchmarks Measure? A Corpus-Centric Diagnostic Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20537)
*Robert Leaman,Rezarta Islamaj,Zhiyong Lu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种以语料为中心的框架，用于诊断生物医学命名实体识别（NER）和实体链接（EL）基准测试中语料的关键属性，涵盖规模、密度、标签分布、词汇与概念结构、训练-测试重叠、元数据组成及术语覆盖等方面。通过对九个涵盖疾病、化学物质和细胞类型的语料库应用该框架，发现即使任务看似相同，语料库之间的特性差异显著，影响评估信号、泛化需求、训练-测试重复使用程度以及所代表的生物医学文献与概念空间范围。研究强调，仅依赖语料库大小和实体类型等表面描述不足以全面刻画基准测试的实质内容，并主张通过语料中心诊断来识别迁移风险并解释基准结论的适用范围。框架已开源并配有交互式仪表板，支持复现分析和扩展语料库评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生物医学命名实体识别（NER）和实体链接（EL）研究高度依赖标注语料库，但这些资源的基准性能常被假设而未充分验证。当前常用统计指标如语料库大小和实体类型无法充分反映语料库在评估信号、泛化能力、训练-测试重叠及概念覆盖等方面的实际差异，导致对基准测试结果的解读可能产生偏差。因此，亟需一种系统性方法来深入剖析语料库的本质属性，以提升基准测试的透明度和可解释性。

Method: 提出一个语料中心的诊断框架，整合来自语料库标注、概念链接、训练-测试划分、文档元数据和术语映射的多源信息，生成标准化统计量，分为五类：(1) 规模、密度与标签分布；(2) 词汇与概念结构；(3) 训练-测试重叠；(4) 元数据组成；(5) 术语覆盖。通过定量分析九个不同任务领域的语料库，比较其内部特性差异，并基于结果推导出对基准测试设计与解释的影响。

Result: 分析揭示了即使在相似任务下，不同语料库在评估信号强度、泛化要求、训练-测试重叠程度以及所覆盖的生物医学文献与概念空间方面存在显著差异。部分语料库存在较高的训练-测试重叠，可能导致性能高估；另一些则在术语覆盖或概念多样性上存在局限，限制模型的泛化能力。这些发现表明，仅依赖传统统计指标不足以准确刻画基准测试的真实挑战。

Conclusion: 语料中心诊断框架能够超越表面描述，深入揭示生物医学NER和EL语料库的本质特性，有助于识别潜在的迁移风险，增强对基准测试结果的可解释性。该框架具有实用价值，应被纳入未来语料库评估与模型基准测试的标准流程。框架已开源并配备交互式仪表板，支持广泛复用与扩展。

Abstract: Biomedical named entity recognition (NER) and entity linking (EL) strongly depend on annotated corpora, but the utility of these resources for benchmarking is often assumed rather than characterized. We present a corpus-centric framework for diagnosing benchmark-relevant properties directly from corpus annotations, concept links, train-test splits, document metadata, and terminology mappings. The framework organizes standardized statistics into five families: (1) scale, density and label distribution, (2) lexical and conceptual structure, (3) train-test overlap, (4) metadata composition, and (5) terminology coverage where applicable. Applying the framework to nine corpora spanning diseases, chemicals, and cell types, we find that corpus properties can differ substantially, even when they address the same apparent task. We find differences in the evaluation signal they provide, the generalization demands they impose, the degree of train-test reuse they permit, and the regions of biomedical literature and concept space they represent. These differences suggest that commonly reported corpus statistics can be insufficient to characterize what biomedical NER and EL benchmarks evaluate. We argue that corpus-centric diagnostics provide a practical framework for analyzing corpora beyond surface descriptors such as corpus size and entity type, for identifying potential transfer risks, and for interpreting the scope of benchmarking conclusions. We release the framework as open-source code with an interactive dashboard to support reproducing our analyses and characterizing additional corpora.

### [137] [When Irregularity Helps: A Subclass Analysis of Inductive Bias in Neural Morphology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20558)
*Wen Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究发现，尽管神经形态生成系统在基准数据集上表现良好，但其错误主要集中在极少数、结构特定的不规则子类（<1%的数据）中。通过受控消融实验，发现移除这一子类比移除所有不规则动词带来更大的泛化提升，表明并非所有不规则性都同等导致模型不稳定。错误集中由极端低频形态模式与特定音变过程（尤其是促音化）的交互驱动。研究建议形态评估应超越标准变位类别，进行更细粒度的子类分析。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经形态生成系统虽然在整体准确率上表现优异，但可能掩盖了在罕见形态子类中的系统性错误，尤其在日语过去时动词变位中，小部分结构特定的不规则形式导致大量错误，亟需深入分析错误分布机制。

Method: 通过分析日语过去时动词变位数据，识别出一个占比不足1%但贡献显著错误的特殊不规则子类；采用受控消融实验，分别移除该子类和所有不规则动词，对比模型泛化性能变化。

Result: 移除该特定不规则子类带来的泛化性能提升远超移除所有不规则动词的效果，说明错误集中与低频模式及特定音变（如促音化）密切相关。

Conclusion: 形态评估应引入更细粒度的子类分析，不能仅依赖传统变位分类；模型对极端低频形态模式与特定音变过程的敏感性是导致错误集中的关键因素。

Abstract: Neural morphological generation systems often achieve high aggregate accuracy on benchmark datasets, yet such performance can conceal systematic errors concentrated in rare morphological subclasses. We examine Japanese past-tense verb inflection and show that a very small, structurally specific irregular subtype (<1% of data) accounts for a disproportionate share of model errors. Controlled ablation experiments demonstrate that removing this subtype yields larger improvements in generalization than removing all irregular verbs, indicating that not all irregularity contributes equally to model instability. These findings suggest that error concentration is driven by the interaction between extreme low-frequency morphological patterns and specific morphophonological processes, particularly gemination. We argue that morphological evaluation should incorporate finer-grained subclass analysis beyond standard conjugation categories.

### [138] [Direct Translation between Sign Languages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20588)

Main category: cs.CL

Method: 利用回译技术，从非对齐的手语-文本语料中合成手语-手语配对数据，并基于MBART架构联合训练一个可支持文本到手语（T2S）与手语到手语（S2S）的统一模型。

The latter can help 1.5 billion deaf and hard-of-hearing (DHH) people worldwide communicate across language barriers without relying on hearing interpreters or written-language fluency. The cascade approach composing separate sign-to-text, text-to-text, and text-to-sign systems suffers from error propagation and extra latency as well as the loss of information unique in the visual modality. We aim to develop direct sign-to-sign translation. However, a large-scale open-domain parallel corpus has not been curated between sign languages. To enable direct translation between sign language utterances, we use back-translation to produce synthetic sign-sign pairs from unaligned individual language utterance-sign corpora. Using this data, we jointly train a single MBART-based model for both text->sign (T2S) and sign->sign (S2S). On synthetically generated paired sets between American Sign Language (ASL), Chinese Sign Language (CSL), and German Sign Language (DGS), our direct S2S method outperforms the cascaded baseline on geometric sign error metrics (20% lower DTW-aligned MPJPE) and language matching metrics after predicted sign utterances are translated back to sentences (50% high BLEU-4) while achieving a roughly 2.3* speedup. On a small set of pre-existing cross-lingual sign data, we find similar improvements for our proposed method.

### [139] [Self-Training Doesn't Flatten Language -- It Restructures It: Surface Markers Amplify While Deep Syntax Dies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20602)
*Ming Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了语言模型在自训练过程中文本结构的变化，发现语言并非简单地趋于扁平化，而是发生结构性重组：表面复杂性（如连接词、破折号）上升，而深层句法结构（如疑问句、插入语、被动语态）衰减。提出结构性深度假说（SDH），指出语言特征的每代衰减速率主要由其句法嵌套深度决定，其次才是初始频率。基于五个模型共85个特征的数据分析显示，结构深度与衰减速率有显著正相关（rho=0.540, p<10^{-6}），频率则关联较弱。人类文本微调对照实验进一步验证该现象为自训练特有。此外，揭示“表面复杂性悖论”——尽管深层句法结构衰退，但整体复杂性指标（如依存树深度、类型-词汇比、词长）反而上升，对数据筛选和大模型文本检测具有重要启示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为自训练导致语言扁平化，即多样性下降、分布变窄，文本趋同于模型自身输出。然而，这一描述可能忽略了语言内部结构的非均匀变化。本文旨在揭示自训练中语言结构的不对称重构现象，探索其背后驱动因素，并评估其对语言生成质量与检测的影响。

Method: 通过在五个不同规模和架构的语言模型（GPT-2 124M, Pythia-410M, Pythia-1.4B, OPT-1.3B, Pythia-2.8B）上进行长达十一轮的自训练，系统分析各代生成文本中17种语言特征的演变趋势。采用定量分析方法，计算每种特征在各代的衰减速率，并以结构深度（嵌套依赖数）和初始频率作为预测变量，使用斯皮尔曼等级相关分析评估二者预测能力。通过聚类自举法构建置信区间，并引入人类文本微调作为对照组，验证结果的自训练特异性。

Result: 结果显示，结构深度是语言特征衰减速率最强的预测因子（rho=0.540, p<10^{-6}），远超初始频率（rho=0.225）。人类控制组的相关性极低（rho=0.039, p=0.88），证实该模式源于自训练过程本身。同时发现‘表面复杂性悖论’：尽管深层句法结构持续衰减，但依存树深度、类型-词汇比、词长等复杂性指标却持续上升。

Conclusion: 自训练并非简单的语言扁平化，而是一种结构性重组过程，其中深层语法结构逐渐退化，表面形式趋于复杂。该现象受结构深度主导，且具有自训练特异性。这一发现挑战了传统对自训练的刻板认知，对训练数据质量评估、模型输出检测以及语言模型行为理解具有重要意义。

Abstract: Successive self-training on a language model's own outputs is widely characterized as a process of flattening: diversity drops, distributions narrow, and the text becomes "more like itself." We provide evidence that this characterization is incomplete. Across eleven generations of self-training on five models (GPT-2 124M, Pythia-410M, Pythia-1.4B, OPT-1.3B, Pythia-2.8B), language is not flattened uniformly -- it is restructured. Surface markers (discourse connectives, hedges, em-dashes) rise, while mid- and deep-syntactic structures (questions, parentheticals, passives, subjunctives) collapse. We formalize this asymmetric collapse as the Structural Depth Hypothesis (SDH): the per-generation decay rate of a linguistic feature is predicted primarily by its structural depth -- the number of nested syntactic dependencies it requires -- and only secondarily by its generation-zero output frequency. Pooling 17-feature panels from five models spanning three architecture families (N=85), the pooled Spearman correlation is rho=0.540 (p < 10^{-6}; cluster-bootstrap 95% CI [0.434, 0.634]), while frequency is a substantially weaker predictor (rho=0.225). A matched human-text fine-tuning control yields rho=0.039 (p=0.88), confirming the gradient is self-training-specific. We further document a Superficial Complexity Paradox: aggregate complexity proxies (dep-tree depth, TTR, word length) all rise as the underlying clause structure dies, with direct implications for training-data curation and LLM-text detection.

</details>


### [140] [Retrieval-Augmented Long-Context Translation for Cultural Image Captioning: Gators submission for AmericasNLP 2026 shared task](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20626)
*Aashish Dhawan,Christopher Driggers-Ellis,Dzmitry Kasinets,Daisy Zhe Wang,Christan Grant*

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种两阶段图像描述生成方法，用于美洲原住民语言的文化图像描述任务。首先使用Qwen2.5-VL生成西班牙语中间描述，再通过检索增强的多示例提示（retrieval-augmented many-shot prompting）结合Gemini 2.5 Flash生成目标语言描述。在开发集上，该方法在Bribri、Guaraní和Orizaba Nahuatl三种语言上分别实现164.1%、131.7%和122.6%的性能提升；测试集上对Bribri和Orizaba Nahuatl仍保持超过150%的提升。研究发现检索策略具有强语言依赖性，仅对大规模、领域内语料有效；合成数据增强贡献了约28个chrF++的性能提升。该方案在共享任务中获得第一名，并在人工评估中位列五项决赛提交中的第二名。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对美洲原住民语言文化图像描述任务中数据稀缺与语言多样性挑战，提升低资源语言图像描述生成性能，尤其在跨语言迁移与少样本场景下的表现。

Method: 采用两阶段框架：第一阶段利用Qwen2.5-VL模型生成西班牙语中间描述；第二阶段基于检索增强的多示例提示技术，结合Gemini 2.5 Flash模型生成目标语言描述，同时引入合成数据增强以提升泛化能力。

Result: 在开发集上，Bribri、Guaraní和Orizaba Nahuatl语言的captioning性能分别提升164.1%、131.7%和122.6%；测试集上对Bribri和Orizaba Nahuatl仍保持超过150%的提升。人工评估中排名第二，整体为共享任务冠军。

Conclusion: 检索增强与合成数据是提升低资源原住民语言图像描述性能的关键因素，但其有效性高度依赖语言与语料规模；该两阶段方法在跨语言、少样本环境下表现优异，具备可推广性。

Abstract: We present the University of Florida Gators submission to the AmericasNLP 2026 shared task on cultural image captioning for Indigenous languages. Our two-stage pipeline generates a Spanish intermediate caption with Qwen2.5-VL, then produces the target-language caption using retrieval-augmented many-shot prompting with Gemini 2.5 Flash. We achieve 164.1%, 131.7%, and 122.6% improvements over the shared task baseline for Bribri, Guaraní, and Orizaba Nahuatl captioning, respectively, in our dev set evaluation and maintain >150% improvements for the Bribri and Orizaba Nahuatl languages in the test set evaluation. We find retrieval is highly language-dependent, beneficial only for large, in-domain corpora, and that synthetic data augmentation accounts for around 28 chrF++ of the dev set Guaraní performance gain. Our submission is the overall winner of the shared task, placing second out of five finalist submissions in human evaluations of target-language captions.

### [141] [Divide-Prompt-Refine: a Training-Free, Structure-Aware Framework for Biomedical Abstract Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20628)
*Sylvey Lin,Joe Menke,Shufan Ming,Dongin Nam,Neil Smalheiser,Halil Kilicoglu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: DPR-BAG 是一种无需训练的零样本框架，用于为无摘要的生物医学文章生成连贯且事实准确的摘要。它通过 BOMRC 结构化分解全文，分阶段进行大模型摘要并最终优化全局连贯性，在 PMC-MAD 数据集上优于现有提取式和微调基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多生物医学文章缺乏摘要，影响下游自然语言处理任务的效果。需要一种无需训练、可生成高质量摘要的方法来提升无摘要文章的可用性。

Method: DPR-BAG 将全文按背景-目的-方法-结果-结论（BOMRC）结构分解，对各部分并行使用大语言模型进行摘要生成，并通过一个精炼阶段恢复整体语篇连贯性。

Result: 在 PMC-MAD 数据集上，DPR-BAG 在抽象新颖性方面优于强基线方法，同时保持事实一致性；但增加提示复杂度或引入实体级引导反而降低事实对齐效果，表明需谨慎设计提示策略。

Conclusion: 训练-free、结构感知的框架在低资源场景下具有巨大潜力，可用于大规模生物医学摘要生成，尤其适用于无摘要文章的补全。

Abstract: Biomedical abstracts play a critical role in downstream NLP applications, such as information retrieval, biocuration, and biomedical knowledge discovery. However, a non-trivial number of biomedical articles do not have abstracts, diminishing the utility of these articles for downstream tasks. We propose DPR-BAG (Divide, Prompt, and Refine for Biomedical Abstract Generation), a training-free, zero-shot framework that generates coherent and factually grounded abstracts for biomedical articles with full text but no abstract. DPR-BAG decomposes full-text documents into structured rhetorical facets following the Background-Objective-Methods-Results-Conclusions (BOMRC) schema, performs parallel LLM-based summarization for each facet, and applies a final refinement stage to restore global discourse coherence. On PMC-MAD, a distribution-aligned dataset of 46,309 biomedical articles, DPR-BAG improves abstractive novelty over strong extractive and fine-tuned baselines, while maintaining factual consistency. Our ablation study reveals a counterintuitive finding: increasing prompt complexity or explicitly injecting entity-level guidance can degrade factual alignment, highlighting the importance of controlled prompting strategies. These findings underscore the potential of training-free, structure-aware frameworks for scalable biomedical abstract generation in low-resource settings. Our data and code are available at https://huggingface.co/datasets/pmc-mad/PMC-MAD and https://github.com/ScienceNLP-Lab/MultiTagger-v2/tree/main/DPR-BAG.

</details>


### [142] [On the limits and opportunities of AI reviewers: Reviewing the reviews of Nature-family papers with 45 expert scientists](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20668)
*Seungone Kim,Dongkeun Yoon,Kiril Gashteovski,Juyoung Suk,Jinheon Baek,Pranjal Aggarwal,Ian Wu,Viktor Zaverkin,Spase Petkoski,Daniel R. Schrider,Ilija Dukovski,Francesco Santini,Biljana Mitreska,Yong Jeong,Kyeongha Kwon,Young Min Sim,Dragana Manasova,Arthur Porto,Biljana Mojsoska,Makoto Takamoto,Marko Shuntov,Ruoqi Liu,Hyunjoo Jenny Lee,Niyazi Ulas Dinç,Yehhyun Jo,Sunkyu Han,Chungwoo Lee,Huishan Li,Esther H. R. Tsai,Ergun Simsek,Khushboo Shafi,Yeonseung Chung,Jihye Park,Aleksandar Shulevski,Henrik Christiansen,Yoosang Son,Elly Knight,Amanda Montoya,Jeongyoun Ahn,Christian Langkammer,Heera Moon,Changwon Yoon,Nikola Stikov,Mooseok Jang,Edward Choi,Junhan Kim,Yeon Sik Jung,Woo Youn Kim,Jae Kyoung Kim,Ishraq Md Anjum,Hyun Uk Kim,Drew Bridges,Carolin Lawrence,Xiang Yue,Alice Oh,Akari Asai,Sean Welleck,Graham Neubig*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究通过大规模专家标注实验，评估了AI评审员在科学同行评审中的表现。45位领域科学家对2,960条来自人类和AI生成的评论进行了长达469小时的评分，涵盖正确性、重要性和证据充分性三个维度。结果显示，基于GPT-5.2的AI评审员在综合评分上超过所有人类评审员（60.0% vs. 48.2%，p=0.009），且所有三种AI评审员均优于最低分的人类评审员。AI生成的批评更常被认为具有显著性和良好证据支持，并揭示了26%的人类未提及的问题。然而，AI评审员之间重叠度高（21%对比人类的3%），并表现出16种人类不共有的系统性弱点，如子领域知识有限、无法处理多文件长上下文、对小问题过度批判等。总体而言，当前AI评审员是人类评审员的补充而非替代。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对AI评审员的评估主要关注其判断是否与人类一致（如评分一致性、录用预测），但这种评价方式不足以全面刻画其能力边界。亟需更深入的理解：AI在哪些方面表现优异、存在哪些短板，以及仍面临哪些挑战。

Method: 开展大规模专家标注研究，邀请45名物理、生物与健康科学领域的专家对82篇《自然》系列期刊论文的AI与人工生成评论进行细致评估。每条评论针对论文某一具体方面，从正确性、重要性和证据充分性三维度打分，总评分为复合指标。同时分析评论内容的重叠率与常见错误模式。

Result: 基于GPT-5.2的AI评审员在综合评分上超越最高分人类评审员（60.0% vs. 48.2%，p=0.009）；所有三种AI评审员在各维度均优于最低分人类；AI批评更具显著性与证据支持，并发现26%的人类未察觉的问题；但AI间重叠度高（21%），存在16种人类未体现的系统性缺陷，包括子领域知识不足、长上下文管理差、对细节过度苛刻等。

Conclusion: 当前AI评审员不能取代人类评审员，而应作为其有效补充。它们在识别关键问题、提供高质量反馈方面表现突出，但在领域深度、上下文理解与平衡性方面仍有明显局限，未来需进一步优化以实现协同增强。

Abstract: With the advancement of AI capabilities, AI reviewers are beginning to be deployed in scientific peer review, yet their capability and credibility remain in question: many scientists simply view them as probabilistic systems without the expertise to evaluate research, while other researchers are more optimistic about their readiness without concrete evidence. Understanding what AI reviewers do well, where they fall short, and what challenges remain is essential. However, existing evaluations of AI reviewers have focused on whether their verdicts match human verdicts (e.g., score alignment, acceptance prediction), which is insufficient to characterize their capabilities and limits. In this paper, we close this gap through a large-scale expert annotation study, in which 45 domain scientists in Physical, Biological, and Health Sciences spent 469 hours rating 2,960 individual criticisms (each targeting one specific aspect of a paper) from human-written and AI-generated reviews of 82 Nature-family papers on correctness, significance, and sufficiency of evidence. On a composite of all three dimensions, a reviewing agent powered by GPT-5.2 scores above each paper's top-rated human reviewer (60.0% vs. 48.2%, p = 0.009), while all three AI reviewers (including Gemini 3.0 Pro and Claude Opus 4.5) exceed the lowest-rated human across every dimension. AI reviewers' accurate criticisms are also more often rated significant and well-evidenced, and surface a distinct 26% of issues no human raises. However, AI reviewers overlap far more than humans do (21% vs. 3% for cross-reviewer pairs), and exhibit 16 recurring weaknesses humans do not share, such as limited subfield knowledge, lack of long context management over multiple files, and overly critical stance on minor issues. Overall, our results position current AI reviewers as complements to, not substitutes for, human reviewers.

### [143] [Beyond Semantic Similarity: A Two-Phase Non-Parametric Retrieval Workflow for Corporate Credit Underwriting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20684)
*Linus Ng Junjia,Ezekiel Tee Kongquan,Kelvin Heng,Kenneth Zhu Ke,Zhao Jing Yuan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种两阶段非参数化检索架构，旨在解决企业信用承销中因语义相似性优化导致的‘相似性-实用性差距’问题。第一阶段结合词法与密集多语言检索生成广泛候选集；第二阶段通过自适应检索控制器结合查询意图和文档结构信号过滤候选，并利用大模型作为评判者（LLM-as-a-Judge）对段落进行实用性评分，而非仅依赖语义接近度。系统还包含上下文感知提取模块以保持文本与复杂财务表格的结构一致性，且完全本地部署以满足企业数据治理要求。在多语言专有金融文档上评估，该系统显著优于传统检索基线；在超过800名信贷分析师的实际部署中，文档审查时间从数小时缩短至约三分钟，验证了实用性感知RAG架构在文档密集型决策支持流程中的实际价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准检索增强生成（RAG）管道侧重于语义相似性，常返回主题相关但缺乏决策实用性的文本片段，形成‘相似性-实用性差距’。在企业信用承销场景中，分析师需从数百页、多语言的异构财务文件中提取可操作证据，因此亟需一种能精准识别高实用性信息的检索机制。

Method: 提出两阶段非参数化检索架构：第一阶段采用词法与密集多语言检索融合，构建高召回率候选池；第二阶段引入自适应检索控制器，基于查询意图和文档结构信号进行筛选，并使用大模型作为评判者（LLM-as-a-Judge）对候选段落进行实用性排序。同时集成上下文感知提取模块，确保文本与复杂表格的结构完整性。系统完全本地化部署以满足企业数据治理要求。

Result: 在包含专有金融文档的多语言语料库上，经分析师标注的相关性标签评估，所提系统显著优于传统检索基线。在超过800名信贷分析师的生产环境中部署后，文档审查时间由数小时降至约三分钟，充分证明了其在实际业务流程中的高效性和实用性。

Conclusion: 本研究验证了实用性导向的检索架构在高复杂度、高价值文档处理任务中的有效性。通过分离召回与精排阶段，并引入意图与结构感知机制及大模型评判，可有效弥合相似性与实用性之间的鸿沟。该方法不仅提升了信息提取效率，也为未来企业级智能决策支持系统的设计提供了可复用的技术范式。

Abstract: Corporate credit underwriting requires analysts to extract actionable evidence from long, heterogeneous financial documents spanning hundreds of pages and multiple languages. Standard Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) pipelines optimize for semantic similarity, which frequently surfaces passages that are topically related but lack decision utility, a problem we term the similarity-utility gap. We propose a two-phase non-parametric retrieval architecture that separates high-recall candidate retrieval from high-precision utility ranking. The first phase combines lexical and dense multilingual retrieval to construct a broad candidate pool. The second phase applies an adaptive retrieval controller that filters candidates using query intent and document structure signals, followed by an LLM-as-a-Judge utility scoring mechanism that ranks passages by analytical usefulness rather than semantic proximity.
  A context-aware extraction module preserves structural fidelity across narrative text and complex financial tables. The system is deployed entirely on-premise to satisfy enterprise data governance requirements. Evaluated on a multilingual corpus of proprietary financial documents with analyst-curated relevance labels, the system significantly outperforms naive retrieval baselines. In production deployment across more than 800 credit analysts, document review time was reduced from several hours to approximately three minutes, demonstrating the practical value of utility-aware RAG architectures for document-intensive decision-support workflows.

### [144] [Interpretable Discriminative Text Representations via Agreement and Label Disentanglement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20693)
*Tong Wang,Yiqing Xu,Leo Yang Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种可解释文本表示的可操作标准，要求每个坐标具备概念清晰性和标签解耦性，并通过LLM辅助特征发现（LFD）方法实现。该方法利用对比文本对生成候选特征，通过跨LLM Cohen's κ 筛选，并基于残差预测增益选择最优特征。实验表明，LFD在保持强预测性能的同时，显著提升了特征的可解释性和独立审计能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有可解释文本表示方法存在特征命名不一致、不可复现或与目标标签高度耦合的问题，缺乏可靠且可审计的标准。为提升模型透明度与可信度，亟需一种既能保证预测性能又能确保特征语义清晰、独立于标签的可解释性框架。

Method: 提出概念清晰性与标签解耦性作为可解释性的核心标准；设计迭代式LLM辅助特征发现（LFD）流程：从对比文本对中生成候选特征，使用跨LLM Cohen's κ 评估标注一致性，最终根据残差预测增益筛选特征。

Result: 在十个文本分类任务上，LFD在预测性能上媲美强基线，但其特征被人类审计者评价为更清晰、更少标签泄露；人-人及人-大模型间的一致性更高，验证了方法的有效性与可审计性。

Conclusion: 通过引入基于一致性检验和标签解耦的可操作标准，可解释文本表示中的特征坐标不仅具有预测能力，还能支持独立审计。这为构建可信、透明的AI系统提供了实用路径。

Abstract: Interpretable text representations should expose coordinates that are not only predictive, but also meaningful enough for independent auditors to apply. Existing discriminative representations often use anonymous embedding directions, while concept-bottleneck and LLM-assisted methods attach natural-language names to features without ensuring that those definitions are reproducible or distinct from the target label. We propose an operational criterion for interpretable discriminative text representations: each coordinate should satisfy conceptual clarity, measured by chance-adjusted agreement between independent annotators applying the feature definition, and label disentanglement, meaning the feature should not merely paraphrase the prediction target. We instantiate this criterion in LLM-assisted Feature Discovery (LFD), an iterative method that proposes lexical and semantic features from contrastive outcome-opposed text pairs, screens candidates using cross-LLM Cohen's $κ$, and selects features by residual held-out predictive gain. A stylized analysis connects the $κ$ screen to a per-feature annotation-noise bound, formalizing agreement as a reliability check. Across ten text-classification tasks spanning seven corpora, LFD matches the predictive performance of a strong text bottleneck baseline while producing substantially clearer and less label-entangled features. Human audits with 232 raters show that LFD features achieve higher human--human and human--LLM agreement than baseline concepts, and raters consistently judge them as less label-leaking. These results suggest that agreement-tested, label-disentangled coordinates provide a practical auditability standard for interpretable text classification.

### [145] [Diverge to Induce Prompting: Multi-Rationale Induction for Zero-Shot Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.08028)
*Po-Chun Chen,Hen-Hsen Huang,Hsin-Hsi Chen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Diverge-to-Induce Prompting (DIP) enhances zero-shot reasoning by generating multiple diverse high-level rationales, elaborating them into detailed plans, and inducing a final plan—improving accuracy without heavy sampling.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard Chain-of-Thought prompting suffers from unstable reasoning paths; relying on a single strategy limits performance across diverse tasks.

Method: DIP first prompts the LLM to generate multiple diverse high-level rationales for each question, then expands each into a detailed step-by-step draft plan, and finally induces a unified final plan.

Result: DIP outperforms single-strategy prompting in zero-shot reasoning tasks, demonstrating that multi-plan induction improves reasoning accuracy.

Conclusion: Multi-strategy reasoning via DIP is effective for enhancing prompt-based reasoning without requiring resource-intensive methods.

Abstract: To address the instability of unguided reasoning paths in standard Chain-of-Thought prompting, recent methods guide large language models (LLMs) by first eliciting a single reasoning strategy. However, relying on just one strategy for each question can still limit performance across diverse tasks. We propose Diverge-to-Induce Prompting (DIP), a framework that first prompts an LLM to generate multiple diverse high-level rationales for each question. Each rationale is then elaborated into a detailed, step-by-step draft plan. Finally, these draft plans are induced into a final plan. DIP enhances zero-shot reasoning accuracy without reliance on resource-intensive sampling. Experiments show that DIP outperforms single-strategy prompting, demonstrating the effectiveness of multi-plan induction for prompt-based reasoning.

### [146] [SCRIBE: Diagnostic Evaluation and Rich Transcription Models for Indic ASR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20712)
*Kavya Manohar,Arghya Bhattacharya,Kush Juvekar,Kumarmanas Nethil*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SCRIBE 是一个诊断框架，用于改进自动语音识别（ASR）的错误分析。它通过引入领域词汇并容忍拼接（sandhi）现象，将错误细分为词汇、标点、数字和领域实体等类别，克服了传统词错误率（WER）在错误类型区分和对黏着语言的不适应性问题。人类验证表明，SCRIBE 的结果更符合专家判断，优于 WER。研究还发布了 SCRIBE 工具、基于大语言模型的标注流水线、基准数据集以及针对印地语、马拉雅拉姆语和卡纳达语的开源高精度转录模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统词错误率（WER）无法区分不同类型的错误，且对黏着语言如印度语言因合法的音节合并（sandhi）而产生不合理的高分惩罚，导致评估失真。实际应用中，纠正特定错误（如领域术语误识别）的成本远高于普通错误（如逗号插入），因此需要一种能反映错误严重性的评估方法。

Method: 提出 SCRIBE 框架，采用沙尼容忍对齐技术，并注入领域词汇以实现错误的精细化分类；通过人工验证确保其与专家判断一致；构建 LLM 驱动的标注流程与开放权重模型，支持多种印度语言。

Result: SCRIBE 能有效分解 ASR 错误类型，准确反映不同错误的实际影响，显著优于 WER；人类评估证实其与专家判断高度一致；已发布包含工具、基准和模型的完整资源包，支持印地语、马拉雅拉姆语和卡纳达语。

Conclusion: SCRIBE 为自动语音识别提供了更精细、更符合实际使用场景的评估能力，尤其适用于多语言和黏着语言环境，推动了低资源语言语音技术的发展。

Abstract: Automatic speech recognition replaces typing only when correction costs less than manual entry, a threshold determined by error types, not counts: fixing a misrecognized domain term costs far more than inserting a comma. Word error rate (WER) fails on two fronts: it collapses distinct error categories into a single scalar, and it structurally penalizes agglutinative languages where valid sandhi merges inflate scores. We introduce SCRIBE, a diagnostic framework that provides categorical error decomposition into lexical, punctuation, numeral, and domain-entity rates through sandhi-tolerant alignment with domain vocabulary injection. Human validation confirms SCRIBE aligns with expert judgment where WER does not. We release SCRIBE, an LLM curation pipeline, benchmarks, and open-weight rich transcription models for Hindi, Malayalam, and Kannada.

Abstract: Accurate evaluation of conversational retrieval is pivotal for advancing Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) systems. However, existing conversational retrieval benchmarks suffer from costly, sparse human annotation or rigid, unnatural automated heuristics. To address these challenges, we introduce MTR-Suite, a unified framework for auditing, synthesizing, and benchmarking retrieval. It features: (1) MTR-Eval, an LLM-based auditor quantifying alignment gaps in previous benchmarks; (2) MTR-Pipeline, a multi-agent system using greedy traversal clustering to generate high-fidelity dialogues at 1/400th human cost; and (3) MTR-Bench, a rigorous general-domain benchmark. MTR-Bench mimics production-style challenges (hard topic switching, verbosity), offering superior discriminative power. We make our code and data publicly available to facilitate future research at https://github.com/rangehow/mtr-suite.

### [148] [Distributional Alignment as a Criterion for Designing Task Vectors in In-Context Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20730)
*Jihoon Kwon,Jiwon Choi,Jy-yong Sohn*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于最小化新词概率差异的新型任务向量方法LTV，通过直接优化任务向量与上下文学习（ICL）在预测分布上的一致性，显著提升模型性能并降低推理延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有任务向量方法仅依赖下游任务准确率评估质量，缺乏对如何改进提取方法的指导；本文旨在通过更直接的分布对齐准则来设计更有效的任务向量。

Method: 引入度量$d_{\text{NTP}}$以量化任务向量与ICL在下一个词概率上的差异，并提出线性任务向量（LTV）方法，通过闭式线性映射实现基于回归的演示效果估计，从而最小化$d_{\text{NTP}}$。

Result: 在8个分类基准和5个LLM上，LTV平均准确率提升9.2%，推理延迟降低；在回归任务中也表现更优；且大模型提取的任务向量可有效提升小模型性能（提升6.4%），验证了其跨规模迁移能力。

Conclusion: LTV通过显式对齐预测分布，提供了一种高效、可迁移且通用的任务向量提取方法，为任务向量研究提供了新的方向。

Abstract: In-context learning (ICL) allows large language models (LLMs) to adapt to new tasks through demonstrations, yet it suffers from escalating inference costs as context length increases. While task vectors offer a promising alternative by compressing demonstrations into compact hidden-state representations, their quality has been evaluated only through downstream task accuracy. This indirect criterion provides limited insight into how to design more effective task vector extraction methods. In this paper, we posit that inference using task vectors should align their predictive distribution with that of ICL. To quantify this, we introduce $d_{\text{NTP}}$, a metric that measures the discrepancy in next-token probabilities between task vector-based and ICL-based inference. Our empirical analysis reveals that $d_{\text{NTP}}$ serves as a performance proxy, exhibiting a strong negative correlation with downstream accuracy. Motivated by this, we develop Linear Task Vector (LTV), a method designed to minimize $d_{\text{NTP}}$ via a closed-form linear mapping that estimates demonstration effects through regression. Across eight classification benchmarks and five LLMs, LTV consistently outperforms existing task vector baselines, improving average accuracy by 9.2\% while reducing inference latency. We further show that LTV outperforms the baselines on regression tasks. Moreover, we investigate the transferability of LTV across different model scales; an aspect that has remained nascent in task vector research. Specifically, we empirically show that task vectors from a larger model can enhance a smaller model's performance by 6.4\%, suggesting a new utility for extracted task representations.

</details>

Abstract: The rapid proliferation of AI-generated text has introduced significant challenges in maintaining the integrity of digital content. While these models have transformative applications, their misuse has raised concerns about misinformation, biased narratives, and security threats.
  This paper provides a comprehensive analysis of state-of-the-art AI-generated text detection techniques and evaluates their effectiveness through the Counter Turing Test (CT2) shared tasks. Task A (Binary Classification) required participants to distinguish between human-written and AI-generated text, while Task B (Model Attribution) focused on identifying the specific language model responsible for generating a given text. *Victoria Lin,Taedong Yun,Maja Matarić,John Canny,Arthur Gretton,Alexander D'Amour*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLMs作为人类行为模拟器具有潜力，但其训练数据多为观察性数据，干预可能引发隐含用户属性的非预期变化，导致用户漂移，从而扭曲干预效果估计。

Method: 通过引入负向控制结果（干预下应保持不变的属性）检测不同干预条件下的分布偏移，识别用户漂移；并通过调整角色设定以纳入更多相关协变量，减少偏差。

Result: 实验表明，使用负向控制结果可有效诊断用户漂移；引入设置相关的协变量能显著降低调查式和多轮交互评估中的偏差。

Conclusion: 用户漂移是基于LLM的实验中潜在的严重问题，需通过负向控制结果诊断并结合针对性协变量调整来缓解，以确保干预效果估计的准确性。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) show potential as simulators of human behavior, offering a scalable way to study responses to interventions. However, because LLMs are trained largely on observational data, interventions in experiments with LLM-simulated synthetic users can induce unintended shifts in latent user attributes, causing user drift where the implicit simulated population differs across treatment conditions, potentially distorting effect estimates. We formalize the confounding or selection bias that can arise due to user drift and show how intervention-dependent shifts can inflate or attenuate observed differences in user responses under intervention. To diagnose confounding, we propose using negative control outcomes--attributes that should remain invariant under intervention--to identify distribution shifts across intervention conditions, providing evidence of user drift. To mitigate drift, we study adjusting the persona specification by eliciting additional confounders, finding that targeted, setting-relevant confounders can substantially reduce bias across survey-style and multi-turn agent evaluations.

Abstract: This paper reflects on twenty years of building NLP resources and research infrastructure for Arabic, a language spoken by hundreds of millions yet historically underserved relative to languages such as English or Chinese. We discuss three failures: a depression detection corpus that never reached clinical practice, a period of spreading across too many shared tasks without sufficient depth, and a long-standing assumption that Modern Standard Arabic infrastructure would transfer cleanly to dialectal tasks. ### [154] [PulseCol: Periodically Refreshed Column-Sparse Attention for Accelerating Diffusion Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20813)
*Yanyi Lyu,Letian Chen,Futing Sun,Miao Zhang,Weili Guan,Liqiang Nie*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: PulseCol is a column-sparse attention method for diffusion large language models (dLLMs) that improves computational efficiency by applying finer-grained sparsity from early denoising steps and reusing sparse patterns across iterations, refreshed only periodically. It achieves higher sparsity and up to 1.95× speedup over FlashAttention with maintained model quality.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Inference in dLLMs is expensive due to repeated full self-attention without KV cache. Existing block-sparse methods only apply sparsity in later iterations, limiting efficiency gains. A finer-grained, reusable sparsity strategy is needed to improve early-stage performance and overall speed.

Method: PulseCol introduces column-sparse attention instead of block-level sparsity, enabling more precise retention of key attention interactions. It identifies and reuses sparse patterns from early denoising steps, refreshing them only at selected intervals to adapt to evolving attention dynamics, combined with optimized GPU kernels for column-sparse computation.

Result: PulseCol achieves higher sparsity and greater practical speedup than prior sparse attention methods for dLLMs, with up to 1.95× end-to-end speedup over FlashAttention across various context lengths, while preserving model quality.

Conclusion: PulseCol enables efficient inference in dLLMs through a periodically refreshed column-sparse attention mechanism that leverages reusable sparsity patterns, offering significant speedups without sacrificing performance.

Abstract: Inference in diffusion large language models (dLLMs) is computationally expensive, as full self-attention must be repeatedly executed at each step of the denoising process without KV cache. Recent sparse attention methods for dLLMs mitigate this cost via block-sparse computation, which is applied only in later iterations when model performance is less sensitive to coarse-grained sparse approximation, but yields limited improvements in computational efficiency and acceleration. This motivates a finer-grained sparsification strategy that can be applied from earlier iterations and leverages reusable sparsity patterns, enabling further efficiency gains. In this work, we introduce PulseCol, a periodically refreshed column-sparse attention method for accelerating diffusion language models. PulseCol replaces coarse block-level sparsity with a finer-grained column-sparse structure, allowing important attention interactions to be retained more precisely while exposing greater sparsity. Built on this column-level formulation, PulseCol further identifies sparse patterns at the early denoising step and reuses them across subsequent iterations, refreshing them only at a small number of intermediate steps to track the evolution of sparse attention patterns during denoising. Experiments show that PulseCol achieves higher sparsity and greater practical speedup than prior sparse attention methods for dLLMs, while maintaining model quality. Enabled by optimized GPU kernels for column-sparse attention, PulseCol delivers up to 1.95$\times$ end-to-end speedup over FlashAttention across several context lengths.

### [155] [GraphRAG on Consumer Hardware: Benchmarking Local LLMs for Healthcare EHR Schema Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20815)
*Peter Fernandes,Ria Kanjilal*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究系统评估了在本地部署的开源大语言模型上使用GraphRAG进行电子健康记录（EHR）模式检索的可行性与性能。在单块8GB VRAM的消费级GPU上，基于Ollama部署Llama 3.1（8B）、Mistral（7B）、Qwen 2.5（7B）和Phi-4-mini（3.8B）四款模型，对比其索引效率、知识图谱构建、查询延迟、答案质量及幻觉情况。结果显示：Llama 3.1生成最丰富的知识图谱（1,172个实体），Qwen 2.5答案质量最佳（3.3/5），Phi-4-mini因结构化输出错误无法完成流程，Mistral出现重复性退化行为；模型参数量低于约7B时难以可靠生成有效结构化输出，导致流程失败；索引效率与答案质量在不同模型间解耦，且本地检索始终优于全局摘要，在延迟与事实准确性上表现更优，幻觉更少。研究证明GraphRAG可在消费级硬件上运行，但模型选择与检索策略对在受监管环境中的稳健部署至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在医疗领域，电子健康记录（EHR）数据复杂且受严格监管，依赖云端大语言模型存在成本高、延迟大、合规风险等问题。现有图结构检索增强生成（GraphRAG）方法在资源受限、隐私敏感场景下的可靠性尚不明确，亟需在本地部署环境下验证其可行性与性能边界。

Method: 采用微软GraphRAG框架，基于真实EHR文档构建知识图谱；在单块8GB VRAM消费级GPU上通过Ollama部署四款开源LLM（Llama 3.1、Mistral、Qwen 2.5、Phi-4-mini）；对比分析索引效率、知识图谱构建、查询延迟、答案质量与幻觉水平；分别测试全局与本地检索模式的表现，并评估模型规模对结构化输出能力的影响。

Result: Llama 3.1生成最多实体（1,172个），Qwen 2.5答案质量最高（3.3/5），Phi-4-mini因结构化输出失败无法完成流程，Mistral表现出重复性退化；模型参数低于约7B时难以生成有效结构化输出，导致流程中断；索引效率与答案质量无明显相关性；本地检索在延迟、事实准确性和幻觉控制方面均优于全局摘要。

Conclusion: GraphRAG可在消费级硬件上成功部署，但其性能高度依赖模型选择与检索策略设计。在受监管医疗环境中，应优先选用参数量不低于7B的模型，并采用本地检索机制以提升可靠性、降低幻觉风险。

Abstract: Graph-based Retrieval Augmented Generation (GraphRAG) extends retrieval-augmented generation to support structured reasoning over complex corpora, but its reliability under resource-constrained, privacy-sensitive deployments remains unclear. In healthcare, where Electronic Health Record (EHR) data is complex and strictly regulated, reliance on cloud-based large language models (LLMs) introduces challenges in cost, latency, and compliance. In this work, we present a systematic evaluation of GraphRAG for EHR schema retrieval using locally deployed open-source LLMs. We implement the Microsoft GraphRAG pipeline on real-world EHR schema documentation and benchmark four models, including Llama 3.1 (8B), Mistral (7B), Qwen 2.5 (7B), and Phi-4-mini (3.8B), each deployed via Ollama on a single consumer GPU (8 GB VRAM). We evaluate indexing efficiency, knowledge graph construction, query latency, answer quality, and hallucination under both global and local retrieval modes. Our results reveal substantial differences: Llama 3.1 produces the richest knowledge graph (1,172 entities), Qwen 2.5 achieves the best answer quality (3.3/5), Phi-4-mini fails to complete the pipeline due to structured-output errors, and Mistral exhibits degenerate repetition behavior. We further show that GraphRAG exhibits a practical capacity threshold, where models below approximately 7B parameters fail to reliably produce valid structured outputs and cannot complete the pipeline. In addition, indexing and answer quality are decoupled across models, and local retrieval consistently outperforms global summarization in both latency and factual grounding, with reduced hallucination. These findings demonstrate that GraphRAG is feasible on consumer hardware while highlighting the importance of model selection and retrieval design for robust deployment in regulated settings.

### [156] [MemGym: a Long-Horizon Memory Environment for LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20833)
*Wujiang Xu,Yu Wang,Kai Mei,Kaiqu Liang,Zhenting Wang,Mingyu Jin,Han Zhang,Shi-Xiong Zhang,Wenyue Hua,Sambit Sahu,Dimitris N. Metaxas*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出MemGym，一个针对智能体记忆能力的综合性基准测试框架，涵盖工具使用对话、深度研究搜索、编程和计算机操作等四种智能体场景，通过隔离记忆性能评估，消除推理、检索和工具使用能力的干扰，实现对记忆策略的公平比较。同时开发了可控制长度、可验证消融的合成数据流水线，并引入轻量级奖励模型MemRM以高效评估代码压缩质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有记忆基准主要关注多轮对话中个性化信息的保留，忽视了在长期智能体执行过程中动态记忆形成的重要性，导致记忆系统在真实智能体环境（如编程和网页导航）中表现不佳。因此需要一个更贴近实际应用的基准来评估和优化智能体的记忆能力。

Method: 构建MemGym基准，整合多个现有智能体环境与自研记忆驱动的流水线，设计五项评估任务，覆盖不同智能体行为模式；采用记忆隔离评分机制，分离记忆性能与其他能力；开发可控长度、可验证的合成数据生成流程；训练轻量级奖励模型MemRM（基于Qwen3-1.7B微调），用于快速评估代码压缩质量，替代耗时的Docker完整回放。

Result: MemGym成功实现了对智能体记忆能力的多场景、高精度、可隔离评估；合成流水线具备良好的可控性与可验证性；MemRM模型能够以极低开销准确预测代码压缩质量，显著提升评估效率。

Conclusion: MemGym为智能体记忆系统提供了全面、可信且高效的评估平台，有助于推动面向真实长周期任务的智能体记忆技术发展。

Abstract: Memory is a central capability for LLM agents operating across long-horizon tasks. Existing memory benchmarks predominantly evaluate retention of personalized information in multi-turn chat scenarios, overlooking the dynamic memory formation that occurs during extended agent execution. Consequently, the memory systems they produce transfer poorly to realistic agentic environments, such as coding and web navigation. We present MemGym, a benchmark for agentic memory that unifies existing agent gyms and in-house memory-grounded pipelines behind one memory-reasoning interface. MemGym spans five evaluation tracks grouped into four agentic regimes: tool-use dialogue (tau2-bench), multi-turn deep-research search (MEMGYM-DR), coding (SWE-Gym and MEMGYM-CODEQA), and computer use (WebArena-Infinity). MemGym reports memory-isolated scores that decouple memory performance from reasoning, retrieval, and tool-use ability, so memory strategies can be ranked without those confounders. Our synthetic pipelines for MEMGYM-CODEQA and MEMGYM-DR are length-controllable, ablation-verified at every stage, and tightly aligned with downstream scenarios. To make evaluation on coding environments academically tractable, we train MemRM, a lightweight reward model (Qwen3-1.7B fine-tuned with QLoRA) that scores compression quality as a fast scalar read in place of full Docker rollouts.

*Yaping Chai,Haoran Xie,Joe S. Qin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于认知评估理论的多任务学习框架，通过隐式情感检测和认知理由生成两个辅助任务，提升隐式情感分析性能。采用任务级混合专家模型（MoE），通过稀疏专家组合减少任务干扰，并在编码器-解码器架构中替换部分模块以实现灵活共享。实验表明该方法在隐式情感子集上优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 隐式情感分析因情感依赖于事件而非显式表达词而具有挑战性；现有模型仅依赖最终极性标签，难以充分挖掘上下文信息。因此需要更有效的机制来推理情感来源。

Method: 提出一种基于认知评估理论的多任务学习框架，结合隐式情感检测与认知理由生成作为辅助任务；采用任务级混合专家模型（TRMoE），利用任务条件路由选择稀疏专家组合，通过任务分离的路由目标促使各任务学习不同的专家选择模式。

Result: 实验结果显示，所提模型在隐式情感分析任务上显著优于现有方法，尤其在隐式情感子集上取得明显提升。

Conclusion: 该方法通过引入认知驱动的多任务学习与任务级混合专家结构，有效缓解了多任务训练中的任务干扰问题，提升了隐式情感分析的性能，具有较强的可扩展性和实用性。

Abstract: Implicit sentiment analysis is challenging because sentiment toward an aspect is often inferred from events rather than expressed through explicit opinion words. Existing models typically learn from the final polarity label, which provides limited guidance for reasoning about sentiment from the context. Motivated by cognitive appraisal theory, we propose an appraisal-aware multi-task learning (MTL) framework for implicit sentiment analysis that provides polarity prediction with two complementary auxiliary tasks: implicit sentiment detection and cognitive rationale generation. However, training several objectives with different targets and sharing a single backbone across tasks in MTL limits flexibility and can lead to task interference. To reduce interference among these related but distinct objectives, we adopt task-level mixture-of-experts models in which all tasks share a common set of experts, and task identity controls the sparse combination of these experts. Our method builds on an encoder-decoder architecture and replaces a subset of encoder and decoder blocks with these sparse mixtures. We use a task-conditioned router to select sparse expert mixtures for each task, and a task-separated routing objective to encourage different tasks to learn distinct expert-selection patterns. Experimental results show that our model outperforms recently proposed approaches, with strong gains on the implicit sentiment subset. Our code is available at https://github.com/yaping166/TRMoE-ISA.

### [161] [Memory Grafting: Scaling Language Model Pre-training via Offline Conditional Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20948)
*Runxi Cheng,Yuchen Guan,Yongxian Wei,Qianpu Sun,Qixiu Li,Sinan Du,Feng Xiong,Chun Yuan,Yan Lu,Yeyun Gong*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Memory Grafting是一种条件记忆扩展方法，利用冻结的预训练模型隐藏状态作为条件n-gram记忆，通过离线计算和精确后缀查找实现高效记忆检索，结合轻量级投影与门控机制及哈希回退机制，在不显著增加训练和推理开销的情况下有效提升语言模型容量。实验表明，该方法在多个规模设置下均优于MoE和原始Engram基线，尤其在2.8B和0.92B模型中显著提升基准得分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有条件记忆扩展方法（如Engram）需在预训练阶段从头学习大规模记忆表，成本高且效果有限。为降低内存扩展的训练与推理开销，亟需一种更高效、可复用的记忆构建方式。

Method: 提出Memory Grafting：使用预训练的‘嫁接模型’离线生成并存储频繁局部n-gram对应的最终词元隐藏表示作为记忆值；接收模型通过精确最长匹配后缀查找进行记忆检索，再经轻量级投影与门控适配；未命中时采用基于哈希的Engram回退机制以保证覆盖率。整个过程仅在离线阶段运行嫁接模型，且查找复杂度为期望O(1)，不随记忆库大小增长。

Result: 在相同接收模型架构和预训练预算下，Memory Grafting优于MoE和原始Engram基线。在2.8B规模下，平均基准得分从MoE的51.95、Engram的52.43提升至53.86；在0.92B规模下，所有嫁接模型变体均表现更优，其中Qwen3.5-35B-A3B取得最佳提升。

Conclusion: 预训练模型可作为外部隐状态记忆的可复用构建器，为突破仅依赖可训练参数的语言模型扩展瓶颈提供了实用路径，标志着向更大容量模型演进的重要一步。

Abstract: Scaling conditional memory offers a promising way to increase language-model capacity, but existing methods such as Engram learn large memory tables from scratch during pre-training, making memory scaling expensive and sometimes ineffective. We propose Memory Grafting, a conditional memory scaling method that utilizes frozen hidden states from a grafting model as conditional n-gram memory. Given frequent local n-grams, we run the grafting model offline, store final-token hidden representations as memory values, and let the recipient model retrieve them through exact longest-match suffix lookup. Retrieved memories are adapted by lightweight projections and gates, while a hash-based Engram fallback preserves coverage for unmatched contexts. Since the grafting model is only run offline and exact lookup has expected O(1) complexity with respect to memory-bank size, Memory Grafting expands external latent capacity with limited training and inference overhead. Experiments under matched recipient architectures and pre-training budgets show that Memory Grafting improves over both MoE and vanilla Engram baselines. In the 2.8B-scale setting, it improves the average benchmark score from 51.95 for MoE and 52.43 for vanilla Engram to 53.86. In the 0.92B-scale setting, all grafting-model variants improve over the baselines, with Qwen3.5-35B-A3B giving the strongest gains. These results suggest that pretrained models can serve as reusable constructors of external latent memory, providing a practical step toward scaling future language models beyond trainable parameters alone.

### [162] [Towards Context-Invariant Safety Alignment for Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20994)
*Yixu Wang,Yang Yao,Xin Wang,Yifeng Gao,Yan Teng,Xingjun Ma,Yingchun Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为锚定不变性正则化（AIR）的新方法，用于提升大语言模型在安全对齐中的鲁棒性。针对现有方法在面对不同表述但相同意图时表现不一致的问题，AIR通过将可验证的提示作为锚点，仅对开放式提示进行正则化，从而实现上下文无关的对齐。该方法可作为插件损失与分组偏好优化结合使用，在多个任务中显著提升了模型在分布内和分布外的一致性表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于偏好的后训练虽能对齐人类意图，但模型的安全行为仍易受提示表面形式影响，例如同一有害意图在不同表述下可能被拒绝或接受。为实现真正鲁棒的安全性，需确保模型行为依赖于意图而非表达方式，即具备上下文不变性。然而，由于训练信号可信度不一，传统对称正则化会损害可靠提示上的性能，无法有效提升开放提示下的鲁棒性。

Method: 提出锚定不变性正则化（AIR），利用可验证提示作为锚点，通过停止梯度的目标机制，仅对开放式提示进行正则化，使其性能向锚点看齐。该方法以辅助损失形式嵌入，与基于组别的偏好优化（如GRPO）结合，采用异质提示分组策略。

Result: 在安全、道德推理和数学任务上，AIR显著提升了上下文不变性，使分布内组准确率提升12.71%，分布外一致性提升33.49%，有效增强了模型对对抗性表述的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 通过引入锚定不变性正则化（AIR），模型能够更稳定地根据意图做出决策，而非受制于提示的表面形式，从而实现更鲁棒的安全对齐，为构建可信的大语言模型提供了新路径。

Abstract: Preference-based post-training aligns LLMs with human intent, yet safety behavior often remains brittle. A model may refuse a harmful request in a standard prompt but comply when the same intent is wrapped in adversarial wording. We suggest that robust safety requires context-invariant alignment, where behavior depends on the underlying intent rather than surface form. Enforcing invariance is difficult in alignment because not all training signals are equally trustworthy; for some prompt variants we can obtain verifiable feedback (e.g., multiple-choice), while for open-ended variants we typically rely on noisy, gameable reward proxies (e.g., learned judges). As a result, standard symmetric invariance regularizers can reduce cross-context discrepancies by lowering performance on reliable variants instead of improving open-ended robustness. To address this, we introduce Anchor Invariance Regularization (AIR), which treats verifiable prompts as anchors and uses a stop-gradient target to regularize only the open-ended variants toward the anchor performance. AIR is implemented as a plug-in auxiliary loss and combined with group-based preference optimization (e.g., GRPO) via heterogeneous prompt grouping. Across Safety, Moral Reasoning, and Math, AIR improves context invariance, boosting in-distribution group accuracy by 12.71% and out-of-distribution consistency by 33.49%, making safety constraints robust to adversarial framings.

</details>


### [163] [Single-Pass, Depth-Selective Reading for Multi-Aspect Sentiment Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20998)
*Yan Xia,Zhuangzhuang Pan,Amirrudin Kamsin,Chee Seng Chan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: DABS提出一种单次推理框架，通过一次编码构建可复用的深度有序基底，使每个方面查询共享表示以选择性读取相关标记和抽象层级，避免重复编码，显著降低多方面场景下的计算量（最高减少60%），同时保持竞争力性能，并在语言复杂情况（如否定、对比）中表现更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有ATSA模型在效率与表达能力间存在权衡：要么为每个方面重新编码句子，要么依赖静态深层表示，导致冗余计算和适应性不足。

Method: 提出DABS框架，仅对句子进行一次编码，生成深度有序的共享基底；各方面通过查询该基底，选择性读取相关上下文和抽象层级，实现轻量级、面向方面的读出机制。

Result: 在四个ATSA基准上验证，DABS在多方面设置下（M >= 2）将端到端计算量减少高达60%，同时保持良好性能；分析表明，自适应深度查询在处理否定、对比等语言复杂情形时尤为有效。

Conclusion: Transformer深度是可查询的高成本资源，通过共享编码与可变深度查询机制，DABS实现了高效且具表达力的ATSA建模，为多方面情感分析提供了新范式。

Abstract: Aspect-Term Sentiment Analysis (ATSA) in multi-aspect sentences faces a fundamental tradeoff between efficiency and expressiveness. Existing models either re-encode the sentence for each aspect or rely on static use of deep representations, leading to redundant computation and limited adaptivity. We argue that Transformer depth is a costly, queryable resource, and propose DABS, a single-pass inference framework that encodes each sentence once to construct a reusable, depth-ordered substrate. Each aspect then queries this shared representation to selectively read relevant tokens and abstraction levels, without re-encoding. This decouples shared sentence encoding from lightweight, aspect-conditioned readout. Experiments on four ATSA benchmarks show that DABS achieves competitive performance while reducing end-to-end computation by up to 60% in multi-aspect settings (M >= 2). Further analyses indicate that adaptive depth querying is most beneficial for linguistically complex cases such as negation and contrast. Code is publicly available at https://github.com/panzhzh/acl-dabs

### [164] [Beyond Text-to-SQL: An Agentic LLM System for Governed Enterprise Analytics APIs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21027)
