TL;DR: Analytic Agent is an LLM-based agentic system designed to help non-technical users interact with enterprise analytics APIs through natural language, ensuring security, compliance, and accurate execution of data queries. It addresses the limitations of traditional Text-to-SQL systems by incorporating governed API interactions and multi-step reasoning.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Non-technical users struggle with traditional business intelligence tools and Text-to-SQL systems in enterprise settings, where analytics rely on governed APIs rather than raw databases. Directing complex logic to LLMs poses reliability and compliance risks.

Method: Analytic Agent uses an LLM-based agentic framework that performs multi-step reasoning, validates user permissions, executes queries via governed APIs, and generates compliant visualizations.

Result: Evaluated on 90 real-world enterprise use cases, Analytic Agent successfully interprets user intents, ensures policy compliance, executes secure queries, and produces accurate visualizations.

Conclusion: Analytic Agent effectively bridges the gap between non-technical users and enterprise analytics by enabling safe, reliable, and compliant natural language access to governed data pipelines.

Abstract: Enterprise analytics aims to make organizational data accessible for decision-making, yet non-technical users still face barriers when using traditional business intelligence tools or Text-to-SQL systems. While recent Text-to-SQL approaches based on Large Language Models (LLMs) promise natural language access to structured data, they fall short in enterprise settings where analytics pipelines rely on governed APIs rather than raw databases. In practice, these APIs encapsulate complex business logic to ensure consistency, auditability, and security. However, delegating mathematical or aggregation logic to an LLM introduces reliability and compliance risks. To this end, we present Analytic Agent, an LLM-based agentic system that translates natural language intents into secure interactions with enterprise analytics APIs. Evaluated on 90 real enterprise use cases constructed by domain experts, it reliably interprets user goals, validates permissions, executes governed queries, and generates compliant visualizations through multi-step reasoning and policy-aware orchestration.

</details>


### [165] [APM: Evaluating Style Personalization in LLMs with Arbitrary Preference Mappings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21063)
*Philipp Spohn,Leander Girrbach,Zeynep Akata*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为任意偏好映射（APM）的基准测试，用于评估大语言模型在无参考响应情况下对用户隐性偏好的个性化能力。该方法通过随机化映射将用户属性与响应特征解耦，避免模型依赖刻板印象，迫使模型从对话历史中推断偏好。实验对比了检索增强、提示优化和路由三种个性化方法在Llama-3.1-8B和Qwen-3.5-27B上的表现，结果显示路由策略最可靠，检索增强仅在更强的基线模型上有效，而软提示优化未能显著超越非个性化基线。整体表明个性化仍具挑战性，但所提方法具备潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型响应常遵循默认风格，难以满足用户未明确表达的语气、冗长程度和正式程度等隐性偏好。传统评估方法因缺乏参考响应、偏好不可验证及评判标准混淆质量与个性化，导致无法准确衡量个性化效果。因此亟需一种能解耦用户属性与响应特征、避免模型利用刻板印象的公平评估机制。

Method: 提出任意偏好映射（APM）基准，通过一个隐藏且每轮重采样的随机映射矩阵 $\mathbf{C}$，将用户属性（如热情）与响应特性（如说服力）进行非语义关联。该设计确保模型无法依赖常识性联想，必须依据对话上下文推断用户偏好，从而实现更真实、无偏的个性化评估。在此基础上，对检索增强、提示优化和路由三种个性化方法进行适配并评估。

Result: 在Llama-3.1-8B和Qwen-3.5-27B上评估显示：路由方法表现最为稳定可靠；检索增强仅在更强的基线模型上带来提升；软提示优化未能显著优于非个性化基线。结果说明当前个性化技术仍面临挑战，但在合理设计下具备改进空间。

Conclusion: 尽管在真实场景中个性化依然困难，但通过引入无偏评估框架APM，本文验证了多种个性化方法的有效性与局限性。其中路由策略最具潜力，未来可结合更强模型与更精细的上下文建模进一步提升个性化能力。

Abstract: Typical LLM responses tend to follow a default style, even though users often have distinct preferences regarding tone, verbosity, and formality that they do not explicitly state in their prompts. Evaluating whether personalization methods can adapt to these implicit preferences is challenging, since users typically provide prompts rather than reference responses, style preferences are not factually verifiable, and reference-free LLM judges may conflate personalization with general response quality. To address these challenges, we introduce the Arbitrary Preference Mapping (APM) benchmark, which decouples user attributes (e.g. enthusiastic) from response principles (e.g. persuasive) via a hidden, randomized mapping $\mathbf{C}$ that maps user attributes to preferences about response traits. Because $\mathbf{C}$ carries no semantic content and is resampled across runs, models cannot exploit stereotypical associations and must infer preferences from conversation history. Using this unbiased evaluation methodology, we adapt retrieval-augmented, prompt-optimization, and routing personalization methods and evaluate them on Llama-3.1-8B and Qwen-3.5-27B. Our results show that routing is the most reliable approach, while RAG only improves with the stronger base LLM, and soft prompt optimization fails to improve significantly over a non-personalized baseline. Our extensive evaluation reveals that in this realistic setting, personalization remains challenging, but our adapted methods show promise.

</details>

*Abdullah Al Zubaer,Lorenz Wendlinger,Simon Alexander Nonn,Michael Granitzer,Jelena Mitrovic*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 系统评估27个专有及开源大型语言模型，采用渐进式提示策略，逐步引入样本答案和评分标准等任务相关信息，使用加权二次κ系数（QWK）衡量模型评分与专家评分的一致性，并比较单模型评分与模型集成的效果。

Conclusion: 大型语言模型在德国法律考试评分中具有应用潜力，尤其在公法领域。有效提示设计与模型选择是关键因素，模型集成可进一步提升评分可靠性，为实现规模化、即时化反馈提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Grading German legal exam solutions faces growing volumes and a shortage of qualified graders, delaying feedback and creating a bottleneck. Despite this practical relevance, literature lacks systematic studies on effective methods for grading legal exams. To address this gap, we investigate whether large language models (LLMs) can support the automated grading of German legal case solutions in criminal and public law, thereby enabling scalable feedback and student self-testing. In addition, our findings suggest that effective prompt design and model selection are necessary for reliable LLM-based grading of legal exams.

Conclusion: 虽然基于APE的错误高亮与建议未能提升生产率或质量，但其在用户体验方面表现更优，表明其具有潜在应用价值，未来可进一步优化以实现效率与质量的双重提升。

### [171] [Automated ICD Classification of Psychiatric Diagnoses: From Classical NLP to Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21154)
*Fernando Ortega,Raúl Lara-Cabrera,Jorge Dueñas-Lerín,Alejandro de la Torre-Luque,Mercé Salvador Robert,Enrique Baca-García*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精神健康已成为全球关注的重点，导致临床诊断编码工作量巨大。手动编码效率低且易出错，亟需自动化工具来提高诊断编码的准确性和效率。现有方法在处理精神科自由文本描述与标准诊断分类（如ICD）之间的映射时存在挑战，尤其在面对术语模糊性和标签分布不均的问题上表现不佳。因此，需要借助先进的NLP与ML技术实现高效、准确的自动化诊断分析。

Method: 本研究采用多种文本表示方法进行对比实验，包括经典频率特征模型（词袋模型BoW、TF-IDF），以及最新的大语言模型（LLMs）如e5_large、BioLORD和Llama-3-8B。所有模型均在包含145,513条西班牙语精神科临床描述的数据集上训练与评估。重点对不同模型在端到端微调下的表现进行比较，并通过$F1_{micro}$指标衡量其多标签分类性能。同时，针对长尾标签分布问题，探索模型对临床术语的适应能力。

Result: 基于Transformer的嵌入模型在各项指标上均显著优于传统频率模型，能够有效捕捉医疗文本中的复杂语义关系和细微差异。其中，经端到端微调后的e5_large模型取得最高性能，$F1_{micro}$达到0.866，是当前最优结果。该模型在处理罕见或长尾标签时表现出更强的泛化能力，且对精神科话语中常见的模糊表达具有较好鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 本研究表明，将大语言模型（LLM）适配至特定临床命名体系是实现精神科诊断自动化的重要路径。通过微调提升模型对医学术语的理解能力，可有效缓解标签分布不均和语义模糊带来的挑战。未来可通过扩展多语言支持和引入更多临床上下文信息进一步提升系统性能。

Abstract: Mental health has become a global priority, leading to a massive administrative burden in the coding of clinical diagnoses. This study proposes the automation of psychiatric diagnostic analysis by mapping free-text descriptions to the International Classification of Diseases (ICD) using Natural Language Processing (NLP) and Machine Learning (ML) techniques. Utilizing a specialized dataset of 145,513 Spanish psychiatric descriptions, various text representation paradigms were evaluated, ranging from classical frequency-based models (BoW, TF-IDF) to state-of-the-art Large Language Models (LLMs) such as e5\_large, BioLORD, and Llama-3-8B. Results indicate that transformer-based embeddings consistently outperform traditional methods by capturing implicit semantic cues and nuanced medical terminology. The e5\_large model, through end-to-end fine-tuning, achieved the highest performance with a $F1_{micro}$ score of 0.866. This research demonstrates that adapting LLMs to specific clinical nomenclature is essential for overcoming the challenges of ``long-tail'' label distributions and the inherent ambiguity of psychiatric discourse.

### [172] [Metaphors in Literary Post-Editing: Opening Pandora's Box?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21178)
*Aletta G. Dorst,Mayra O. Nas,Katinka Zeven*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了文学文本后编辑者对神经机器翻译（NMT）和大语言模型（LLM）翻译隐喻的反应与处理方式。结果显示，三分之一的隐喻在输出中被后编辑者修改，表明文学机器翻译在比喻语言处理上存在显著问题。后编辑者意识到翻译过于字面化，尤其针对多词表达；但有时难以判断修改方案是否合适。他们对机器翻译质量评价较低，并认为后编辑工作量更大、更费力，甚至超过从头翻译。这支持了先前研究的观点：后编辑限制了译者的创造力，削弱了其对文本的归属感。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究文学机器翻译中隐喻翻译的质量问题，以及后编辑者在处理此类问题时的反应与挑战，揭示后编辑对创作自由和文本所有权的影响。

Method: 通过分析后编辑者对NMT和LLM生成的文学文本中隐喻翻译的修改行为与反馈，评估翻译质量及后编辑负担。

Result: 约三分之一的隐喻被后编辑修改；后编辑者普遍认为翻译过于字面化，尤其在多词表达上；难以判断解决方案的可接受性；整体翻译质量评价低，后编辑工作量大于从头翻译。

Conclusion: 文学机器翻译在处理隐喻等修辞语言时表现不佳，后编辑过程不仅增加工作负担，还限制译者创造力并削弱其文本归属感，表明当前技术仍需改进。

Abstract: This paper investigates how post-editors of literary texts react and respond to the way metaphors have been translated by Neu ral Machine Translation (NMT) and Large Language Models (LLMs). The results show that one in three metaphors in the output were changed by the post-editors, demonstrating that the translation of fig urative language is indeed problematic in literary MT (LitMT). The responses indi cate that the post-editors were aware of overly literal translations, though mostly for multiword expressions. Moreover, at times they found it difficult to determine whether solutions were acceptable. They rated the overall quality of the MT out put as quite poor and stated that the post editing was more work and more effort than it would have been translating from scratch. This supports previous studies ar guing that post-editing constrains transla tors in their creativity and diminishes their sense of text ownership.

### [174] [LamPO: A Lambda Style Policy Optimization for Reasoning Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21235)
*Zhe Yuan,Yipeng Zhou,Jinghan Li,Xinyuan Chen,Bowen Deng,Zhiqian Chen,Liang Zhao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: LamPO提出一种基于配对分解优势的强化学习方法，通过保留生成响应间的细粒度关系信息，提升稀疏奖励下的信用分配效果。结合置信度加权与轻量级ROUGE-L辅助奖励，显著改善训练稳定性与样本效率，在数学与科学问答任务中优于GRPO及其他RLVR方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于组相对的目标（如GRPO）仅使用标量统计汇总群体表现，丢失了候选响应间的细粒度关系信息，导致在稀疏奖励场景下信用分配不准确，尤其当多个解法仅在推理质量上细微差异时。

Method: 提出LamPO，用配对分解优势替代标量组优势；通过序列对数概率差计算置信度权重，动态调节每对比较；保持PPO风格的无评论家和裁剪更新结构；引入ROUGE-L辅助奖励以缓解奖励稀疏性。

Result: 在AIME24、AIME25、MATH-500和GPQA-Diamond数据集上，使用Qwen3-1.7B、Qwen3-4B和Phi-4-mini模型，LamPO持续优于GRPO及近期RLVR方法，训练更稳定，样本效率更高。

Conclusion: LamPO通过保留响应间的细粒度关系并优化信用分配，在稀疏奖励场景下显著提升了语言模型的推理能力，为强化学习驱动的推理模型提供了一种高效且稳定的训练范式。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has become an effective paradigm for improving reasoning language models on tasks such as mathematics, coding, and scientific question answering. However, widely used group-relative objectives, such as GRPO, summarize each sampled group with scalar statistics and therefore discard fine-grained relational information among candidate responses. This weakens credit assignment under sparse outcome rewards, especially when multiple generated solutions differ only subtly in reasoning quality. We propose \textbf{LamPO}, a \textbf{Lambda-Style Policy Optimization} method that replaces scalar group advantages with a \emph{Pairwise Decomposed Advantage}. LamPO aggregates pairwise reward gaps within each response group and modulates each comparison by a confidence-aware weight computed from sequence log-probability differences, while retaining the critic-free and clipped-update structure of PPO-style optimization. When reference solutions are available, we further add a lightweight ROUGE-L-based dense auxiliary reward to reduce reward sparsity. Experiments on AIME24, AIME25, MATH-500, and GPQA-Diamond with Qwen3-1.7B, Qwen3-4B, and Phi-4-mini show that LamPO consistently improves over GRPO and recent RLVR variants, with more stable training dynamics and better sample efficiency.

To bridge this gap, we propose a risk-aware hybrid selective classification framework, evaluated on early Human Immunodeficiency Virus suspicion identification in Spanish clinical notes. Our dual-verification approach explicitly decouples aleatoric uncertainty through Mondrian conformal prediction and epistemic uncertainty using a Multi-Centroid Mahalanobis Distance veto. Empirical evaluations reveal that standard uncertainty metrics and baseline classifiers are structurally insufficient for safe medical triage, suffering severe coverage collapse when forced to operate under strict reliability constraints. In contrast, by demanding that clinical narratives pass both probabilistic and geometric safeguards, the proposed framework successfully isolates a highly trustworthy operational domain.

### [176] [Tracing the ongoing emergence of human-like reasoning in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21299)
*Paolo Morosi,Nikoleta Pantelidou,Fritz Günther,Elena Pagliarini,Evelina Leivada*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究通过跨语言实验比较了25个大型语言模型（LLMs）与人类在条件推理中的表现，发现人类能基于语用推理对条件句进行语义扩展，而大多数LLMs要么严格遵循逻辑真值表但忽略语用信息，要么固守单一解释，缺乏人类式的灵活推理。尽管模型在语义层面准确，但在捕捉人类特有的语用丰富性方面仍显不足。模型表现不受其是否开源、训练方式或架构类型的影响，表明语用推理仍是人工智能系统中尚未成熟的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究大型语言模型是否具备与人类相似的语用推理能力，特别是在处理条件句时能否超越字面意义进行语义扩展。

Method: 设计了一项与人群匹配的跨语言实验，评估25个LLMs和同等数量的人类在四种语言中对条件句的推理表现，对比其在逻辑与语用推理上的差异。

Result: 人类在不同语言中均表现出基于语用的推理能力；而LLMs行为多样：部分严格遵循真值表但忽略语用，部分则固定采用单一解释，偏离真值表但体现规则化处理，整体未能复制人类的灵活语用推理。

Conclusion: LLMs是准确的语义操作者，但未能捕捉人类推理中典型的语用丰富性。语用推理尚未成为人工智能系统的成熟能力，且其表现不依赖于模型的开放性、训练方式或架构类型。

Abstract: Humans effortlessly go beyond literal meanings: If you mow the lawn, I will give you fifty dollars, is typically understood as implying that the speaker will pay only if the lawn is mowed, whereas If you are hungry, there is pizza in the oven implies that pizza is available regardless of the hearers hunger. Large Language Models - LLMs - show human-like performance on many tasks, yet it remains unclear whether they reason like humans. To address this, we conducted a population-matching experiment assessing how twentyfive LLMs compute conditional inferences across four languages, compared to an equal number of humans per language. We find that humans enrich logical reasoning through pragmatic inferences across languages. Model behavior is more variable. Some LLMs perfectly follow the truth-table of conditionals but they ignore pragmatic inferences, while others deviate from the truth-table, adhering to a single interpretation across the board, thus reflecting accurate rule-based processing but not human-like reasoning. Overall, LLMs are accurate semantic operators, but fail to capture the pragmatic enrichments characteristic of human reasoning. Crucially, LLM accuracy is neither predicted nor boosted by open vs. closed status, training orientation, or architecture type, suggesting that pragmatic reasoning is still an emerging ability in the cognitive toolkit of artificial systems.

### [177] [TextReg: Mitigating Prompt Distributional Overfitting via Regularized Text-Space Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21318)
*Lucheng Fu,Ye Yu,Yiyang Wang,Yiqiao Jin,Haibo Jin,B. Aditya Prakash,Haohan Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文研究了大语言模型（LLMs）在提示优化过程中出现的分布外泛化能力差的问题，指出其根源在于离散文本空间优化中缺乏表示控制，导致提示分布过拟合。为此，作者提出了TextReg框架，通过正则化文本梯度实现软惩罚目标，结合双重证据梯度净化、语义编辑正则化和正则化引导的提示更新，有效提升提示的泛化能力。在多个推理基准测试中，TextReg显著优于现有方法，出域泛化性能提升最高达+16.5%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的提示优化方法在迭代生成反馈时，导致提示变长、引入过多特定样本规则，从而降低泛化能力，表现出分布外过拟合现象，亟需一种能控制提示表示复杂度并提升泛化性的优化机制。

Method: 提出TextReg正则化框架，包含双重证据梯度净化、语义编辑正则化与正则化引导的提示更新，通过正则化文本梯度实现软惩罚，以抑制提示表示的过度复杂化。

Result: 在多个推理基准上，TextReg显著提升提示的出域泛化能力，相比TextGrad最高提升11.8%，相比REVOLVE最高提升16.5%。

Conclusion: 提示分布过拟合源于离散文本空间优化中表示控制不足，而TextReg通过正则化机制有效缓解了这一问题，显著提升了大语言模型在未知分布上的泛化性能。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are highly sensitive to the prompts used to specify task objectives and behavioral constraints. Many recent prompt optimization methods iteratively rewrite prompts using LLM-generated feedback, but the resulting prompts often become longer, accumulate narrow sample-specific rules, and generalize poorly beyond the training distribution. We study this failure mode as prompt distributional overfitting and argue that it reflects a lack of representation control in discrete text-space optimization. We formalize this view through representational inefficiency, a dual-factor measure that decomposes prompt inefficiency into capacity cost and scope narrowness, attributing distributional prompt overfitting to their coupled growth during optimization. We propose TextReg, a regularization framework that realizes a soft-penalty objective through regularized textual gradients, combining Dual-Evidence Gradient Purification, Semantic Edit Regularization, and Regularization-Guided Prompt Update. Across multiple reasoning benchmarks, TextReg substantially improves out-of-distribution (OOD) generalization, with accuracy gains of up to +11.8% over TextGrad and +16.5% over REVOLVE.

### [178] [SymbolicLight V1: Spike-Gated Dual-Path Language Modeling with High Activation Sparsity and Sub-Billion-Scale Pre-Training Evidence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21333)
*Ting Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SymbolicLight V1 是一种新型脉冲语言模型，通过结合二进制漏电积分与放电（LIF）脉冲动力学和连续残差流，实现了高激活稀疏性（>89%）与Transformer级别的语言质量。其双路径稀疏TCAM模块用指数衰减长程记忆路径和脉冲门控局部注意力路径替代传统密集自注意力，提升长程依赖建模能力与短程精度。在30亿词的中英双语语料上从零训练的1.94亿参数模型，在独立四次运行中达到8.88-8.93的验证困惑度（PPL），比GPT-2 201M仅低7.7%，优于GPT-2 124M。组件消融实验表明，脉冲门控局部注意力是性能关键，且使用确定性top-k掩码替代LIF动态会带来更大性能下降，说明时间积分机制对性能至关重要。0.8B参数规模扩展实验验证了可扩展性与稀疏性保持，但当前仍依赖密集硬件推理，速度慢于GPT-2，未来在神经形态硬件上的部署被视为潜力方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有原生训练的脉冲语言模型难以同时实现Transformer级别的语言质量、稳定多领域预训练以及高激活稀疏性。本文旨在设计一种新型脉冲语言模型，以突破上述限制，实现高性能与高稀疏性的统一。

Method: 提出SymbolicLight V1模型，采用二进制漏电积分与放电（LIF）脉冲动力学与连续残差流相结合的架构；引入双路径稀疏TCAM模块，包含指数衰减长程记忆路径与脉冲门控局部注意力路径；使用动态上下文条件解码头与双语分词器。模型从零开始在中英双语语料上训练，并通过控制训练预算进行组件消融分析。

Result: 194M参数模型在30亿词语料上训练后，达到8.88-8.93的验证困惑度（PPL），激活稀疏性超过89%；相比GPT-2 201M仅落后7.7%，优于GPT-2 124M；组件消融显示脉冲门控局部注意力贡献最大，而替换为确定性top-k掩码导致更严重性能下降，说明时间积分而非单纯稀疏性驱动性能；0.8B参数扩展实验验证了模型可扩展性与稀疏性保持；当前推理仍依赖密集硬件，速度低于GPT-2，但神经形态部署具有潜力。

Conclusion: SymbolicLight V1展示了脉冲语言模型在保持高稀疏性的同时，能够实现接近Transformer的语言质量与稳定性。其核心在于脉冲门控注意力与时间积分机制的协同作用。尽管当前硬件效率受限，但该模型为未来在神经形态芯片上实现高效、节能的自然语言处理系统提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Natively trained spiking language models struggle to combine Transformer-like language quality, stable multi-domain pre-training, and high activation sparsity. We present SymbolicLight V1, a spike-gated dual-path language model that combines binary Leaky Integrate-and-Fire spike dynamics with a continuous residual stream. Its Dual-Path SparseTCAM module replaces dense self-attention with an exponential-decay aggregation path for long-range memory and a spike-gated local attention path for short-range precision, complemented by a dynamic context-conditioned decoding head and a bilingual tokenizer.
  A 194M-parameter SymbolicLight V1 model trained from scratch on a 3B-token Chinese-English corpus reaches held-out validation PPL 8.88-8.93 across four independent runs at >89% per-element activation sparsity. It trails GPT-2 201M by 7.7% in PPL while surpassing GPT-2 124M under the reported comparison. Component ablations at matched 0.5B-token training budgets show that the spike-gated local attention path is the largest contributor, and that replacing LIF dynamics with a deterministic top-k mask at matched sparsity causes a larger degradation, indicating that temporal integration rather than sparsity alone drives performance. We also report a 0.8B-parameter scale-up run trained on 48.8B tokens as evidence of optimization and sparsity preservation, not as a primary quality comparison. Current dense-hardware inference is slower than GPT-2, so neuromorphic deployment is presented as a future sparsity-driven opportunity rather than an achieved hardware speedup.

### [179] [Text Analytics Evaluation Framework: A Case Study on LLMs and Social Media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21338)
*Yuefeng Shi,Nedjma Ousidhoum,Jose Camacho-Collados*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文通过构建一个包含470个手动设计问题的基于问题的评估框架，系统评估了大语言模型（LLMs）在处理长序列非结构化文本（如社交媒体帖子）时的表现。研究发现，随着输入规模增大和任务复杂度提升，尤其是涉及多标签或目标依赖场景时，LLM性能显著下降；当输入超过500条数据时，尤其在数值类任务中，性能急剧恶化，暴露出当前LLMs在大规模文本量化分析方面的架构瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型虽在多种NLP任务中表现出色，但在实际数据处理场景中，特别是在处理大量非结构化文本（如社交媒体内容）时仍存在明显能力不足，亟需系统性评估其在真实复杂环境中的表现。

Method: 提出一种基于问题的评估框架，涵盖470个精心设计的问题，覆盖情感分析、仇恨言论检测、情绪识别等任务，并在多个Twitter数据集上测试不同规模与复杂度下的模型表现。

Result: LLM性能受输入规模和数据复杂度影响显著，在多标签或目标依赖任务中表现下降明显；随着任务复杂度上升（从存在判断到比较、计数、计算），性能逐步降低；当输入超过500条时，特别是开放权重模型，在数值任务上出现严重性能退化。

Conclusion: 当前大语言模型在处理大规模文本集合进行严谨定量分析方面存在关键架构缺陷，亟需改进以适应真实世界复杂的数据分析需求。

Abstract: LLMs have demonstrated exceptional proficiency in a wide range of NLP tasks. However, a notable gap remains in practical data analysis scenarios, particularly when LLMs are required to process long sequences of unstructured documents, such as news feeds or, as specifically addressed in this paper, social media posts. To empirically assess the effectiveness of LLMs in this setting, we introduce a question-based evaluation framework comprising 470 manually curated questions designed to evaluate LLMs' semantic understanding and reasoning abilities over aggregated text data. We apply our benchmark on diverse Twitter datasets covering various NLP tasks, including sentiment analysis, hate speech detection, and emotion recognition. Our results reveal that the performance depends heavily on input scale and the complexity of the data sources, declining noticeably in multi-label or target-dependent scenarios. In addition, as task complexity increases, performance drops progressively from basic semantic existence identification to more demanding operations such as comparison, counting, and calculation. Furthermore, as the input size grows beyond 500 instances, we identify a common limitation across LLMs, particularly Open-weights models: performance degrades substantially, especially on numerical tasks. These findings highlight critical architectural bottlenecks in current LLMs for performing rigorous quantitative analysis over large text collections.

*Abdullah Al Nomaan Nafi,Fnu Suya,Swarup Bhunia,Prabuddha Chakraborty*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: LASH 是一种黑盒框架，通过自适应组合多个基础攻击的输出作为种子提示，以提升对大型语言模型的越狱攻击成功率。它在 JailbreakBench 测试中表现出色，平均成功率达 84.5%（关键词评估）和 74.5%（两阶段评估），优于五个先进基线方法，且仅需 30 次平均目标查询。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动化越狱方法多局限于单一攻击类型，缺乏通用性；不同方法在不同模型和危害类别上表现各异，表明存在互补性，可通过动态组合提升整体效果。

Method: LASH 将多种攻击生成的提示作为种子池，通过遗传优化器搜索最优种子子集与混合权重，利用合成模块生成候选提示，并结合关键词拒绝检测与 LLM 判官评分的两阶段评估函数进行反馈优化。

Result: 在六个目标模型上，LASH 在 JailbreakBench 上实现 84.5% 的平均攻击成功率（关键词评估）和 74.5%（两阶段评估），显著优于基线方法，且在三种防御机制下仍具竞争力，诱导出更具攻击性的内部表示。

Conclusion: 自适应组合异构越狱策略是黑盒红队测试中极具潜力的方向，能有效突破单一攻击方法的局限性。

Abstract: Jailbreak attacks expose a persistent gap between the intended safety behavior of aligned large language models and their behavior under adversarial prompting. Existing automated methods are increasingly effective but each commits to a single attack family (e.g., one refinement loop, one tree search, one mutation space, or one strategy library) and no single family dominates: the best-performing method shifts across target models and harm categories, suggesting complementary strengths that per-prompt composition could exploit. We introduce LASH (LLM Adaptive Semantic Hybridization), a black-box framework that treats outputs from multiple base attacks as reusable seed prompts and adaptively composes them for each target request. Given a seed pool, LASH searches over seed subsets and softmax-normalized mixture weights; a composition module synthesizes a single candidate prompt, and a derivative-free genetic optimizer updates the weights using black-box target feedback and a two-stage fitness function combining keyword-based refusal detection with LLM-judge scoring. On JailbreakBench, which contains 100 harmful prompts across 10 categories, we evaluate LASH on six common target models. LASH achieves an average attack success rate of 84.5% under keyword-based evaluation and 74.5% under two-stage evaluation, where responses are first filtered for refusals and then scored by an LLM judge for whether they substantively fulfill the original harmful request. LASH outperforms five state-of-the-art baselines on both metrics with only 30 mean target queries. LASH also remains competitive under three defense mechanisms and induces more success-like internal representations. These results suggest that adaptive composition across heterogeneous jailbreak strategies is a promising direction for black-box red-teaming.

</details>


### [181] ["I didn't Make the Micro Decisions": Measuring, Inducing, and Exposing Goal-Level AI Contributions in Collaboration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21363)
*Eunsu Kim,Jessica R. Mindel,Kyungjin Kim,Sherry Tongshuang Wu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为CoTrace的目标级归因框架，用于分析人类与AI在协作过程中目标的共同构建过程。该框架将显式目标分解为可验证的需求，并追踪对话轮次中模型的直接贡献和间接影响。通过对638个真实协作日志的应用发现，尽管模型仅占目标构建贡献的11-26%，但在引入具体、低层级需求方面贡献显著，并存在多种间接影响。控制模拟实验表明，交互设计显著影响模型的目标构建行为。用户研究表明，展示目标级分析后，用户对自身贡献的感知平均提升近2分（5分制），揭示了用户对自身AI辅助工作的认知存在系统性偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型在帮助用户形成、调整和扩展目标中的作用日益增强，准确归因人类与AI在协作中的贡献变得至关重要。然而，现有方法多聚焦于最终成果，忽略了目标本身在对话中被共同塑造的过程，因此需要一种能够捕捉目标演化过程的归因机制。

Method: 提出CoTrace框架，将目标分解为可验证的子需求，通过分析对话历史中的每一轮交互，识别模型的直接贡献（如生成具体需求）和间接影响（如引导方向、启发思路），实现对目标构建过程的细粒度追踪与归因。

Result: 在638个真实协作日志上的实证分析显示，模型在目标构建中占比仅11-26%，但其在提出具体、低层级需求方面贡献突出，并存在多种间接影响；控制实验表明交互设计显著改变模型行为；用户研究发现，展示目标级分析可使用户对自身贡献的感知提升近2分，说明存在系统性认知偏差。

Conclusion: CoTrace框架有效揭示了人类与AI在目标构建过程中的复杂互动关系，强调了对协作过程进行细粒度归因的重要性。结果表明，用户普遍低估自身在目标形成中的作用，而高估模型的主导地位，提示需改进人机协作的认知工具与界面设计。

Abstract: As large language models (LLMs) increasingly shape how users form, refine, and extend their goals, attributing contributions in human-AI collaboration becomes critical for users calibrating their own reliance and for evaluators assessing AI-assisted work. Yet existing methods focus on final artifacts, missing the process through which goals themselves are jointly shaped. We introduce a goal-level attribution framework, CoTrace, that decomposes explicit goals into verifiable requirements and traces both direct contributions and indirect influences across dialogue turns. Applying CoTrace to 638 real-world collaboration logs, we find that while models account for only 11-26% of goal-shaping contribution, they contribute substantially more on introducing lower-level concrete requirements, and make various kinds of indirect contributions. Through controlled simulations, we show that interaction design choices significantly affect model goal-shaping behavior. In a user study, exposing participants to goal-level analyses shifts their perceived contributions by nearly 2 points on a 5-point scale, revealing systematic miscalibration in how users understand their own AI-assisted work.

</details>

Result: 传统系统仍保持领先，但基于大语言模型的方法表现出显著潜力，尤其在处理长距离共指方面。

Abstract: This paper describes the fifth edition of the Shared Task on Multilingual Coreference Resolution, held in conjunction with the CODI-CRAC 2026 workshop. Building on previous iterations, the task required participants to develop systems capable of mention identification and identity-based coreference clustering.
  The 2026 edition specifically emphasizes long-range entities, defined as coreferential chains spanning significant distances, across many words and sentences.
  The task expanded its linguistic scope by incorporating five new datasets and two additional languages. These additions leverage version 1.4 of CorefUD, a harmonized multilingual collection comprising 27 datasets in 19 languages.
  In total, ten systems participated, including four LLM-based approaches (three fine-tuned models and one few-shot approach). While traditional systems still maintained their lead, LLMs demonstrated significant potential, suggesting they may soon challenge established approaches in future editions.

### [183] [Post-Hoc Understanding of Metaphor Processing in Decoder-Only Language Models via Conditional Scale Entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21391)
*Lawhori Chakrabarti,Jennifer Johnson-Leung,Bert Baumgaertner,Aleksandar Vakanski,Min Xian,Boyu Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为条件尺度熵（CSE）的新方法，用于衡量Transformer模型在不同层位置上跨频率尺度的计算广度。研究发现，隐喻性词汇在连续层位置上表现出显著更高的频谱宽度，这一现象在多个Decoder-only架构中一致存在，且不受更新幅度影响。该效应在多种模型（从124M到20B参数）中均成立，并通过了聚类置换校正和独立语料验证，排除了语义复杂度等干扰因素。结果表明，多尺度协调是隐喻处理的稳定特征，而CSE为分析Transformer跨深度结构提供了有力工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解Transformer模型在处理隐喻时如何在不同层间组织重新解释过程，是机制可解释性中的一个开放问题。现有方法难以分离更新结构与强度，因此需要一种能捕捉跨尺度计算模式的新指标。

Method: 提出条件尺度熵（CSE），基于小波变换量化模型在各层位置上的频率尺度参与广度；通过两个定理证明其对更新幅度的不变性，从而隔离结构模式；在多个Decoder-only模型上对比隐喻与字面词的CSE值，并进行置换检验、控制变量分析与独立数据验证。

Result: 隐喻性词语在连续层位置上产生显著更高的CSE值，该现象在不同规模模型中一致出现，且不依赖于更新强度或语义复杂度；多尺度协调成为隐喻处理的稳定特征；CSE被证实为刻画变压器跨深度结构的有效工具。

Conclusion: 多尺度协调是隐喻语言处理在Decoder-only架构中的稳定特征；条件尺度熵（CSE）是一种有效的机制可解释性工具，可用于揭示模型内部跨深度的结构动态。

Abstract: Metaphor requires a language model to resolve a token whose contextual meaning diverges from its basic literal sense. Understanding how transformer models organize this reinterpretation across depth remains an open problem in mechanistic interpretability. We introduce conditional scale entropy (CSE), a wavelet-derived measure of how broadly transformer computation engages across frequency scales at each layer position. Two theorems establish that CSE is invariant to update magnitude, isolating the structural pattern of updates from their intensity. Using CSE, we find that metaphorical tokens produce significantly higher spectral breadth than literal tokens at contiguous layer positions on every decoder-only architecture tested, from 124M to 20B parameters (GPT-2 family, LLaMA-2 7B, GPT-oss 20B). The effect survives cluster-based permutation correction, recurs in the early-to-mid relative depth range across models, and converges with an independent analysis of 200 naturalistic VUA pairs. Specificity controls further show that the effect is not explained by semantic complexity or by matched propositional content. These results identify multi-scale coordination as a consistent signature of metaphorical language processing in the decoder-only architectures examined, and establish CSE as a principled tool for characterizing cross-depth structure in transformers.

</details>


### [184] [Leveraging LLMs for Grammar Adaptation: A Study on Metamodel-Grammar Co-Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21465)
*Weixing Zhang,Bowen Jiang,Rahul Sharma,Regina Hebig,Daniel Strüber*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于大语言模型（LLM）的自动语法适应方法，通过学习历史版本中的语法变更来应对元模型演进带来的语法一致性问题。在六个真实世界的Xtext领域特定语言上评估，使用四个DSL作为训练集、两个作为测试集，并对QVTo进行纵向案例研究。结果表明，所有三个LLM在测试集上均达到100%的规则级适应一致性和输出相似性，远超规则方法（如DOT为84.21%，Xcore为62.50%）。在QVTo案例中，LLM方法无需人工编辑即可跨三次演化步骤复用适应策略，而规则方法需手动调整两次。然而，在大规模语法（如EAST-ADL，297条规则）场景下，LLM的一致性低于90%。该研究展示了LLM在复杂语法场景中的优势，也揭示了其在大规模语法上的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 元模型演化导致语法需要频繁更新，传统手工修改效率低；现有规则方法虽部分自动化但难以应对复杂场景，亟需更高效、智能的适应机制。

Method: 提出一种基于大语言模型的方法，利用历史版本中的语法变更数据进行学习，生成适用于新版本语法的适应规则。通过设计提示策略（prompting strategies），结合多个大模型（Claude Sonnet 4.5、ChatGPT 5.1、Gemini 3）实现自动语法适应。

Result: 在测试集上，所有三款LLM均实现100%的规则级适应一致性和输出相似性，显著优于规则方法（最高仅84.21%）；在QVTo纵向研究中，LLM成功跨演化步骤复用适应策略，无需人工干预；但在大规模语法（如EAST-ADL）中，适应一致性低于90%，表现出性能下降。

Conclusion: 基于大语言模型的语法适应方法在处理复杂语法场景中展现出显著优势，尤其在减少人工干预和提升自动化程度方面表现优异；然而，其在大规模语法适应任务中仍面临挑战，需进一步优化以提升可扩展性与稳定性。

Abstract: In model-driven engineering, metamodel evolution leads to the need to adapt corresponding grammars to maintain consistency, which typically requires tedious manual work. Existing rule-based methods can achieve partial automation but have limitations when handling complex grammar scenarios. This paper proposes a Large Language Model-based approach that automatically applies adaptations to new grammars after evolution by learning grammar adaptations from previous versions. We evaluated this approach on six real-world Xtext domain-specific languages, using four DSLs as a training set to develop prompting strategies, two DSLs as a test set for validation, and conducting a longitudinal case study on QVTo. The evaluation used three Large Language Models (Claude Sonnet 4.5, ChatGPT 5.1, Gemini 3) and measured grammar adaptation quality from three dimensions: grammar rule-level adaptation consistency, output similarity, and metamodel conformance. Results show that on the test set, all three LLMs achieved 100% adaptation consistency and output similarity, while the rule-based approach achieved only 84.21% on DOT and 62.50% on Xcore. In the QVTo longitudinal study, the LLM-based approach successfully reused learned adaptations across all three evolution steps without manual grammar editing, while the rule-based approach required manual adjustments in two of three transitions. However, on large-scale grammars (EAST-ADL, 297 rules), LLMs' adaptation consistency was far below 90%. This study demonstrates the advantages of LLM-based approaches in handling complex grammar scenarios, while revealing their limitations in large-scale grammar adaptation.

</details>

### [185] [GraphDiffMed: Knowledge-Constrained Differential Attention with Pharmacological Graph Priors for Medication Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20188)
*Krati Saxena,Tomohiro Shibata*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: GraphDiffMed 是一种基于双尺度微分注意力机制的知识约束药物推荐框架，通过在访视内和访视间层面应用微分注意力来过滤噪声信号，并结合药理学约束进行学习，有效提升了药物推荐的质量与安全性，在MIMIC-III数据集上表现优于现有基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从电子健康记录中推荐安全有效的药物组合是临床人工智能中的核心挑战，因患者病程长、数据嘈杂且临床异质性强，现有方法难以同时兼顾时间建模与药理知识整合，且对噪声敏感。

Method: 提出GraphDiffMed框架，采用双尺度微分注意力（Differential Attention v2）分别处理单次就诊内部和跨就诊之间的时序信息，结合药理学约束（如药物-药物相互作用）进行联合学习，以增强模型对噪声的鲁棒性并提升推荐可靠性。

Result: 在MIMIC-III数据集上的实验表明，GraphDiffMed在推荐质量与排序性能上均优于强基线模型，同时展现出更优的安全性平衡；消融实验显示，仅使用人口统计学辅助特征即可达到最佳性能。

Conclusion: 将噪声感知注意力与药理学约束相结合，可显著提升药物推荐的可靠性与临床意义，为智能临床决策提供新路径。

Abstract: Recommending safe and effective medication combinations from electronic health records (EHRs) is a core clinical AI problem, yet it remains difficult because patient trajectories are long, noisy, and clinically heterogeneous. Existing methods typically excel at either temporal modeling across visits or pharmacological knowledge integration (e.g., drug-drug interactions, DDIs), but rarely achieve both while robustly suppressing noise. We present GraphDiffMed, a knowledge-constrained medication recommendation framework built on dual-scale Differential Attention v2. Differential attention is applied at both intra-visit and inter-visit levels to filter spurious signals within encounters and across longitudinal history, while pharmacological constraints are incorporated during learning. Experiments on MIMIC-III and ablation studies show that this design consistently improves recommendation quality and ranking over strong baselines while achieving a more favorable safety performance balance. We further find that the strongest-performing configuration uses only demographic auxiliary features under our experimental setting. Overall, GraphDiffMed demonstrates that combining noise-aware attention with pharmacological constraints yields more reliable and clinically meaningful medication recommendation. We open-source our code at https://github.com/saxenakrati09/GraphDiffMed.

### [186] [TabPFN-MT: A Natively Multitask In-Context Learner for Tabular Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20234)
*Cormac Cureton,Narges Armanfard*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TabPFN-MT 是一种针对小到中等规模表格数据的多任务上下文学习模型，通过扩展的 y-编码器和共享解码头实现多目标同时预测，显著提升推理效率（从 O(T) 降至 O(1)），在 344 个数据集上达到新的 SOTA 性能，尤其在多任务场景下表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 Prior-Data Fitted networks (PFNs) 仅支持单任务推理，多次前向传播导致计算成本高且无法共享任务间信息；为解决此问题，需设计能高效处理多目标预测的模型，尤其适用于小样本表格数据场景。

Method: 提出 TabPFN-MT，基于扩展的多目标合成先验进行训练，采用增强的 y-编码器与共享解码头结构，利用上下文学习而非梯度更新，实现多任务并行推理。

Result: 在 344 个数据集上的评估显示，TabPFN-MT 在小至中等规模数据下达成新 SOTA；多任务场景下平均准确率排名达 4.89，优于所有对比模型；推理复杂度由 O(T) 降为 O(1)，大幅提高效率。

Conclusion: TabPFN-MT 成功实现了高效、高性能的多任务表格上下文学习，在保持低计算开销的同时显著提升多目标预测能力，是小样本表格数据建模的新标杆。

Abstract: Prior-Data Fitted networks (PFNs) have been very successful in tabular contexts, handling prediction tasks in context. However, they are designed for single-task inference, meaning that predicting several target values within a context requires repeated forward calls and precludes inter-task information sharing. We propose TabPFN-MT, which is trained on an expanded multi-target synthetic prior to capture inter-task dependencies in context. This model uses an expanded $y$-encoder and a shared decoder head to enable multitask in-context learning and simultaneous inference. The model is uniquely specialized for small-to-medium datasets by relying on in-context learning rather than traditional gradient-based training. Within this regime (averaging fewer than 1,000 samples), extensive evaluations across 344 datasets demonstrate that TabPFN-MT establishes a new state-of-the-art for deep tabular multitask learning. Furthermore, despite the inherent compute asymmetry of joint optimization, our model remains highly competitive with the latest state-of-the-art single-task ensembles. Notably, on multitask datasets it achieves an overall Accuracy rank of 4.89, the highest average rank among all models tested. Crucially, TabPFN-MT delivers this highly competitive performance while reducing the inference cost for $T$ tasks from $O(T)$ to $O(1)$ forward passes, offering a massive computational efficiency improvement for multi-target tabular applications.

### [187] [Provably Learning Diffusion Models under the Manifold Hypothesis: Collapse and Refine](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20235)
*Wei Huang,Andi Han,Mingyuan Bai,Huanjian Zhou,Qixin Zhang,Taiji Suzuki,Kenji Fukumizu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种名为Score-induced Latent Diffusion (SiLD)的两阶段框架，通过单一去噪得分匹配目标实现流形学习与密度估计，克服了传统基于VAE的潜在扩散模型中启发式KL正则化的不足。理论分析揭示了在小噪声尺度下得分函数的奇异性导致维度快速坍缩至数据流形投影，在中等噪声尺度下训练则优化流形上的内在密度。实验表明，SiLD在生成质量和重建性能上优于或匹配现有方法，并且样本复杂度依赖于内在维度而非环境维度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前扩散模型虽能生成高质量高维数据，但其训练如何高效学习得分函数、避免在低维流形支持的数据上遭遇维度灾难，尚缺乏理论解释。

Method: 提出Score-induced Latent Diffusion (SiLD)框架，利用得分函数的几何特性，通过一个统一的去噪得分匹配目标实现两阶段过程：先通过小噪声下的得分奇异性驱动维度坍缩至数据流形，再在中等噪声下精细估计流形上的密度分布。

Result: 理论证明样本复杂度仅依赖于数据的内在维度；实验在Stacked MNIST、CelebA变体和分子生成任务中显示，SiLD在生成质量与重建性能上均优于或等同于基于VAE的潜变量扩散模型。

Conclusion: SiLD通过得分函数的内在几何机制，实现了高效且理论可解释的流形学习与密度估计，为扩散模型在低维流形数据上的高效训练提供了新范式。

Abstract: Diffusion models generate high-dimensional data with remarkable quality, yet how their training efficiently learns the score function, bypassing the curse of dimensionality when data is supported on low-dimensional manifolds, remains theoretically unexplained. We identify a collapse-and-refine mechanism driven by the geometry of the score function itself: at small noise scales, the diverging singularity of the score drives a rapid dimensional collapse of the induced denoising map onto the data manifold projection; at moderate noise scales, training refines the intrinsic density on the learned manifold. We instantiate this principle as Score-induced Latent Diffusion (SiLD), a two-stage framework in which both manifold learning and density estimation emerge from a single denoising score matching objective, replacing the heuristic KL regularization of VAE-based latent diffusion models. We prove that the resulting sample complexity depends on the intrinsic dimension rather than the ambient dimension. Experiments on Stacked MNIST, CelebA variants, and molecular generation benchmarks show that SiLD matches or outperforms VAE-based LDMs in generation quality and consistently improves reconstruction, validating our theoretical predictions.

</details>

Abstract: Battery health diagnostics today rely overwhelmingly on electrochemical signals measured at the cell terminals. We define three primary benchmark tasks: SOH regression, second-life classification, and anomaly detection, plus an auxiliary anomaly-subtype classification task. The dataset is released on Zenodo under CC-BY-4.0, and the bridge code and benchmark suite are released under Apache-2.0. This work provides a public benchmark for magnetic-sensing battery diagnostics while paired magnetic-electrochemical measurements remain scarce.

### [189] [Geometry-Lite: Interpretable Safety Probing via Layer-Wise Margin Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20241)
*Woo Seob Sim,Yu Rang Park*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Geometry-Lite 是一种紧凑的提示级探测器，通过分析多层隐藏状态中的安全信号几何结构，揭示了安全证据在不同层间的分布与稳定性。研究发现，安全判断主要依赖于持久的边界位置几何特征（如最终边缘值和不安全侧的层占用），而非层间动态变化。尽管层间漂移和结构摘要对整体性能贡献有限，但在低误报率阈值下可微调召回率。此外，在基准迁移时，基于类条件均值的几何结构比优化线性边界更具鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有提示级安全探测器虽具备良好的平均检测性能，但缺乏对安全信号在多层中如何形成、哪些几何特性支持低误报决策、以及在不同数据分布下是否稳定的理解。因此需要一种能分解并可视化多层安全信号几何特性的方法。

Method: 提出 Geometry-Lite 探测框架，将每层最后一个提示令牌的表示映射到三种读出方式下的有符号边际：质心、局部邻域和监督线性边界；并通过边界位置、层间变化和粗略形状总结边际轮廓，实现对多层安全信号的系统性分解与分析。

Result: 在九个指令微调模型（1.2B–70B）和七个安全基准上，Geometry-Lite 在保持接近多层堆叠性能的同时，显著优于单层探测器。结果显示，安全证据主要由持久的边界位置几何主导，而层间漂移和结构摘要对总体性能提升作用较小，仅在特定条件下有助于召回率调整。在基准迁移场景中，类条件均值几何结构表现出更强的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 提示级安全证据并非主要源于层间动态演化信号，而是由稳定存在的层内边际几何构成。其有效成分与读出偏差在关键决策区域中得以显现，为理解大语言模型的安全机制提供了新的几何视角。

Abstract: Prompt-level safety probes for large language models use hidden-state representations to separate safe from unsafe prompts, but strong average detection performance does not explain the geometry of this separation. In particular, it remains unclear how safety evidence is formed across layers, which aspects of that layer-wise geometry support low-false-positive decisions, and which geometric biases remain stable under benchmark shift. We study this as an empirical decomposition problem and introduce Geometry-Lite, a compact prompt-level probe that maps each layer's final prompt-token representation to signed margins under centroid, local-neighborhood, and supervised linear-boundary readouts, then summarizes the resulting margin profiles by boundary position, layer-to-layer change, and coarse shape. Across nine instruction-tuned backbones ($1.2$B--$70$B) and seven safety benchmarks, Geometry-Lite improves over single-layer probes while remaining close to raw multi-layer score stacking, making it a useful instrument for analyzing the multi-layer safety signal. The decomposition shows that safety evidence is expressed primarily through persistent boundary-position geometry: final or extremal margins and unsafe-side layer occupancy dominate aggregate detection performance. In contrast, finite-difference drift and structural summaries add little to pooled AUROC, although drift can provide small recall-oriented corrections under shifted low-FPR thresholds. Under benchmark shift, optimized linear boundaries are sharp on the training mixture, whereas class-conditional mean geometry retains separation more reliably on a predefined hard held-out subset. Overall, prompt-level safety evidence is not primarily a layer-to-layer motion signal, but a persistent layer-wise margin geometry whose useful components and readout-level biases become visible in decision-critical regimes.

Method: 提出CP-MoE框架，包含两个核心组件：(1) 一致性保持路由偏差，利用瞬态专家估计表示相似性并引导更兼容的专家选择；(2) 瞬态专家引导的正则化机制，选择性保护关键历史参数以防止在合并过程中被覆盖。

Abstract: Catastrophic forgetting remains a major obstacle to continual learning in large language models (LLMs) and vision--language models (VLMs). To address this, we propose CP-MoE, a continual learning framework built around a transient expert that captures early task-specific updates and guides their integration into stable experts. CP-MoE introduces a consistency-preserving routing bias, which uses the transient expert to estimate representation similarity with stable experts and steer routing towards more compatible expert selection, and a transient expert-guided regularisation mechanism, which selectively protects important historical parameters during merging. Together, these components reduce parameter interference and forgetting while preserving cross-task knowledge transfer. ### [192] [Automated Kernel Discovery Towards Understanding High-dimensional Bayesian Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20249)
*Taeyoung Yun,Woocheol Shin,Inhyuck Song,Jaewoo Lee,Jinkyoo Park*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动化核函数设计方法在高维场景下受限于有限的核组合规则，且基于大模型的方法需依赖原始观测数据条件化，面临上下文长度限制和模式提取困难问题。因此亟需一种能探索更广泛核空间、无需观测条件化的新型方法。

Method: 提出两阶段LLM驱动的进化框架：第一阶段由大模型生成新颖的数学形式；第二阶段将这些形式转化为合法可执行的代码。结合留一法连续概率评分（LOO-CRPS）作为选择标准，以抑制过拟合。

Result: 在五个高维贝叶斯优化基准上，所提方法平均排名为1.2（共17个对比方法），显著优于现有基线；通过分析发现部分特定结构的核函数对高维优化性能提升有关键作用。

Conclusion: Kernel Discovery成功实现了高维贝叶斯优化中核函数的高效自动发现，克服了传统方法的局限性，揭示了有效核函数的潜在结构特征，为未来自适应核设计提供了新范式。

Abstract: Gaussian Process (GP) kernels are central to Bayesian optimization (BO), yet designing effective kernels for high-dimensional problems still relies on extensive manual engineering. Existing automated approaches struggle in high dimensions for two bottlenecks: their kernel search space is limited to additions and multiplications of base kernels, and LLM-based approaches require conditioning on raw observations, which becomes infeasible due to context-length limits and the difficulty of extracting meaningful patterns. We introduce \textbf{Kernel Discovery}, a LLM-driven evolutionary framework for high-dimensional BO that searches a broader kernel space beyond predefined composition rules and does not require conditioning on observations. Motivated by the observation that directly prompting an LLM to generate kernel code yields syntactically varied but functionally identical kernels, we adopt a two-stage approach: an LLM first proposes novel mathematical forms, then a second LLM call converts each form into validated, executable code. We also propose a leave-one-out continuous ranked probability score (LOO-CRPS) as a selection criterion that penalizes overfitted kernels. On five high-dimensional BO benchmarks, our method achieves an average rank of \textbf{1.2 out of 17}, outperforming competitive baselines.
  We further analyze the discovered kernels to identify which kernels lead to improvements in high-dimensional BO.

We hypothesize that jointly training pedestrians and the SDC with multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) produces more realistic interaction scenarios than training the SDC against fixed pedestrian policies, and that the resulting behavior gap between predictable and unpredictable crossings can be measured directly from trajectories. Pedestrian locomotion follows scripted Dijkstra pathfinding, while an RL policy controls high-level go/wait decisions. Jaywalking probability depends on a per-pedestrian personality trait sampled at episode start and hidden from the SDC. In 500-episode evaluations, the co-trained SDC reached 78% of goals with a 14% collision rate, compared to 35% goals and 33% collisions for the best rule-based baseline. A speed differential metric shows that the SDC traveled 2.65 m/s faster near jaywalkers than near crosswalk users at close range (0-3 m), indicating that jaywalking encounters were not anticipated.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GRPO等强化学习方法在面对超出当前模型能力的任务时，由于采样方案单一（仅依赖原始提示），难以获得高质量轨迹，导致缺乏有效梯度方向，训练容易停滞。因此需要一种更智能的采样与训练机制来提升探索效率与策略更新质量。

Method: 提出FBOS-RL框架，引入反馈驱动的探索增强机制，并设计两个协同的目标：EPA用于对齐策略以提升已有能力的利用效率，ECC用于激发探索以拓展模型能力边界，二者形成正向循环，促进持续优化。

Result: 实验表明，FBOS-RL在相同采样量下训练速度更快，最终性能更高，同时保持更高的策略熵和更低的梯度范数，证明了其高效性与稳定性。

Conclusion: FBOS-RL通过反馈驱动的双目标协同机制，实现了探索与利用的动态平衡，有效克服了传统强化学习中因低质量采样导致的训练停滞问题，为大模型推理能力的对齐与提升提供了新范式。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning has become a cornerstone for aligning and unlocking the reasoning capabilities of large-scale models. At its core, the training loop of GRPO and its variants alternates between rollout sampling and policy update. Unlike supervised learning, where each gradient step is anchored to an explicit ground-truth target, the optimal gradient direction for updating model parameters in this setting is not known a priori; the high-quality rollouts drawn during the sampling stage therefore act as the implicit "teacher" that guides every parameter update. However, GRPO adopt a simple sampling scheme that conditions all rollouts on the same original prompt. When a task lies beyond the policy model's current capability, this sampling scheme rarely yields a high-quality rollout, leaving the policy model without a meaningful gradient direction when updating its parameters, which causes training to stall. To address this issue, we propose FBOS-RL, a Feedback-Driven Bi-Objective Synergistic reinforcement learning framework. Specifically, we let the model perform Feedback-Guided Exploration Enhancement based on the feedback provided by the environment, and on top of this we design two mutually reinforcing training objectives: Exploitation-oriented Policy Alignment(EPA) and Exploration-oriented Capability Cultivation(ECC). Extensive experiments demonstrate that EPA and ECC can mutually reinforce each other, forming a positive flywheel effect that significantly improves both the training efficiency and the final performance ceiling of reinforcement learning. Specifically, under an identical number of rollouts, FBOS-RL learns substantially faster than GRPO and feedback-based baselines and ultimately attains a higher performance ceiling, while exhibiting higher policy entropy and lower gradient norms throughout training.

</details>


### [195] [Instance Discrimination for Link Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20257)
*Valentin Cuzin-Rambaud,Mathieu Lefort,Rémy Cazabet*

Method: 提出基于社区结构的新型结构增强方法；设计L-GRACE和L-BGRL两个新模型，采用链接表示进行学习，以适应链接预测任务需求。

Result: 所提方法在无属性图上表现优异，显著优于现有方法，在自监督与监督设置下均达到或接近当前最优性能。

Abstract: Recently, instance discrimination models have emerged as a major solution for self-supervised learning. Having already demonstrated its effectiveness in the image domain, instance discrimination learning is now proving equally convincing in the graph domain, in particular for node classification. However, fewer contributions have tackled the link prediction task. In this contribution, we propose to adapt existing methods to this context. We first provide a rigorous evaluation of existing self-supervised models in the field of link prediction, showing that the main performance depends on the augmentation process (like in computer vision). We then propose a new structural augmentation based on the community structure that is relevant for link prediction. Our main contribution introduces two new models, L-GRACE and L-BGRL, based on link representations instead of node representations, which improve the performance of the existing methods, especially on unattributed graphs, and we show that they perform on par with the state of the art, both in supervised and self-supervised contexts.

### [196] [Catching a Moving Subspace: Low-Rank Bandits Beyond Stationarity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20269)
*Hamed Khosravi,Xiaoming Huo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了具有潜在低秩结构且子空间随时间漂移的上下文强化学习问题，提出SPSC算法在未知分段边界下实现内在秩动态后悔率$\widetilde{O}(r\sqrt{T})$，突破传统线性带宽的环境维度依赖；通过揭示可识别性的三重条件边界，首次完整刻画了此类问题的可解区域，并在多个真实与合成数据集上验证其优越性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法仅能处理低秩或非平稳性之一：静态低秩带宽在子空间变化时失效，而非平稳线性带宽则维持高维环境下的次优后悔率。本文旨在统一处理两者，提升实际应用中推荐、临床剂量等场景的效率与适应性。

Method: 提出SPSC算法，结合各向同性探测与窗口化投影岭UCB利用策略，在学习到的低维子空间内进行探索与利用；采用CUSUM风格变体在线检测分段边界，实现对未知切换点的自适应追踪。

Result: 理论证明在满足三个必要条件（已知噪声方差、状态-噪声耦合有界、探测支持满维）下，移动子空间可被唯一识别；算法达到$\widetilde{O}(r\sqrt{T}) + \widetilde{O}(T^{2/3}) + O(W\,V_{\mathrm{in}})$的动态后悔率，显著优于传统$\\widetilde{O}(d\\sqrt{T})$；实验在11个基准测试中均验证其优势，尤其当$d-r \\gtrsim T^{1/6}$时表现突出。

Conclusion: 这是首个同时刻画识别边界并实现内在秩动态后悔率的工作，为非平稳低秩上下文带宽提供了理论完备与实践高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Many bandit deployments (recommendation, clinical dosing, ad targeting) share two facts prior work handles only in isolation: rewards live on a low-dimensional latent subspace, and that subspace drifts. Stationary low-rank bandits exploit rank but break under subspace change; non-stationary linear bandits adapt to drift but pay ambient rate $\widetilde{O}(d\sqrt{T})$. We study piecewise-stationary low-rank linear contextual bandits with scalar feedback: $θ_t = B_k^\star w_t$ with rank-$r$ factor $B_k^\star\in\mathbb{R}^{d\times r}$ constant within each of $K$ unknown segments and able to shift at boundaries. Our results are tight along three axes. (i) Identification boundary. With single-play scalar rewards, the moving subspace is recoverable through quadratic functionals of rewards iff three probe-side conditions hold: known noise variance, bounded state-noise coupling, and full-dimensional probe support. Each is necessary in the unrestricted-second-moment problem, and jointly they are sufficient, characterizing the boundary of the solvable region. (ii) Algorithm and dynamic regret. SPSC interleaves isotropic probes with windowed projected ridge-UCB exploitation inside the learned $r$-dimensional subspace; a CUSUM-style variant discovers segment boundaries online. The costed dynamic regret is $\widetilde{O}(r\sqrt{T})+\widetilde{O}(T^{2/3})+O(W\,V_{\mathrm{in}})$, replacing the ambient $d\sqrt{T}$ rate with the intrinsic rank. (iii) Empirics. On eleven benchmarks spanning synthetic, UCI/MovieLens, semi-synthetic clinical, and ZOZOTOWN production-log data, SPSC outperforms non-stationary and low-rank baselines whenever $d-r\gtrsim T^{1/6}$, matching the analytical crossover. To our knowledge, this is the first work to characterize the identification boundary and attain the intrinsic-rank dynamic-regret rate in this setting.

### [197] [Conformal Selective Acting: Anytime-Valid Risk Control for RLVR-Trained LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20270)
*Hamed Khosravi,Xiaoming Huo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CSA 是一种用于强化学习微调的本地专用大模型（LLM）在受监管组织中的部署框架，旨在满足每轮部署的误差预算 $\alpha$ 下的即时安全性要求。现有方法无法在自适应、在线更新的数据流中提供路径一致的逐轮选择性风险控制：离线方法依赖交换性假设，在线方法仅约束长期平均风险，非交换性扩展有效性不足，而最接近的 A-RCPS 方法控制的是边际风险而非选择性风险。CSA 通过构建基于 Bonferroni 网格的 Ville 型 e-过程，并在 RLVR 过滤条件下评估，填补了这一空白。理论证明其具备：(i) 路径一致的选择性风险上界 $R_T^{\mathrm{act}} \le \alpha + O(N_T^{-1/2})$；(ii) 达到最优率的认证性能 $\Theta(\bar\eta^{-2}\log(1/\delta))$；(iii) 不随时间变化的释放率差距。在 8 个专家基准、160 个对抗分布偏移场景和 10,300 轮在线 LoRA 更新实验中，只有 CSA 满足路径有效性且不拒绝任何部署。CSA 并非新模型或训练算法，而是与模型无关的部署侧补充，适用于无法使用前沿 API 的操作者。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在受监管环境中部署经过强化学习微调的本地专用大模型时，必须在每轮部署中满足严格的误差预算 $\alpha$，且不能跨部署聚合数据或等待长期平均表现。现有安全包装器无法在自适应、在线更新的数据流中实现路径一致的选择性风险控制，尤其缺乏对即时、逐轮安全性的保障。因此需要一种能在无交换性假设、无需长期平均、且不拒绝合理部署的前提下，提供强有效性保证的实时安全验证机制。

Method: 提出 Conformal Selective Acting (CSA)，采用 (测试统计量, 有效性保证, 部署规则) 框架，识别出关键空缺：即在每阈值的 e-过程、选择性风险、任意时间路径有效性、最大认证阈值规则之间存在不可兼容的组合。CSA 通过构建基于 Bonferroni 网格的 Ville 型 e-过程，结合 RLVR 过滤条件，在每轮独立评估风险，实现路径一致性。利用预测性更新和单调风险校准假设，设计部署规则以确保及时响应。

Result: 理论分析表明：(i) CSA 实现路径一致的选择性风险上界 $R_T^{\mathrm{act}} \le \alpha + O(N_T^{-1/2})$；(ii) 认证效率达到率最优 $\Theta(\bar\eta^{-2}\log(1/\delta))$；(iii) 释放率差距不随时间增长。实验证明，在 480 个专家流、160 个对抗分布偏移流、以及超过 10,300 轮在线更新的复杂场景中，只有 CSA 满足路径有效性且不拒绝任何合法部署，优于其他十种对比方法。

Conclusion: CSA 是首个在自适应、在线更新流中实现路径一致选择性风险控制的部署包装器，填补了现有方法在即时安全性上的关键空白。它不依赖于特定模型或训练方式，是面向无法使用前沿 API 的操作者的通用部署安全保障工具，为受监管环境下本地 LLM 的可信部署提供了坚实基础。

Abstract: A local specialist LLM, fine-tuned with reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards (RLVR) on operator-local data, is installed in a regulated organization with per-deployment error budget $α$. The operator needs a safety certificate for this deployment's stream at every round: no pooling across deployments, no waiting for a long-run average. Existing wrappers cannot deliver this on adaptive, online-updated streams: offline conformal-risk methods require exchangeability; online-conformal methods bound only long-run averages; non-exchangeable extensions are marginally valid; and the closest anytime wrapper, A-RCPS, controls marginal rather than selective risk. Using a (test statistic, validity guarantee, deployment rule) framework, we identify one empty cell forced by deployment requirements: e-process per threshold, selective risk, anytime-pathwise validity, max-certified-threshold rule. Conformal Selective Acting (CSA) fills it as a per-round wrapper maintaining a Ville-type e-process per threshold on a Bonferroni grid, evaluated against the RLVR filtration. Under predictable updates and isotonic-calibrated monotone risk we prove (i) an anytime-pathwise selective-risk bound $R_T^{\mathrm{act}}\leα+O(N_T^{-1/2})$, (ii) rate-optimal certification matching $Θ(\barη^{-2}\log(1/δ))$, and (iii) a horizon-independent release-rate gap. Across eight specialist benchmarks ($480$ streams), sixteen adversarial distribution-shift cells ($160$ streams), and five live Expert-Iteration RLVR cells with online LoRA over four base models in three architecture families ($10{,}300$ rounds), CSA is the only method among ten compared that satisfies pathwise validity and non-refusing deployment on every cell. We do not propose a new LLM, training algorithm, or policy class; CSA is the deployment-side complement, orthogonal to the model, for operators who cannot use a frontier API.

</details>


### [198] [Modality-Decoupled Online Recursive Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20273)
*Siyuan Li,Youyuan Zhang,Fangming Liu,Jing Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: M-ORE 是一种用于多模态大语言模型（MLLM）的模态解耦在线递归编辑方法，旨在解决在有限计算和内存预算下持续学习时出现的跨模态冲突与长时程干扰问题。通过统一的近端投影公式推导出闭式更新，并利用Sherman-Morrison递归实现恒定每次编辑开销。该方法分别维护文本堆栈和视觉投影器的模块化局部统计信息，避免视觉激活主导更新；同时在固定正交低秩编辑子空间中进行连续更新，缓解长期干扰。实验表明，M-ORE 在多个 MLLM 架构和在线编辑基准上显著提升可靠性、泛化性和局部性，且具备良好的质量-效率权衡。代码已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有为纯文本大模型设计的编辑方法在多模态大模型（MLLMs）上表现不佳，主要由于视觉主导的激活影响更新统计，导致跨模态冲突；同时，顺序编辑在共享编辑空间中相互干扰，引发长时程干扰问题。因此需要一种能有效解耦模态、降低干扰、适应持续学习的在线编辑机制。

Result: 在多个 MLLM 基线和在线编辑任务上，M-ORE 显著优于现有强基线，在可靠性、泛化性和局部性方面均有提升，同时保持高效的计算性能，展现出优异的质量-效率平衡。

Abstract: Online model editing for multimodal large language models (MLLMs) requires assimilating a stream of corrections under tight compute and memory budgets. Yet editors developed for text-only LLMs often degrade on MLLMs: visually dominant activations skew the statistics that shape updates, causing cross-modal conflict, while sequential writes become entangled in a shared edit space and amplify long-horizon interference, causing inter-edit interference. To address these, we propose M-ORE, a modality-decoupled online recursive editor for lifelong MLLM adaptation. M-ORE is derived from a unified proximal-projection formulation and admits a closed-form update with a Sherman-Morrison recursion, yielding constant per-edit overhead. It maintains module-wise locality statistics for the text stack and the visual projector to avoid visually dominated update shaping and performs continual updates in a fixed orthogonal low-rank edit subspace via a Sherman-Morrison recursion to mitigate long-horizon interference. Experiments on multiple MLLM backbones and online editing benchmarks show that our M-ORE method consistently improves reliability, generality, and locality over strong baselines, while achieving favorable quality-efficiency scaling. Our code is publicly available at https://github.com/lab-klc/M-ORE.

### [199] [OmniISR: A Unified Framework for Centralized and Federated Learning via Intermediate Supervision and Regularization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20276)
*Wei-Bin Kou,Guangxu Zhu,Ming Tang,Chen Zhang,Lisheng Wu,Lei Zhou,Yujiu Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: OmniISR 是一个统一框架，融合了集中式学习（CL）、联邦学习（FL）及混合模式，通过多层中间监督与正则化（ISR）信号实现兼容。采用互信息（MI）对齐内部协变量漂移，负熵（NE）抑制过自信预测并防止设备特异性表示坍塌。理论分析表明，该方法具备非渐近的 O(1/sqrt(T)) 收敛性、降低客户端漂移、保证更新一致性，并加速逃离严格鞍点。实验显示其在多种场景下显著提升性能，减少 CL-FL 差距 22.60%，在 37/48 的配对指标中胜出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有边缘智能部署面临法律差异导致的计算范式冲突：部分区域支持集中式学习（CL），另一些则强制数据本地化需使用联邦学习（FL）。两者优化机制不兼容，简单集成缺乏理论保障，亟需一种统一且可理论证明的融合框架。

Method: 提出 OmniISR 框架，在多个隐藏层引入中间监督与正则化信号；使用互信息（MI）作为监督信号以对齐 CL 的内部协变量漂移与 FL 的客户端表示漂移；采用负熵（NE）作为正则项，抑制过自信预测，保留表示不确定性，防止设备特定表示坍塌。

Result: 实验验证了 OmniISR 在集中式与联邦式学习中均有效提升模型性能；显著缩小 CL 与 FL 之间的性能差距（达 22.60%）；在 37/48 的配对指标上优于现有方法；理论分析提供了收敛性、漂移控制、梯度对齐和逃逸时间等多重保证。

Conclusion: OmniISR 提供了一个统一、理论严谨且高效的跨范式训练框架，成功弥合了集中式与联邦学习之间的鸿沟，为异构环境下的边缘智能部署提供了可靠解决方案。

Abstract: The global deployment of edge intelligence operates across heterogeneous legal frameworks. While some regions permit centralized learning (CL) via cloud data aggregation, others enforce strict data localization, necessitating federated learning (FL). This operational dichotomy introduces two incompatible optimization regimes (i.e., unbiased global gradients yet coupled with internal covariate shift in CL versus biased, drift-prone local updates in FL), resulting in that any naive integration of the two lacks rigorous theoretical guarantees. To fill this gap, we propose OmniISR, a unified framework that fuses pure CL, pure FL, and hybrid CL-FL training modes via equipping intermediate supervision and regularization (ISR) signals at multiple hidden layers. Specifically, we propose (i) to use mutual-information (MI) as intermediate supervision to align shifting internal covariate in CL and client-drifting representations in FL, and (ii) to adopt negative-entropy (NE) as intermediate regularizer to penalize overconfident prediction, preserve representational uncertainty, and avoid device-specific collapse. On the theory side, we derive (i) a unified, ISR-agnostic, and non-asymptotic O(1/sqrt(T)) convergence bound that shows the introduced ISR does not violate standard SGD convergence, (ii) a federated drift-bound that quantifies the ISR-reduced client drift, (iii) a gradient-alignment guarantee that ensures non-conflicting CL and FL updates under mild bias, and (iv) an explicit escape-time bound that indicates that CL-FL hybrid mixing enlarges effective stochasticity and accelerates escape from strict saddles. Extensive experiments demonstrate that OmniISR consistently improves model performance in both centralized and federated paradigms, reduces the CL-FL gap by 22.60%, and yields 37/48 paired metric wins across multiple FL algorithms.

### [200] [ClaimDiff-RL: Fine-Grained Caption Reinforcement Learning through Visual Claim Comparison](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20278)

Method: 引入ClaimDiff-RL框架，基于参考句与图像，由多模态判别器提取视觉相关的原子主张差异，逐个验证其真实性，标注错误类型与严重程度，并生成用于奖励构建的细粒度统计信息。

Result: 在160张图像的人工标注诊断基准、公开数据集及VQA任务上，ClaimDiff-RL显著改善了幻觉与遗漏事实之间的平衡，保持了通用能力，并在物体计数、空间关系、场景识别等细粒度维度上超越Gemini-3-Pro-Preview。

Conclusion: 基于可验证、带类型的原子主张差异作为奖励单元，能够有效支持细粒度、可诊断的图像描述强化学习，为提升生成内容的准确性与完整性提供了新范式。

Abstract: Long-form image captioning exposes a reward granularity problem in RL: captions are judged as whole sequences, while the important errors occur at the level of individual visual claims. A good dense caption should be both faithful and informative, avoiding hallucination without omitting salient details. Yet pairwise preferences, reference-based metrics, and holistic scalar rewards compress these local errors into a single sequence-level signal, obscuring the tradeoff between factuality and coverage. We introduce ClaimDiff-RL, a framework that uses reference-conditioned atomic claim differences as the reward unit for caption RL. Given an image, an actor caption, and a reference caption, a multimodal judge enumerates visually grounded differences, verifies each difference against the image, assigns open-vocabulary error types and severity levels, and produces per-difference statistics for reward composition. This makes hallucinated claims and omitted salient facts separately measurable and tunable. Experiments show that holistic scalar rewards can reduce hallucination by increasing missing facts, while ClaimDiff-RL exposes this faithfulness and coverage tradeoff and enables more balanced operating points. On a 160-image human-labeled diagnostic benchmark, public captioning benchmarks, and VQA benchmarks, ClaimDiff-RL improves the hallucination--missing-fact balance, preserves general capability, and even surpasses Gemini-3-Pro-Preview on several fine-grained Capability dimensions such as object counting, spatial relations, and scene recognition. These results suggest that typed, verifiable claim differences are an effective reward unit for fine-grained and diagnosable caption RL.

</details>


### [201] [Introspective X Training: Feedback Conditioning Improves Scaling Across all LLM Training Stages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20285)
*Brandon Cui,Ximing Lu,Jaehun Jung,Syeda Nahida Akter,Hyunwoo Kim,Yuxiao Qu,David Acuna,Shrimai Prabhumoye,Yejin Choi,Prithviraj Ammanabrolu*

TL;DR: 提出Introspective Training (IXT)方法，利用后期训练阶段的动态信息指导早期训练，通过思维奖励模型生成自然语言反馈并用于数据标注，实现质量感知训练；通过前缀条件化处理，使模型在训练初期即关注关键信息，显著提升计算效率（最高2.8倍）并突破数学与代码等领域的性能瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大模型训练流程中，后期阶段（如后训练）的动态信息未被有效利用于早期阶段（如预训练），导致训练效率受限。如何更高效地跨多个不断扩展的训练阶段进行扩展成为关键挑战。

Method: 提出Introspective Training (IXT)，基于离线奖励条件强化学习思想，使用思维奖励模型对数据生成自然语言批评反馈，并将该反馈作为前缀嵌入训练数据中，实现对不同令牌的差异化对待，从而在训练早期即引入质量感知机制。

Result: 在7.5-12B参数的Transformer密集型大模型上从头训练至18万亿次标记，实验表明IXT可显著改善缩放曲线，提升最多2.8倍的计算效率，并在数学、代码等复杂任务中达到传统训练无法企及的性能水平。

Conclusion: IXT通过引入后期训练反馈指导早期训练，实现了更高效、更高质量的大模型训练，在计算效率和性能上限方面均取得显著突破。

Abstract: We tackle the question of how to scale more efficiently across the many, ever-growing stages of current LLM training pipelines. Our guiding intuition stems from the fact that the dynamics of later stages of the pipeline, e.g. post-training, can be used to inform earlier stages such as pre-training. To this end, we propose Introspective Training (or IXT), inspired by offline reward-conditioned reinforcement learning and applicable to any stage of training. IXT uses a thinking reward model to annotate data with natural language critique based feedback, enabling quality aware training from the earliest stages of the pipeline. Models are then trained by prefix-conditioning the data with the generated feedback -- ensuring that not all tokens are treated equally starting much earlier in training than usual. Comprehensive experiments on 7.5-12B transformer-based dense LLMs trained from scratch all the way up to 18 Trillion tokens seen show that our method: bends scaling curves resulting in up to 2.8x more compute efficiency generally; and reaches performance levels unachievable for models trained otherwise in domains such as math and code.

### [202] [Plug-and-Play Spiking Operators: Breaking the Nonlinearity Bottleneck in Spiking Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20289)
*Xinzhe Yuan,Xiang Peng,Bin Gu,Huan Xiong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种即插即用的框架，用于在ANN-to-SNN转换中实现针对Transformer模型非线性操作的脉冲友好近似。该框架将复杂的非线性运算分解为除法、指数和ℓ₂范数三种基本计算单元，并通过LIF神经元群组结合轻量级位移缩放来实现，避免浮点运算。通过模块化设计，支持Softmax、SiLU及归一化等常见非线性操作，无需微调。实验表明，在多种LLM任务中，仅替换目标非线性层时，性能下降小于1%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前ANN-to-SNN转换方法主要关注线性代数操作的脉冲驱动实现，但对关键非线性操作（如Softmax、SiLU）支持不足。这些非线性操作通常涉及除法、指数或范数计算，难以在标准漏电积分与发放（LIF）神经元动态下自然实现，限制了其在类神经形态计算环境中的应用。因此亟需一种兼容性强、无需训练的非线性操作脉冲化方案。

Method: 将Transformer中的非线性操作分解为三种通用计算原语：除法、指数和ℓ₂范数。采用LIF神经元群组进行群体计算，并引入轻量级位移缩放以规避浮点数运算。通过模块化设计，构建可复用的算子块，无缝集成至现有ANN-to-SNN转换流程中。

Result: 所提方法在多个大型语言模型上验证有效，仅替换非线性操作时，各项任务上的精度损失均低于1%，表现出极高的兼容性与性能保持能力。

Conclusion: 本框架提供了一种高效、无需微调的脉冲友好非线性操作实现方式，显著提升了ANN-to-SNN转换在大型语言模型中的实用性，推动了神经形态计算在复杂深度学习模型上的部署。

Abstract: ANN-to-SNN conversion offers a practical, training-free route to spiking large language models. However, current pipelines primarily focus on spike-driven realizations for Transformer linear-algebra operations, while providing limited support for key nonlinear operators. This gap limits compatibility with neuromorphic-style execution constraints, where such nonlinearities typically require division, exponentiation, or norm computations that are not naturally supported by standard leaky integrate-and-fire dynamics. To solve this problem, we propose a plug-and-play framework that implements spike-friendly approximations for Transformer nonlinearities and integrates into existing ANN-to-SNN pipelines. Our method decomposes these nonlinear computations into three recurring primitives -- division, exponentiation, and $\ell_2$ norms -- and realizes them via population computation using LIF neuron groups, combined with lightweight bit-shift scaling to avoid floating-point arithmetic. By composing these primitives as modular operator blocks, our framework supports common Transformer nonlinearities (e.g., Softmax, SiLU, and normalization) without any fine-tuning. Experiments on a range of LLMs Transformers show that selectively replacing the targeted nonlinear operators incurs less than a $1\%$ accuracy drop across all evaluated tasks.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have enabled web agents that follow natural language goals through multi-step browser interactions. However, agents fine-tuned on specific trajectories and domain often struggle to generalize out of domain, and offline training can be compute-inefficient due to noisy, redundant trajectories and long accessibility-tree (AXTree) states. To address both issues, we propose Weasel, a trajectory selection method for offline training of web agents. Weasel selects a fixed-budget subset of trajectory steps by optimizing an objective that balances unary importance with pairwise diversity over states, websites, and interaction patterns, solving efficiently with a greedy algorithm. We further improve efficiency with target-centered AXTree pruning that keeps only content around the ground-truth action target, and we mitigate style mismatch for reasoning-native models by replacing expert traces with model-generated, style-consistent rationales. Across AgentTrek and NNetNav training datasets, evaluations in WebArena, WorkArena, and MiniWob, and experiments with Qwen2.5-7B, Gemma3-4B, and Qwen3-8B, Weasel improves out-of-domain performance while reducing training cost, producing roughly 9.7-12.5$\times$ training speedups over standard fine-tuning. ### [204] [TreeText-CTS: Compact, Source-Traceable Tree-Path Evidence for Irregular Clinical Time-Series Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20292)
*Kwanhyung Lee,Juhwan Choi,Jongheon Kim,Joohyung Lee,Hyeongwon Jang,Eunho Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TreeText-CTS 是一种新型的文本化电子健康记录（EHR）时间序列接口，将不规则的EHR轨迹转化为可读、紧凑且可追溯来源的树路径证据单元。它通过冻结的XGBoost模型处理多尺度窗口摘要，并将激活的树路径转化为由阈值条件组成的确定性证据。一个证据选择器提取有信息量的子集，再由语言模型编码器整合进行预测。在PhysioNet 2012死亡率、MIMIC-III死亡率和PhysioNet 2019脓毒症发作预测任务中，TreeText-CTS在AUROC和AUPRC上均优于现有文本接口，AUPRC提升6.0至9.7个百分点，同时保持与数值模型相当的性能。消融实验表明，树路径构建、证据选择和语言模型融合均对性能有贡献。由于所有输入语言模型的片段均由激活的树路径阈值条件构成，该方法确保了预测所用证据的可检查性和来源可追溯性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数值时间序列模型虽能有效处理不规则EHR数据，但无法提供支持风险评估的可读证据；而传统文本接口要么冗长（原始序列化），要么难以追溯（自由形式总结）。因此需要一种既能保持可读性，又能保证证据来源可追溯的高效方法。

Method: TreeText-CTS 将多尺度窗口摘要输入冻结的XGBoost模型，生成树路径证据；通过证据选择器筛选关键路径，再由语言模型编码器整合形成最终预测输入。整个过程无需患者级总结或自回归解码，所有输出证据均可追溯至具体测量值和时间窗。

Result: 在多个基准数据集上，TreeText-CTS 在文本接口中表现最优，尤其在AUPRC上相比最强基线提升6.0–9.7个百分点，同时性能接近甚至媲美数值模型。消融实验验证了各模块的有效性。

Conclusion: TreeText-CTS 成功实现了高精度、可解释、可追溯的EHR时间序列建模，为临床决策支持提供了可信的可读证据。

Abstract: Numerical time-series models can effectively process irregular electronic health record (EHR) trajectories, but they do not naturally expose the measurements and temporal patterns supporting each risk estimate as readable evidence. Existing text-based interfaces improve readability, but typically rely on either raw serialization, which is lengthy and redundant, or patient-level free-form summaries, which are difficult to trace to source measurements and time windows. To bridge this gap, we introduce TreeText-CTS (Clinical Time-Series), which converts irregular EHR trajectories into human-readable, compact, source-traceable tree-path evidence units without patient-level summarization or inference-time autoregressive decoding. TreeText-CTS routes multi-scale window summaries through frozen XGBoost models and verbalizes activated tree paths as deterministic, source-traceable evidence units composed of threshold conditions. An evidence selector assembles an informative subset of these units, which a language-model encoder then integrates for prediction. Across PhysioNet 2012 mortality, MIMIC-III mortality, and PhysioNet 2019 sepsis-onset forecasting, TreeText-CTS achieves the best AUROC and AUPRC among evaluated text-based EHR time-series interfaces, improving AUPRC by 6.0 to 9.7 absolute percentage points over the strongest prior text-based interface while remaining competitive with numerical time-series models. Ablations show that tree-path evidence construction, evidence selection, and language-model composition each contribute to performance. Because every span passed to the language-model encoder is constructed from activated tree-path threshold conditions, TreeText-CTS makes the evidence supplied to the final predictor inspectable and source-traceable.

### [205] [Quant.npu: Enabling Efficient Mobile NPU Inference for on-device LLMs via Fully Static Quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20295)
*Jinghe Zhang,Daliang Xu,Chenghua Wang,Weikai Xie,Tao Qi,Yun Ma,Mengwei Xu,Gang Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Quant.npu 是一种针对移动设备 NPU 硬件约束的全静态整数量化框架，通过引入可学习量化参数和旋转矩阵，实现无需运行时重新计算的低比特激活-权重量化。该方法提出基于旋转与位宽感知的初始化策略，以及分布感知的选择性优化（两阶段量化流程），有效解决梯度不稳定性问题，并结合敏感度引导的自适应混合精度方案，在保持高精度的同时将推理延迟降低最高达15.1%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有后训练量化（PTQ）方法多依赖动态激活量化，无法满足 NPU 硬件对全静态量化的要求，导致在移动设备上推理效率受限。因此亟需一种既能保持高精度又兼容 NPU 静态量化约束的新型量化方法。

Method: Quant.npu 采用全静态整数量化，引入可学习量化参数与旋转矩阵；提出旋转与位宽感知的初始化策略以稳定优化过程；设计分布感知的选择性优化（两阶段量化管道）区分旋转与未旋转张量；并结合敏感度引导的自适应混合精度机制，实现精度与效率的平衡。

Result: 在真实移动 NPU 上的实验表明，Quant.npu 在精度上媲美当前最优方法，同时推理延迟最多减少15.1%，显著提升部署效率。

Conclusion: Quant.npu 成功实现了高精度、低延迟的全静态量化，为 LLM 在 NPU 上的高效部署提供了可行方案，具有良好的实际应用价值。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed on mobile devices, where Neural Processing Units (NPUs) necessitate fully static quantization for optimal inference efficiency. However, existing post-training quantization (PTQ) methods predominantly rely on dynamic activation quantization, rendering them incompatible with NPU hardware constraints. To bridge the gap between high-fidelity PTQ and NPU-constrained inference, we propose Quant.npu, a integer-only fully static quantization framework. It incorporates learnable quantization parameters and rotation matrices, enabling low-bit activation-weight quantization without runtime quantization parameters re-computation. Crucially, we identify that initialization and selective optimization of quantization parameters is pivotal for optimization stability, as improper initialization and naive joint optimization induce gradient instability that disrupts the optimization of rotation matrices. To address this, we propose a rotation-and-bit-width-aware initialization tailored to diverse activation profiles and a distribution-aware selective optimization (two-stage quantization pipeline) tailored to rotated and unrotated tensors. Furthermore, we introduce a sensitivity-guided adaptive mixed-precision scheme to balance accuracy with inference efficiency. Extensive experiments on real-world mobile NPUs demonstrate that Quant.npu achieves comparable accuracy to state-of-the-art methods, while reducing inference latency by up to 15.1%.
