### [206] [Spectral Unforgetting: Post-Hoc Recovery of Damaged Capabilities Without Retraining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20296)
*Aarash Abro,Muhammad Tahir*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了微调语言模型时出现的灾难性遗忘现象，提出一种仅使用预训练检查点 $W_{\mathrm{base}}$ 和微调后检查点 $W_{\mathrm{ft}}$ 的后处理修复方法 DG-Hard。该方法通过谱分析将微调更新 $\Delta = W_{\mathrm{ft}} - W_{\mathrm{base}}$ 视为嵌入在独立同分布噪声中的低秩任务对齐信号，并应用 Donoho-Gavish 硬阈值法保留高能量结构部分、去除谱主干噪声，实现无需数据依赖调参的闭式SVD滤波修复。为克服评估难题，引入分区条件指标，分别衡量能力恢复、性能保持、无损伤和目标任务保留。在14个（模型, 任务）组合与九个跨领域基准测试中，DG-Hard 在平衡修复效果上优于其他后处理基线，且在未使用对齐数据的情况下恢复了因良性微调而退化的安全性对齐。结果表明，部分微调导致的能力损失并非特化不可避免的后果，而是权重更新中可移除的谱残留。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微调语言模型常导致未显式训练过的其他能力下降，即灾难性遗忘。现有方法难以在恢复旧能力的同时保留新任务性能，且缺乏有效的评估机制。因此需要一种无需额外数据、能精准修复微调副作用的后处理方案，并建立合理的评估标准以准确衡量修复效果。

Method: 提出 DG-Hard 方法，基于预训练与微调检查点之间的权重差 $\Delta$，将其视为低秩任务信号与随机噪声的混合体。利用 Donoho-Gavish 硬阈值法对每个权重差矩阵进行奇异值分解（SVD）过滤，仅保留高能量的结构成分，去除谱分布中的“噪声主干”，实现无需数据依赖的闭式修复。

Result: 在14个（模型, 任务）设置和9个跨域基准测试中，DG-Hard 在综合修复表现上优于所有后处理基线；能够有效恢复因微调而受损的安全对齐能力，即使未使用任何安全对齐数据。实验表明，微调造成的部分能力损失源于可被移除的谱残留，而非必然的特化代价。

Conclusion: 微调带来的部分能力退化并非不可避免，而是由权重更新中可识别的谱残差引起。通过仅使用两个检查点的谱修复方法（DG-Hard），可在不牺牲目标任务性能的前提下，高效恢复多种下游能力与安全对齐，验证了谱级修复的有效性与普适性。

Abstract: Fine-tuning a language model for a target task routinely degrades capabilities the training data never explicitly threatened. We study this phenomenon, known as catastrophic forgetting, and propose a post-hoc repair solution that uses only the pretrained checkpoint $W_{\mathrm{base}}$ and its fine-tuned descendant $W_{\mathrm{ft}}$. The goal is not merely to revert the model toward the base checkpoint, but to recover capabilities damaged by fine-tuning while preserving both the target-task gains and any beneficial held-out improvements. We introduce DG-Hard, a checkpoint-only spectral repair method for the fine-tuning update $Δ= W_{\mathrm{ft}} - W_{\mathrm{base}}$. DG-Hard treats $Δ$ as a low-rank task-aligned signal embedded in an IID-like noise residual that gradient descent has no incentive to remove, and applies the Donoho-Gavish hard singular-value threshold to each weight-delta matrix, keeping the structured high-energy part of the update and removing the spectral bulk. This reduces repair to a closed-form SVD filtering step requiring no data-dependent tuning. A central difficulty is evaluation: average accuracy hides per-benchmark failures, while naive recovery scores reward models that simply revert toward the base. We therefore introduce a partition-conditional metric that separately tracks healing, preservation, non-damage, and target-task retention. Across $14$ (model, task) settings and nine cross-domain held-out benchmarks, DG-Hard achieves the strongest balanced repair among post-hoc baselines. DG-Hard also restores safety alignment degraded by benign fine-tuning on three independent safety axes, despite using no alignment data. These results suggest that part of fine-tuning-induced capability loss is not an unavoidable consequence of specialization, but a removable spectral residue in the weight update itself.

</details>


### [207] [Mechanisms of Misgeneralization in Physical Sequence Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20299)
*Kento Nishi,Raphael Tang,Karun Kumar,Core Francisco Park,Hidenori Tanaka*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了生成序列模型在物理领域（如机器人学、机械模拟）中因训练数据分布偏差导致的物理误泛化问题。尽管单个生成轨迹看似合理，但整体物理量（如行程距离或能量消耗）的分布却与预期不符。作者提出‘物理误泛化’概念，并通过合成任务揭示其机制：模型局部误差在物理测量中累积，导致分布偏移。为此，作者引入‘数据偏差核’来量化这些误差，预测哪些物理量会失衡，并基于此设计了一种核引导的干预策略以改善分布控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在物理领域使用生成序列模型时，工程师常通过精心设计的演示数据来约束生成轨迹的物理量分布（如行程距离或能量），但标准深度学习方法往往无法保持这种分布意图，导致生成结果虽个体合理，但整体分布失准。这一现象被称为物理误泛化，亟需理论解释和解决方法。

Method: 提出数据偏差核（data deviation kernel）以量化模型局部误差在物理测量中的传播效应；通过控制实验验证该机制在合成任务中的有效性；将方法扩展至真实场景（迷宫导航、双摆运动），用于预测并修正物理量分布偏差；基于机理分析设计核引导的干预策略。

Result: 数据偏差核能有效预测物理量分布的偏移方向与程度，在合成任务及实际应用中均表现良好；所提出的核引导干预显著改善了生成轨迹在目标物理量上的分布一致性，缓解了物理误泛化问题。

Conclusion: 物理误泛化是生成模型在物理系统中常见且严重的问题，源于局部误差在物理量测量中的累积传播。通过引入数据偏差核进行机制建模与预测，可为分布控制提供可解释的干预路径，推动生成模型在物理系统中的可靠应用。

Abstract: Generative sequence models are often trained to plan motion in physical domains, from robotics to mechanical simulations. When constructing a dataset to train such a model, engineers may curate demonstrations to specify how trajectories should be distributed over a physical quantity like travel distance or mechanical energy. For example, a roboticist building a maze navigation agent might choose demonstrations whose travel distances cover a fixed range uniformly, hoping to constrain the agent's expected power usage. We find that standard deep learning can violate this intent: each generated trajectory can seem plausible on its own, but the aggregate distribution over the physical quantity is wrong. We call this failure physical misgeneralization, and develop an account of its mechanism. Using controlled synthetic tasks, we show that physical misgeneralization arises when local errors typical of the model class propagate through the physical measurement to shift the recovered distribution. We estimate these errors with a data deviation kernel, and we use it to predict which physical quantities gain or lose mass in both our synthetic and more applied maze navigation and double-pendulum motion tasks. Finally, our mechanistic interpretation helps identify which mitigation strategies are structurally promising, and we use it to propose a kernel-informed intervention.

Abstract: In this paper, we propose a robust subspace-constrained quadratic model (SCQM) for learning low-dimensional structure from high-dimensional data. This generalization enables reliable performance under both heavy-tailed and light-tailed noise, thereby substantially enhancing robustness across diverse data regimes. To efficiently address the resulting nonconvex optimization problem, we develop a gradient-based algorithm equipped with a backtracking line-search strategy that ensures stable and efficient convergence. ### [209] [Neural Collapse by Design: Learning Class Prototypes on the Hypersphere](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20302)
*Panagiotis Koromilas,Theodoros Giannakopoulos,Mihalis A. Nicolaou,Yannis Panagakis*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有监督学习方法无法达到理论最优的神经坍缩（NC）状态：交叉熵（CE）因未约束径向自由度导致退化几何，而监督对比学习（SCL）虽在预训练中逼近NC，但在线性探测阶段丢失该结构。两者本质为同一方法的不同表现形式，需针对性修复各自缺陷以实现设计上的神经坍缩。

Method: 提出归一化交叉熵（NTCE）和非线性归一化损失（NONL），增强负样本有效集合并解耦对齐与均匀性项；同时证明SCL中分类器权重天然等于类均值嵌入，故线性探测既冗余又损害性能。采用固定原型策略替代传统分类器训练。

Result: NTCE与NONL在四个基准（包括ImageNet-1K）上超越传统交叉熵准确率，95%以上逼近神经坍缩状态，仅用7.5%迭代次数即达成多数指标的收敛；固定原型的SCL可避免长时间分类器训练，性能媲美线性探测。迁移学习平均提升5.5%，极端类别不平衡下最高达8.7%，且在ImageNet-C上降低平均交叉熵，验证了以原型为中心的超球面学习范式优势。

Conclusion: 本研究将监督学习重新定义为在单位超球面上进行原型学习，通过设计使神经坍缩得以实现。无论从交叉熵或对比学习路径出发，均可高效、稳定地抵达最优几何结构，显著提升模型性能与训练效率。

Abstract: Supervised classification has a theoretical optimum, Neural Collapse (NC), yet neither of its two dominant paradigms reaches it in practice. Cross entropy (CE) leaves radial degrees of freedom unconstrained and converges to a degenerate geometry, while supervised contrastive learning (SCL) drives features toward NC during pretraining but discards this structure in a post hoc linear probing phase. We show that both paradigms are different appearances of the same method, prototype contrast on the unit hypersphere, and that closing the gap requires fixing each at its specific point of failure. From the CE side, we propose NTCE and NONL, two normalized losses that import contrastive optimization's missing ingredients into classifier learning: a large effective negative set and decoupled alignment and uniformity terms. From the SCL side, we prove that SCL's objective already optimizes throughout training for a principled classifier whose weights are the class mean embeddings, making linear probing both redundant and harmful. Empirically, on four benchmarks including ImageNet-1K, NTCE and NONL surpass CE accuracy, closely approximate NC ($\geq 95\%$), and match CE's converged NC on 4/5 metrics in under $7.5\%$ of its iterations, while SCL with fixed prototypes matches linear probing without the hours-long classifier training phase. The learned geometry yields $+5.5\%$ mean relative improvement in transfer learning, up to $+8.7\%$ under severe class imbalance, and lower mCE on ImageNet-C, recasting supervised learning as prototype learning on the hypersphere, with NC reached by design on both paths.

### [211] [WaveGraphNet: Physics-Consistent Guided-Wave Damage Localization through Coupled Inverse-Forward Graph Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20311)
*Vinay Sharma,Aditya Bharade,Olga Fink*

Method: 提出WaveGraphNet，将传感器布局建模为图，节点为传感器，边为波传播路径；设计逆向分支从波响应谱特征推断损伤位置，正向分支预测给定损伤位置下的波能偏差模式；通过正向分支作为物理一致性约束，增强逆向推理的合理性。

Result: 所提方法在稀疏传感条件下显著提升了损伤定位精度与外推能力，在基准测试中优于非图及图基基线方法，验证了耦合逆向-正向图学习的有效性。

Conclusion: 耦合逆向-正向图学习为稀疏导波传感条件下的损伤定位提供了一种高效且鲁棒的解决方案，尤其适用于训练数据覆盖不全的场景。

Abstract: Guided-wave structural health monitoring enables damage localization in composite plates using sparse networks of bonded piezoelectric transducers. However, inferring the spatial location of defects from pitch-catch measurements remains weakly constrained when only a limited set of damage locations is available for training. As a result, models trained to predict defect locations may perform well on seen cases but generalize poorly to unseen regions of the structure.
  This paper proposes WaveGraphNet, a coupled inverse--forward graph learning framework for guided-wave damage localization in Carbon Fiber Reinforced Polymer (CFRP) plates. The sensing layout is explicitly modeled as a graph, where transducers are represented as nodes and measured propagation paths define the graph connectivity. An inverse branch maps graph-structured spectral descriptors of differential guided-wave responses to a damage location, while a forward branch predicts the path-wise energy-deviation patterns of measured wave responses associated with a candidate location. During training, the forward branch serves as a physics-consistent regularizer, discouraging location estimates that are numerically plausible but inconsistent with the measured redistribution of wave-response energy. This coupling encourages agreement between inferred damage coordinates and the underlying wave propagation behavior.
  Within this benchmark, the proposed graph-based formulation provides a strong localization model for sparse guided-wave sensing and demonstrates improved robustness in extrapolation to held-out regions compared to both non-graph and graph baselines. These results highlight the potential of coupled inverse-forward graph learning as an effective strategy for guided-wave localization under limited spatial coverage.

### [212] [Less Data, Faster Training: repeating smaller datasets speeds up learning via sampling biases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20314)
*Jingwen Liu,Ezra Edelman,Surbhi Goel,Bingbin Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了'小数据与大数据之间的差距'，发现减少样本重复使用反而能在训练中节省计算资源，这一现象在多种算法任务、模型架构和优化器中均被观察到，且无法用现有理论解释。作者认为，这种加速源于采样偏差带来的分层增长策略，尤其在数据量较小时更为显著。通过理论分析和多种干预实验的实证支持，研究指出使用较小数据集并多次重复并非仅是数据稀缺时的权宜之计，而可主动利用作为优化中的有利归纳偏置，尤其适用于推理任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 结合理论分析与多类干预实验（如改变采样策略、调整数据重复次数等），系统评估不同数据规模与重复频率对训练效率的影响，并分析其背后的分层增长机制。

Result: 在多种任务和模型设置下，小数据高重复策略显著降低计算开销，且性能不降反升；其优势主要来自采样偏差引发的有利分层增长模式。

Conclusion: 小数据高重复并非被动选择，而是一种可主动利用的优化策略，尤其在推理类任务中具有显著优势，为高效训练提供了新思路。

Abstract: This work investigates the ``small-vs-large gap'', where repeating on fewer samples can lead to compute saving during training compared to using a larger dataset. This is observed across algorithmic tasks, architectures and optimizers and cannot be explained using prior theory. We argue that the speedup comes from appropriate layer-wise growth enabled by sampling biases, which is more pronounced when the dataset size is smaller. We provide both theoretical analysis and empirical evidence from various interventions. Our results suggest that using a smaller dataset with more repetitions is not just a fallback strategy under data scarcity, but can be proactively leveraged as a favorable inductive biases for optimization, particularly in reasoning tasks.

### [213] [Causal Unlearning in Collaborative Optimization: Exact and Approximate Influence Reversal under Adversarial Contributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20341)
*Ali Mahdavi,Azadeh Zamanifar,Amirfarhad Farhadi,Omid Kashefi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: HF-KCU 是一种高效且精确的联邦学习数据删除方法，通过在克雷洛夫子空间中使用共轭梯度迭代近似影响函数，将复杂度从 O(d^3) 降低到 O(kd)，其中 k<<d。采用因果加权机制确保仅持有被删数据的客户端接收参数更新，防止对无关客户端的误修改。该方法具备对抗有界扰动的能力，支持在现实威胁模型下的稳定运行。在 ResNet-18、SimpleCNN、ViT-Lite 等架构上验证，于 CIFAR-10 上实现 47.75 倍加速，测试精度损失小于 0.60%，成员推断攻击成功率接近随机水平（0.499），证实隐私恢复有效性。理论分析提供收敛保证，误差以 O((k^{1/2}-1)/(k^{1/2}+1)) 速率下降。该方法适合异步、资源受限的生产级联邦系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 联邦学习需满足隐私法规中的数据删除要求，但每次删除后重新训练计算成本过高，亟需高效且精准的数据移除机制。

Method: 提出 HF-KCU 方法，利用共轭梯度在克雷洛夫子空间中近似影响函数，结合因果加权机制仅更新涉及被删数据的客户端，并具备对 Hessian 和梯度扰动的鲁棒性。

Result: 在 CIFAR-10 (Dirichlet, alpha=0.5) 上实现 47.75 倍速度提升，测试准确率与基线相差不超过 0.60%；成员推断攻击成功率降至 0.499，表明隐私恢复有效；理论证明了近似误差随迭代次数递减。

Conclusion: HF-KCU 实现了高效、精准、可解释的数据删除，在保障模型性能和隐私的同时，适用于异步、资源受限的生产环境，是可行的联邦学习数据删除解决方案。

Abstract: Federated learning systems must support data deletion requests to comply with privacy regulations, yet retraining from scratch after each deletion is computationally prohibitive. We present HF-KCU, a method that removes a client's contribution by approximating the influence function through conjugate gradient iterations in Krylov subspaces, reducing complexity from O(d^3) to O(kd) where k<<d.A causal weighting mechanism ensures that only clients holding the deleted data receive parameter updates, preventing spurious changes to unaffected clients. Our method is designed to handle bounded adversarial perturbations to the Hessian and gradient, providing graceful degradation under realistic threat models. We validate HF-KCU across convolutional (ResNet-18, SimpleCNN) and transformer (ViT-Lite) architectures on CIFAR-10, MNIST, and Fashion-MNIST. On CIFAR-10 under Dirichlet (alpha=0.5) partitioning, HF-KCU achieves 47.75 times speedup over retraining while maintaining test accuracy within 0.60% of the rational baseline(71.16 vs 71.76 %). Membership inference attacks on the forget set yield success rates of 0.499 matching the retrained model and confirming effective privacy restoration. We provide convergence guarantees showing that the Krylov approximation error decreases as O((k ^1/2-1)/(k^1/2+1)) where k is the Hessian condition number. The causal weighting mechanism ensures surgical updates, where only clients holding deleted data are modified, preserving model quality for unaffected participants and avoiding the instability of gradient-based approaches in asynchronous federated settings. This design provides interpretability as each update is directly traceable to the influence of the deleted data. The method's efficiency and precision make it suitable for production federated systems where deletion requests arrive asynchronously and computational budgets are constrained.

### [214] [Symmetrization of Loss Functions for Robust Training of Neural Networks in the Presence of Noisy Labels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20347)
*Alexandre Lemire Paquin,Brahim Chaib-Draa,Philippe Giguère*

TL;DR: 本文研究了多分类场景下标签噪声的鲁棒损失函数设计，提出通过损失函数对称化方法构造具有理论保障的损失。重点分析了交叉熵损失的对称化形式，导出多分类的无铰链损失（unhinged loss），并证明其在特定条件下是唯一的凸对称损失。该损失在得分向量相等时作为任意对称损失的线性近似，具有基础局部性质。进一步提出SGCE和alpha-MAE两种插值损失，可在多分类无铰链损失与平均绝对误差之间调节，并控制平滑性。实验表明其在标准噪声标签数据集上表现优于现有方法。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标注训练数据成本高且易出错，因此需要设计对标签噪声鲁棒的损失函数。对称性条件可提供理论上的鲁棒性保证，但现有方法在多分类场景下的对称损失设计尚不充分，亟需系统研究。

Method: 基于损失函数的唯一分解：对任意多分类损失函数进行对称分量与类无关项的分解，通过对交叉熵损失进行对称化处理，推导出多分类无铰链损失。利用凸性与对称性约束，证明其唯一性；通过线性逼近分析其局部特性。引入新损失函数SGCE与alpha-MAE，实现对无铰链损失与MAE之间的平滑插值，并控制beta-平滑性。

Result: 提出的多分类无铰链损失满足对称性条件且为唯一凸对称损失，具有重要的局部近似性质；SGCE与alpha-MAE在多个标准噪声标签基准上表现出竞争力，优于或接近现有鲁棒损失函数。

Conclusion: 通过对损失函数的对称化分析，本文揭示了多分类无铰链损失的理论地位与局部作用，提出的新损失函数有效平衡了鲁棒性与平滑性，在噪声标签学习中展现出良好性能。

Abstract: Labeling a training set is often expensive and susceptible to errors, making the design of robust loss functions for label noise an important problem. The symmetry condition provides theoretical guarantees for robustness to such noise. In this work, we study a symmetrization method arising from the unique decomposition of any multi-class loss function into a symmetric component and a class-insensitive term. In particular, symmetrizing the cross-entropy loss leads to a linear multi-class extension of the unhinged loss. Unlike in the binary case, the multi-class version must have specific coefficients in order to satisfy the symmetry condition. Under suitable assumptions, we show that this multi-class unhinged loss is the unique convex multi-class symmetric loss. We also show that it has a fundamental local role: the linear approximation of any symmetric loss around score vectors with equal components is equivalent to the multi-class unhinged loss. We then introduce SGCE and alpha-MAE, two loss functions that interpolate between the multi-class unhinged loss and the Mean Absolute Error while allowing control of the beta-smoothness of the loss. Experiments on standard noisy-label benchmarks show competitive performance compared with existing robust loss functions.

### [215] [Consistently Informative Soft-Label Temperature for Knowledge Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20357)
*Hoang-Chau Luong,Nghia Van Vo,Kaiqi Zhao,Lingwei Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出CIST方法，通过为教师和学生分配独立的样本自适应温度，解决标准知识蒸馏中固定温度导致的软标签熵不一致问题，提升蒸馏效果并保持低计算开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准知识蒸馏中的固定温度设计是样本无关的，导致教师软标签的熵不一致，部分预测过于尖锐或过度平滑，且教师与学生间强制统一温度限制了不同容量模型间的灵活匹配。

Method: 提出CIST（Consistently Informative Soft-label Temperature），为教师和学生分别设计样本级自适应温度，并根据教师置信度和学生学习难度重加权蒸馏目标，实现更一致的信息性软标签。

Result: 在视觉和语言任务上，CIST显著优于标准KD和强基线方法，在保持极低计算开销的前提下实现了稳定提升。

Conclusion: CIST通过自适应温度机制有效缓解了固定温度带来的信息不一致问题，提供了理论支持和实证优势，是一种高效且通用的知识蒸馏改进方案。

Abstract: Knowledge distillation (KD) transfers knowledge from a high-capacity teacher to a compact student by matching their predictive distributions, with temperature scaling serving as a central mechanism for smoothing teacher predictions and exposing informative "dark knowledge" beyond the hard label. However, the standard fixed-temperature design is inherently sample-agnostic. Since samples differ in logit scale and learning difficulty, a single global temperature produces teacher soft labels with highly inconsistent entropy: some predictions remain overly sharp and provide limited inter-class information, whereas others become over-smoothed and lose class-discriminative information. Moreover, sharing the same temperature between teacher and student further imposes rigid logit-scale alignment despite their capacity mismatch. To address these limitations, we propose CIST (Consistently Informative Soft-label Temperature), which assigns separate sample-wise adaptive temperatures to the teacher and student. This design produces consistently informative teacher soft labels while relaxing rigid teacher--student logit-scale matching. It also reweights the distillation objective according to teacher confidence and student learning difficulty. Theoretically, we show that teacher-label entropy is largely governed by the ratio between the maximum teacher logit and the temperature, providing a principled basis for adaptive smoothing. Empirically, CIST mitigates the inconsistency induced by fixed temperature, and experiments on both vision and language distillation tasks show consistent improvements over standard KD and strong baselines with negligible computational overhead.

### [218] [Decomposing MXFP4 quantization error for LLM reinforcement learning: reducible bias, recoverable deadzone, and an irreducible floor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20402)
*Xiaocan Li,Shiliang Wu,Zheng Shen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MXFP4量化可显著加速大语言模型的强化学习后训练，但量化误差导致严重精度下降。本文首次提出量化误差的三重精确分解，揭示其由‘尺度偏置’、‘死区截断’和‘网格噪声’三部分构成，分别影响梯度准确性、回放质量与策略熵。通过针对性修正：宏块缩放减少尺度偏置，异常值回退恢复死区数据并部分缓解偏置，自适应量化噪声控制熵，成功在Qwen2.5-3B和Qwen3-30B-A3B-Base模型上将精度恢复至BF16水平的0.7%和3.0%以内。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将量化误差视为单一噪声，忽略了其对强化学习不同训练路径的差异化影响。为提升MXFP4量化下大语言模型强化学习的精度，需深入理解误差来源及其作用机制。

Method: 提出量化误差的三重分解理论，识别出尺度偏置（幂次舍入）、死区截断（小值归零）和网格噪声（4位格点舍入）三种成分，并设计对应修正策略：宏块缩放、异常值回退与自适应量化噪声（AQN）。

Result: 在Qwen2.5-3B和Qwen3-30B-A3B-Base模型上，所提方法使量化后训练精度分别恢复至BF16基准的0.7%和3.0%以内，显著缓解了量化带来的性能损失。

Conclusion: 通过理论分解量化误差并设计针对性修正机制，可有效缓解MXFP4量化在强化学习训练中的多维度负面影响，实现接近全精度的性能表现。

Abstract: MXFP4 arithmetic can dramatically accelerate reinforcement learning (RL) post-training of large language models (LLMs), yet the quantization error introduces severe accuracy degradation. Existing work treats the quantization error as a monolithic noise term, missing the distinct mechanisms upon interpreting how quantization error damages training. We prove an exact three-way decomposition of quantization error and show how each component dominates a distinct RL training pathway. Our theoretical and empirical analysis decomposes the MXFP4 quantization error into three additive components: "scale bias" from power-of-two rounding, "deadzone truncation" from zeroing small values, and "grid noise" from rounding to the nearest 4-bit grid. Each component dominates a distinct RL failure mode: scale bias accumulates multiplicatively through the backward pass, affecting gradient accuracy; deadzone truncation degrades rollout quality; and grid noise raises the policy's entropy. We combine corrections that are RL failure mode-targeted but not component-exclusive: Macro-block scaling to reduce scale bias, Outlier Fallback recovers deadzone entries, but also partially reduces scale bias induced error, and Adaptive Quantization Noise (AQN) for controlling the policy entropy. On Qwen2.5-3B dense and Qwen3-30B-A3B-Base mixture-of-experts model, the targeted corrections recover BF16 accuracy to within 0.7% and 3.0% respectively.

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) effectively aligns Large Language Models (LLMs) with aggregate human preferences but often fails to address the diverse and conflicting needs of individual users. Our contribution is the discovery of a universal spectral representation within LLMs, which is proven to be highly amenable to model merging. This theoretical insight enables a two-phase methodology: we first learn a basis of specialized policies offline, each focused on a distinct, fine-grained preference dimension. An online adaptation algorithm then efficiently ``soups'' these policies at inference time, either by merging their outputs or parameters, enabling rapid model adaptation without the need for costly online retraining w.r.t. tailored preference rewards. Experiments on online preference alignment benchmarks demonstrate that our method achieves significant performance improvements over existing state-of-the-art approaches, presenting a scalable and computationally efficient solution for dynamically adapting LLMs to individual user preferences.

### [220] [Supervised Latent Restructuring for Small-Data Quantum Learning in Plant Phenomics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20413)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: High-dimensional biological data often exhibit a severe mismatch between feature dimensionality and sample size, making reliable classification difficult in extremely small-data regimes. In these settings, kernel methods can lose discriminative power when latent compression fails to preserve class-separating structure. We study this problem in fine-grained plant phenomics and propose a hybrid workflow that compresses 1280-dimensional deep image embeddings into a 64-dimensional PCA space and then restructures them into an 11-dimensional supervised latent space using Linear Discriminant Analysis (LDA), followed by GPU-accelerated Quantum Kernel Alignment (QKA) on NVIDIA L40S hardware. Empirically, supervised latent restructuring substantially improves the geometric separability of the compressed representation, increasing the Silhouette coefficient from 0.003 in the raw embedding space and -0.006 in PCA-64 to 0.197 in the supervised LDA-11 space. However, downstream classical evaluation reveals a clear compression trade-off: Linear SVM and XGBoost improve in the restructured latent space, whereas RBF-SVM and Random Forest degrade under the same 11-dimensional bottleneck. Under a constrained optimization budget, QKA in this regime remains challenging, indicating that latent geometry alone is not sufficient for strong trainable quantum performance. These findings position representation geometry as a central design variable in small-data quantum learning and expose the practical difficulty of recovering nonlinear discriminative structure from aggressively compressed biological representations.

Abstract: We study whether multimodal large language models (MLLMs) can leverage crystallographic plane indices (Miller indices) as a structured latent representation for reasoning about fracture geometry. *Sven Kruschel,Julian Rosenberger,Lasse Bohlen,Mathias Kraus,Patrick Zschech*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了对话式可解释人工智能（XAI）助手在提升用户预测准确性、模型理解及错误识别方面的效果。通过设计实验，比较对话式与问答式辅助方式对用户表现的影响。初步测试显示，参与者在两种辅助条件下均显著优于模型，但两者间无明显性能差异，且参与度较低。研究结果将用于优化后续大规模实验的设计，包括增强用户参与度的干预措施和探索提升预测表现的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有可解释AI技术虽旨在提供模型洞察并提升用户表现，但在实际应用中常未能达到预期效果。对话式XAI助手有望克服这些局限，但缺乏实证证据支持其对客观性能指标的影响。因此，亟需系统性评估不同解释辅助方式的有效性。

Method: 采用可解释性设计的预测模型，构建用户可通过识别并纠正系统性错误来超越模型的情境。通过实验对比对话式辅助与问答式辅助对用户表现的影响，测量预测准确率、模型理解程度及错误识别能力。

Result: 初步实验（N=42）表明，所有参与者均显著优于原始模型，但对话式与问答式辅助之间未发现性能差异，且整体用户参与度较低。

Conclusion: 当前辅助方式在提升用户表现方面有效，但存在参与度不足问题。未来研究需改进激励机制，并深入探究用户如何利用解释信息实现超越模型的表现。

Abstract: Explainable AI (XAI) techniques aim to provide insights into predictive models and enhance user performance, yet they often fall short of these expectations. Conversational XAI assistants promise to overcome such limitations, but empirical evidence on their impact on objective performance measures remains limited. We propose an experimental design for evaluating explanation assistance through prediction accuracy, model understanding, and error identification. Using an explainable-by-design prediction model, we create conditions where users can outperform the model by identifying and compensating for systematic errors. We compare conversational assistance against Q&A-based assistance to assess which better supports users in working with model explanations. Preliminary results from testing our experimental design show that participants (N=42) in both treatments significantly outperformed the model but reveal no performance differences between assistance types and modest engagement overall. These findings inform refinements for our planned full study, including enhanced engagement interventions and investigation of the mechanisms driving improved predictions.

### [223] [Weight Decay Regimes in Grokking Transformers: Cheap Online Diagnostics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20441)
*Lucky Verma*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究发现，经过模运算训练的Transformer模型在记忆、泛化和崩溃之间表现出明显的相变。权重衰减作为控制这些状态的标量参数，通过两个低成本在线诊断（注意力头之间的平均余弦相似度和熵标准差）可追踪训练动态，且计算成本低于损失景观分析。在11种实验条件和三种模型规模下，权重衰减轴清晰划分了三个阶段：记忆、发展性理解（developmental grokking）和崩溃。通过逻辑拟合确定记忆到发展性的临界点为 $λ_c=0.0158$（95%置信区间 [0.0109, 0.0200]），幂律拟合得到经验指数 $ν=0.757$（置信区间 [0.725, 0.799]），该值与已知理论模型（如 $ν=1/2$ 和3D伊辛模型 $ν\approx 0.63$）不一致，因此暂定为经验结果，待更密集的有限尺度缩放研究进一步确认。多任务复制实验（n=280，四种模运算）验证了权重衰减控制模式的稳定性；在 $λ=0.05$ 下，注意力头重新初始化显著改变第二阶段振幅（Cohen's $d=-1.190$, p=4.5×10⁻³），而权重范数剪裁则无此效应。跨架构探测（4层MLP、LSTM、Mamba）也再现了权重衰减控制的相变，但存在架构特异性临界值。主要结论限于小规模Transformer注意力模型中的模运算任务，非注意力实验仅为范围探针，关于通用架构、语言模型或普适类的主张超出本研究范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索小型Transformer模型在模运算任务中训练过程中的相变现象，理解权重衰减如何调控记忆、泛化与崩溃等不同行为模式，并开发低成本、高效的在线诊断工具以监测训练动态。

Method: 通过系统调节权重衰减系数 $\lambda$，在多种模型规模（0.82M至85M参数）和实验条件下训练Transformer模型，观察其在模运算任务上的表现。引入两个基于注意力激活的在线诊断指标：平均成对注意力头余弦相似度与熵标准差。采用逻辑回归拟合定位记忆-发展性过渡点，幂律拟合估计临界指数 $\nu$。进行多任务复制、注意力头重初始化与权重范数剪裁对比实验，以及跨架构（MLP、LSTM、Mamba）测试以验证结果稳健性。

Result: 权重衰减 $\lambda$ 有效控制模型从记忆到发展性理解再到崩溃的三阶段转变。临界值 $\lambda_c = 0.0158$ 被精确估计，幂律指数 $\nu = 0.757$ 显著偏离经典理论模型，提示可能为新经验规律。诊断指标能有效追踪训练状态变化，且计算成本低。跨架构实验显示相变模式普遍存在，但临界值随架构变化。重初始化显著影响相位行为，而权重剪裁不影响，表明结构敏感性。

Conclusion: 权重衰减是调控小规模Transformer在模运算任务中训练相变的关键控制参数。两个轻量级诊断工具可高效追踪训练动态。经验临界指数 $\nu \approx 0.757$ 表明可能存在尚未识别的普适类，需未来更精细的有限尺寸标度研究支持。研究结果具有跨架构可迁移性，但结论不适用于大规模语言模型或普遍性分类。

Abstract: Transformers trained on modular arithmetic exhibit sharp transitions between memorization, generalization, and collapse. We show that weight decay acts as a scalar empirical control parameter for these regimes, and introduce two cheap online diagnostics, mean pairwise attention-head cosine similarity and entropy standard deviation, that track training dynamics from attention activations alone and complement loss-landscape diagnostics at lower compute cost. Across eleven experimental conditions and three model scales (0.82M to 85M parameters), the weight-decay axis separates memorization, developmental grokking, and collapse. A near-transition logistic fit localizes the memorization-to-developmental boundary at $λ_c=0.0158$ (95% CI [0.0109, 0.0200], N=210); a power-law fit gives an empirical exponent $ν=0.757$ (CI [0.725, 0.799]). Reference exponents $ν=1/2$ and 3D Ising $ν\approx 0.63$ lie outside this empirical CI under our four-bin grid, so we report $ν$ as empirical and defer universality-class identification to denser finite-size-scaling work. A horizon-matched multi-task replication (n=280, four modular operations) preserves the weight-decay control pattern; a paired attention-head re-initialization experiment at $λ=0.05$ changes Phase-2 amplitude (Cohen's $d=-1.190$, n=10, $p_t=4.5 \times 10^{-3}$), while matched weight-norm clipping does not. Three cross-architecture probes (4L MLP, 4L LSTM, and 4L Mamba; each n=70) replicate the weight-decay-controlled transition with architecture-specific $λ_c$ values. Main diagnostic claims are scoped to modular arithmetic in small transformer attention models; the non-attention experiments are scope probes, and architecture-wide, language-model, and universality-class claims are out of scope.

</details>


### [224] [LLM Pretraining Shapes a Generalizable Manifold: Insights into Cross-Modal Transfer to Time Series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20449)
*Alexis Roger,Prateek Humane,Zhenghan Tai,Gwen Legate,Andrei Mircea,Vasilii Feofanov,Irina Rish*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 语言预训练的Transformer可通过跨模态迁移成为有效的时间序列预测器，因其在预训练中构建了可复用的流形结构。冻结LLM状态的线性探测即可解码真实时间序列轨迹，无需成对监督；在该投影空间中的检索可实现具有竞争力的预测。预训练初始化改善优化过程，产生连贯梯度和高度各向异性的损失景观，而微调则作为低维对齐，重用已有方向而非从头学习时间模式。低秩更新、子空间对齐及周期性、趋势和重复性的共享特征均支持此几何解释：语言预训练构建流形，微调将数值动态投影到任务相关方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索语言预训练的Transformer能否有效用于时间序列预测，并揭示其背后机制。

Method: 通过线性探测、检索、损失景观分析、微调更新特性分析等方法，研究预训练模型在时间序列任务中的表现与内在机制。

Result: 冻结的LLM状态可无监督解码时间序列轨迹，预训练初始化显著改善优化，微调仅需低维对齐即可实现有效预测，且存在共享的时间模式特征。

Conclusion: 语言预训练通过构建可复用的几何流形，为时间序列预测提供先验结构；微调仅需将数值动态投影至任务相关方向，实现了高效的跨模态迁移。

Abstract: Can language-pretrained transformers become effective time-series forecasters, and why? In this paper, we show that cross-modal transfer arises because language pretraining preconditions time series training with a reusable manifold. A linear probe on frozen LLM states decodes realistic time-series trajectories without paired supervision, and retrieval in this projected space yields competitive forecasts, showing that structure and dynamics exist before finetuning. Pretrained initialization also improves optimization, producing coherent gradients and a highly anisotropic loss landscape unlike random initialization. Finetuning then acts as low-dimensional alignment, reusing existing directions rather than learning temporal primitives from scratch, as evidenced by low-rank updates, subspace alignment, and shared features for periodicity, trend, and repetition. Together, these results support a geometric account of LLM-to-time-series transfer: language pretraining builds the manifold, and finetuning projects numerical dynamics onto task-relevant directions.

### [225] [CASCADE Conformal Prediction: Uncertainty-Adaptive Prediction Intervals for Two-Stage Clinical Decision Support](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20468)
*Ricardo Diaz-Rincon,Muxuan Liang,Adolfo Ramirez-Zamora,Benjamin Shickel*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为CASCADE的新颖的置信预测框架，用于帕金森病药物剂量管理中的不确定性量化。该方法通过利用分类任务中的认知不确定性来动态调整回归任务的预测区间，实现了连续的风险适应。与传统方法相比，该框架在高置信度患者中可使预测区间缩小38.9%，同时自动扩大不确定情况下的区间以确保覆盖性，有效衔接了临床决策与剂量预测之间的差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 帕金森病的药物管理因疾病进展异质性、患者反应差异和药物副作用而具有挑战性。现有AI模型虽能预测左旋多巴等效每日剂量（LEDD），但标准不确定性量化无法有效传达预测可靠性，导致高低置信度的临床决策被同等对待。

Method: CASCADE框架基于置信预测，将主分类任务（判断是否需要调整药物）的认知不确定性通过Venn-Abers多概率不确定性映射为非符合性分数，并用于动态缩放次级回归任务（预测剂量变化量）的预测区间，实现连续风险适应。

Result: 实验表明，CASCADE在高置信度患者中生成的预测区间比标准置信基线窄38.9%，同时在不确定病例中自动扩展区间以保证稳健覆盖，显著提升了预测效率与临床实用性。

Conclusion: CASCADE通过将认知不确定性从分类任务传递至回归任务，实现了对帕金森病药物剂量预测的自适应不确定性量化，既提高了高置信度预测的精度，又保障了低置信度情况下的安全性，为临床决策支持提供了更可靠、灵活的工具。

Abstract: Effective medication management in Parkinson's Disease (PD) is challenging due to heterogeneous disease progression, variable patient response, and medication side effects. While AI models can forecast levodopa equivalent daily dose (LEDD) as a measure of medication needs, standard uncertainty quantification often fails to communicate the reliability of these predictions, treating high and low confidence clinical decisions identically. We introduce CASCADE (Calibrated Adaptive Scaling via Conformal And Distributional Estimation), a novel conformal prediction framework that propagates epistemic uncertainty from a screening classifier to adapt downstream predictions. Unlike standard conformal methods that rely on auxiliary residual regression, we leverage epistemic uncertainty from a primary classification task (identifying whether a medication change is needed) to dynamically scale the prediction intervals of a secondary regression task (predicting how much change). By mapping Venn-Abers multi-probabilistic uncertainty directly to non-conformity scores, our framework achieves continuous risk adaptation. We demonstrate that this ``cascade effect'' produces highly efficient intervals for confident patients (38.9% narrower than standard conformal baselines) while automatically expanding intervals to ensure robust coverage for uncertain cases, bridging the gap between discrete clinical decision-making and continuous dose forecasting in PD.

### [226] [ZEBRA: Zero-shot Budgeted Resource Allocation for LLM Orchestration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20485)
*May Hamri,Inbal Talgam-Cohen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ZEBRA 是一个零样本框架，将多阶段预算分配问题转化为连续非线性背包问题。通过 LLM 控制器估计各阶段的效用曲线，并利用拉格朗日乘子的水填充搜索法确定最优预算分配。该方法统一处理加性和乘性聚合，显著优于直接由 LLM 分配预算的方法，在多个任务上表现出更高的效率与鲁棒性，且能根据任务结构自适应调整分配策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法无法在多智能体流水线中动态分配预算，而实际应用中需在固定预算下高效利用资源，因此亟需一种能在推理时灵活分配预算的机制。

Method: 使用 LLM 作为控制器估计各阶段的效用曲线，将预算分配问题建模为连续非线性背包问题，采用水填充算法结合拉格朗日乘子求解最优分配方案。

Result: 在 APPS 编程基准上，ZEBRA 在预算为 0.5 时恢复了 94.4% 的无约束性能，优于 LLM-direct 的 88.1%；在 HotpotQA 多阶段任务中，提升达 14.3 个百分点，且对效用曲线估计噪声具有鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 轻量级的算法指导可在推理时显著提升多智能体系统的经济效率，ZEBRA 能根据任务结构自适应分配预算，展现出良好的泛化能力与实用性。

Abstract: As autonomous agents increasingly execute end-to-end tasks under fixed monetary budgets, the pressing open question shifts from whether the budget is respected, to how to spend it effectively. Existing budget-aware methods typically control reasoning step-by-step within a single agent, or learn resource allocation policies via RL. None address how to split a budget across the composing phases of a multi-agent pipeline at inference time. We propose ZEBRA, a zero-shot framework that reduces multi-phase budget allocation to a continuous nonlinear knapsack problem: an LLM controller estimates per-phase utility curves, and a water-filling search on the Lagrange multiplier returns the per-phase split. Additive and multiplicative aggregations are unified under the same solver. On a $150$-task APPS coding benchmark, both ZEBRA variants outperform LLM-direct (budget allocation directly by an LLM) on every aggregate metric. At a budget of $α= 0.5$ of the unconstrained spend, ZEBRA recovers $94.4\%$ of unconstrained quality, versus $88.1\%$ for LLM-direct. The advantage is statistically significant and transfers beyond coding: on a $3$-phase HotpotQA pipeline, ZEBRA beats LLM-direct by $14.3$pp, with allocations empirically robust to curve-estimation noise. On HotpotQA, ZEBRA arrives at a different budget split (near-balanced) compared to the APPS one (skewed towards a refinement phase), showing adaptation to the pipeline structure. More broadly, we show that lightweight algorithmic guidance at inference time can improve the economic behavior of autonomous multi-agent systems.

### [227] [Tippett-minimum Fusion of Representation-space Diffusion Models for Multi-Encoder Out-of-Distribution Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20502)
*Neelkamal Bhuyan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出一种多编码器融合的表示空间扩散模型（RDM）方法，通过统计识别各编码器对不同分布偏移的敏感性，引入无需OOD标签的编码器无关两级$\min(\cdot)$门控机制EncMin2L，以更低参数成本实现更优的OOD检测性能。利用两种基于ID数据的诊断工具$η^2$和$Δμ$量化编码器专长，结合Tippett最小p值合并策略生成稳定校准的OOD信号，实现四种分布偏移类型下均≥0.94 AUROC，优于现有最优方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有OOD检测方法在面对多种分布偏移（如全局域变化、语义差异、纹理不同、协变量损坏）时表现不佳，且多数依赖大量标注的OOD数据或高复杂度模型。亟需一种高效、通用且无需额外标注的多编码器融合框架，实现对各类分布偏移的统一鲁棒检测。

Method: 采用多编码器融合结构，每个编码器独立训练表示空间扩散模型（RDM），通过分析内部ID数据中特征响应的统计特性，识别其对特定分布偏移的敏感性；设计编码器无关的两级$\min(\cdot)$门控机制EncMin2L，动态组合并校准各编码器输出的扩散似然得分；使用$η^2$（类条件F检验）与$Δμ$（合成损坏下的对数似然变化）作为无监督诊断指标评估编码器专长；最终通过Tippett最小p值合并策略整合各编码器得分，生成整体稳健的OOD判别信号。

Result: EncMin2L在四种典型分布偏移（全局域变化、语义偏差、纹理差异、协变量损坏）上均达到≥0.94 AUROC，显著优于单体多编码器基线模型，且参数量仅为后者的1/2.3，验证了其高效性与泛化能力。在多个重叠基准上超越当前最优的表示空间扩散型OOD检测方法。

Conclusion: 本研究提出了一种基于多编码器融合与自适应门控的新型无监督OOD检测框架EncMin2L，仅依赖ID数据即可实现对多样化分布偏移的精准感知与检测，在性能与效率上均取得突破，为复杂现实场景中的鲁棒性模型部署提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: We address out-of-distribution (OOD) detection across the full spectrum of distribution shifts -- global domain changes, semantic divergence, texture differences, and covariate corruptions -- through a multi-encoder fusion of per-encoder representation-space diffusion models (RDMs). We statistically identify each encoder's sensitivity to specific shift types from ID data alone and introduce EncMin2L -- an encoder-agnostic two-level $\min(\cdot)$-gate that combines and calibrates per-encoder diffusion-based likelihood detectors without OOD labels, outperforming monolithic multi-encoder baselines at $2.3\times$ lower parameter cost. Two ID-data diagnostics: $η^2$ (class-conditional F-test) and $Δμ$ (log-likelihood shift under synthetic corruptions) -- quantify encoder specialization, while a Tippett minimum $p$-value combination aggregates per-encoder scores into a single, calibration-stable OOD signal. EncMin2L achieves $\geq 0.94$ AUROC across all four shift types simultaneously, outperforming the state-of-the-art representation-space diffusion OOD detectors across overlapping benchmarks.

### [228] [Reinforcing Human Behavior Simulation via Verbal Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20506)
*Weiwei Sun,Xuhui Zhou,Jiarui Liu,Weihua Du,Haojia Sun,Yiqing Xie,Qianou Ma,Sihao Chen,Mengting Wan,Longqi Yang,Pei Zhou,Sherry Wu,Sean Welleck,Graham Neubig,Yiming Yang,Maarten Sap*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DITTO 是一种通过将口头反馈作为强化学习中的首要信号来训练大型语言模型的方法，旨在使 LLM 更加拟人化。该方法在每次推理后接收口头反馈，并生成受反馈指导的改进版本，两者通过 GRPO 联合优化，将口头指导提炼到基础策略中，且无需在测试时再次提供反馈。研究还提出了 SOUL 基准，涵盖 10 个任务、6 个类别，用于评估人类行为模拟能力。DITTO 在平均性能上比基础模型提升 36%，并在 6/10 的 SOUL 基准上超越 GPT-5.4，证明了基于口头反馈的强化学习在训练拟人化 LLM 方面具有巨大潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大型语言模型在学习方面主要依赖可量化、客观的奖励信号（如代码或数学问题的正确性），但人类行为的学习更多依赖于主观、多维度的口头反馈。随着 LLM 被广泛用于模拟用户、患者、学生等角色，迫切需要让模型具备从口头反馈中学习的能力，以实现更真实的人类行为模拟。

Method: 提出 DITTO 模型，采用一种新的强化学习框架，将口头反馈视为第一类信号。每个推理周期后，模型接收口头反馈，并生成一个受反馈影响的改进输出。通过 GRPO（Generalized Reward Policy Optimization）联合优化原始输出和反馈引导的改进输出，实现对口头指导的隐式吸收，从而在不依赖反馈的情况下完成推理。同时构建 SOUL 基准数据集，覆盖多个模拟场景。

Result: DITTO 在平均性能上相比基础模型提升 36%，并在 6/10 的 SOUL 基准任务中优于 GPT-5.4，表明基于口头反馈的强化学习是训练拟人化语言模型的有效路径。

Conclusion: 通过将口头反馈作为核心学习信号，结合专门设计的训练框架与评估基准，DITTO 成功提升了语言模型在复杂社会行为模拟任务中的表现，验证了在非结构化、主观反馈下进行强化学习的可行性与有效性，为未来更具人性化的 AI 系统提供了新方向。

Abstract: Humans learn social norms and behaviors from verbal feedback (e.g., a parent saying "that was rude" or a friend explaining "here's why that hurt"). Yet, learning from feedback for LLMs has largely focused on domains like code and math, where RL rewards are directly verifiable and condensed into scalar values. As LLMs are increasingly used to simulate human behavior, e.g., standing in for users, patients, students, and other personas, there is a pressing need to make them more human-like, which requires embracing a fundamentally different kind of signal: feedback that is verbal, subjective, and multi-faceted. We present DITTO, a model trained by treating verbal feedback as a first-class signal in reinforcement learning. After each rollout, DITTO receives verbal feedback and generates a feedback-conditioned improved rollout; both outputs are jointly optimized with GRPO, distilling verbal guidance into the base policy without requiring feedback at test time. We also introduce SOUL (Simulation gym Of hUman-Like behavior), a unified benchmark and training data suite spanning 10 tasks across six categories: Theory of Mind, character role play, social skill, learner simulation, user simulation, and persona simulation. DITTO achieves an average 36% improvement over the base model and exceeds GPT-5.4 on 6 of 10 SOUL benchmarks, demonstrating that RL with verbal feedback is a promising direction for training LLMs to simulate human behavior.

</details>


### [229] [Online Conformal Prediction with Corrupted Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20515)
*Bowen Wang,Matteo Zecchin,Osvaldo Simeone*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究在线共形预测（OCP）在反馈被污染情况下的鲁棒性问题。提出两种鲁棒方案：基于过滤的鲁棒OCP和基于主动补偿的鲁棒OCP，均能提供明确的误覆盖保证，并在独立随机翻转和有记忆限制的任意误差模型下进行分析。实验表明，在反馈污染条件下，新方法显著改善了校准性能并生成更小的预测集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准OCP依赖于对过去预测集覆盖率的精确反馈，但在实际中反馈可能因噪声、通信故障或对抗性操纵而被污染，导致校准保证失效。因此需要设计对反馈污染具有鲁棒性的OCP方法。

Method: 将反馈污染建模为任意二值翻转序列；提出两种鲁棒策略：1）利用预测阈值的结构特性进行反馈过滤；2）引入主动补偿机制以减轻污染影响。

Result: 所提方法在多种反馈污染模型下均能保持可靠的误覆盖保证；实验显示其在真实数据集上显著优于基线OCP方法，具有更好的校准性和更紧凑的预测集。

Conclusion: 提出的两种鲁棒OCP方法有效缓解了反馈污染对校准性能的影响，提升了OCP在非平稳、动态环境中的实用性与可靠性。

Abstract: Modern artificial intelligence systems require calibrated uncertainty estimates that remain reliable in sequential and non-stationary environments. Online conformal prediction (OCP) addresses this challenge through adaptively updated prediction sets that provide deterministic long-run miscoverage guarantees. These guarantees, however, hinge on the assumption of perfect feedback about the coverage of past prediction sets. In practice, the observed miscoverage indicator may be corrupted by noise, communication failures, or adversarial manipulation, which can severely degrade OCP's calibration guarantees. In this paper, we study OCP under corrupted feedback. We first model feedback corruption as an arbitrary binary flip sequence, and analyze how feedback corruption affects and degrades the miscoverage performance of standard OCP. We then propose two robust schemes: robust OCP via filtering, which leverages the structural properties of the predicted threshold to filter corrupted feedback, and robust OCP via active compensation, which incorporates an active compensation mechanism to mitigate the effect of corrupted feedback. For both methods, we establish explicit miscoverage guarantees, which are further specialized for an independent stochastic flip model and for an arbitrary error model with memory bounds. Experiments on real-world datasets validate the proposed approach, showing markedly improved calibration and significantly smaller prediction sets compared with baseline OCP methods under corrupted feedback.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Fine-tuning adapts a pretrained machine learning model to a small, sensitive dataset, but this process risks memorizing individual new data points, making the model vulnerable to adversaries who seek to extract sensitive information. In this work, we develop a randomized algorithm based on the exponential mechanism for fine-tuning while ensuring differential privacy. Our key idea is to construct a simple utility function that combines a local quadratic approximation of the pretrained model with information from the new dataset. The resulting exponential mechanism admits exact sampling from a multivariate normal distribution in closed form. We establish theoretical privacy guarantees, sensitivity bounds, and accuracy estimations for our method. We further introduce a random-projection strategy that makes the approach scalable to high-dimensional models. Numerical experiments on the MNIST benchmark and the MIMIC clinical dataset demonstrate competitive performance against existing differentially private fine-tuning techniques.

Abstract: Optimization algorithms are core methods by which machine learning models iteratively minimize loss functions, update parameters, learn from data, and improve performance. Momentum SGD and AdamW represent two important optimization paradigms. AdamW produces stable updates and usually has strong robustness across training scenarios, but its generalization performance is sometimes weaker than that of momentum methods. Momentum SGD can often obtain better generalization after careful tuning, but it is more sensitive to gradient-scale variation and hyperparameter settings. To balance the strengths and weaknesses of the two paradigms, this paper proposes Ada2MS, an optimization algorithm that achieves a smooth transition between AdamW-like behavior and momentum-SGD-like behavior through continuous exponential interpolation between elementwise second-moment estimates and global second-moment estimates. On the visual tasks evaluated in this study, Ada2MS obtains competitive results under a unified optimizer-comparison protocol. The code will be released at https://github.com/mengzhu0308/Ada2MS

### [233] [Latent Process Generator Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20547)
*Lukas Billera,Hedwig Nora Nordlinder,Ben Murrell*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为潜在过程生成匹配（Latent Process Generator Matching）的通用框架，将观测生成状态视为可处理马尔可夫过程 $Y_t$ 的确定性映射 $X_t = \Phi(Y_t)$。该框架允许学习图像空间中具有与投影过程相同单时刻边缘分布的生成器，从而推广并涵盖现有文献中的离散潜在过程结果，将生成匹配理论从静态潜变量扩展到更丰富的时变潜在条件过程。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出潜在过程生成匹配框架，将观测状态 $X_t$ 建模为可处理马尔可夫过程 $Y_t$ 的确定性函数 $\Phi(Y_t)$，并通过投影方式学习图像空间中的生成器，使其满足与投影过程相同的单时刻边缘分布。

Result: 证明了在该框架下可以学习到与投影过程具有相同单时刻边缘分布的生成器；该方法推广并包含已有离散潜在过程的结果，并将生成匹配理论从静态潜变量扩展至时变潜变量情形。

Abstract: Many recent flow-matching and diffusion-style generative models rely on auxiliary stochastic dynamics during training: a richer process is simulated to define conditional targets, but the auxiliary state is either intractable to sample at generation time or simply not part of the desired output. Existing Generator Matching theory formalises conditioning on static latent random variables, and several recent papers prove special cases of projection results for particular augmented-state constructions. We introduce latent process generator matching, a general framework that treats the observed generative state as a deterministic image $X_t=Φ(Y_t)$ of a tractable Markov process $Y_t$. We show that in this setting one may learn the generator of a stochastic process on the image space which has the same one-time marginal distributions as the projected process. This generalizes and subsumes the discrete latent process results from the literature, and extends Generator Matching from static latent variables to a rich family of time-dependent latent conditional processes.

### [235] [ReversedQ: Opportunities for Faster Q-Learning in Episodic Online Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20592)

Abstract: We study model-free Q-learning in finite-horizon episodic Markov Decision Processes (MDPs) with stationary dynamics across episodes. We identify a central issue in nascent model-free posterior-sampling works: the reliance on delayed learning in order to prove theoretical guarantees. In particular, we identify three opportunities for faster learning - (i) value-function update order, (ii) update frequencies, and (iii) value-function initialization. Abstract: Compositional generalization is essential for reaching unseen goals under novel contextual variations in offline goal-conditioned reinforcement learning (GCRL), where a generalist goal-reaching agent must be learned from limited data. Most prior approaches pursue this via trajectory stitching over temporally contiguous segments, which limits composing behaviors across varying contexts. To overcome this limitation, we formalize analogy transduction as synthesizing new plans by composing task-endogenous analogies with given contexts and propose a novel analogy representation tailored for it. Grounded in our theory, this analogy representation captures what changes under optimal task execution, remains invariant to contextual variations, and is sufficient for optimal goal reaching. We further contend that generalization to unseen analogy-context pairs is a practical obstacle in analogy transduction, and introduce a new approach for offline GCRL that enables analogy transduction beyond seen pairs to unseen combinations. We empirically demonstrate the effectiveness of our approach on OGBench manipulation environments, substantially outperforming prior methods that do not perform analogy transduction. ### [237] [Matryoshka Concept Bottleneck Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20612)
*Ziye Chen,Hongbin Lin,Xinyue Xu,Jie Li,Lijie Hu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为Matryoshka Concept Bottleneck Model (MCBM)的统一架构，通过嵌套层次化的概念结构实现可适应的概念利用，显著降低测试时干预成本，理论和实验证明其在保持性能的同时将干预成本从线性降至对数级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有CBM方法受限于静态概念集或需为不同概念预算训练多个模型，导致人工标注成本高、计算与维护开销大，亟需一种能动态适应概念粒度且无需重训的解决方案。

Method: 受俄罗斯套娃表示学习启发，将概念按最大相关性与最小冗余组织成嵌套层次结构，支持多层级推理；通过设计统一模型实现不同概念粒度下的自适应推理，避免重复训练。

Result: 理论上证明干预成本由$O(K)$降为$O(\log K)$，且性能单调提升；实验表明性能媲美独立训练的模型，同时支持高效、灵活的专家交互。

Conclusion: MCBM提供了一种高效、可扩展的解释性深度学习框架，解决了传统CBM在实际部署中因干预成本过高而难以应用的问题。

Abstract: Concept Bottleneck Models (CBMs) have emerged as a prominent paradigm for interpretable deep learning, learning by grounding predictions in human-understandable concepts. However, their practical deployment is hindered by the high cost of test-time intervention, as correcting model errors typically requires human experts to manually inspect and verify a large set of predicted concepts. Existing approaches suffer from a fundamental structural limitation: they either adopt a single static concept set, forcing experts to exhaustively annotate concepts and incurring prohibitive intervention costs, or train multiple models tailored to different concept budgets, resulting in substantial computational and maintenance overhead. To address this challenge, we propose the Matryoshka Concept Bottleneck Model (MCBM), a unified architecture that enables adaptive concept utilization within a single model. Inspired by Matryoshka Representation Learning, MCBM organizes concepts into a nested hierarchy based on maximum relevance and minimum redundancy, allowing inference at multiple levels of conceptual granularity without retraining. Theoretically, we show that MCBM reduces the expected intervention costs from linear to logarithmic order, $O(\log K)$, while guaranteeing monotonic performance improvement. Empirically, extensive experiments demonstrate that MCBM matches the performance of independently trained models while enabling dynamic and efficient expert interaction.

</details>


### [238] [SURF: Steering the Scalarization Weight to Uniformly Traverse the Pareto Front](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20619)
*Liuyuan Jiang,Chentong Huang,Lisha Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出SURF（Sampling Uniformly along the PaReto Front），一种基于几何分析的多目标优化中实现帕累托前沿（PF）均匀覆盖的方法。通过分析标量权重变化时解在PF上的遍历速度，构建弧长累积分布函数（CDF），并逆向该CDF以获得最优权重采样规则。针对结构化问题（如双目标强化学习），推导出闭式表达式；对于一般问题，则采用交替进行CDF重建与权重采样。理论证明在特定条件下SURF线性收敛至有限采样下界。实验表明，在多目标强化学习、多目标游戏环境及大模型对齐任务中，SURF显著优于基线方法，实现了更均匀的帕累托前沿覆盖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有标量法在多目标优化中虽简单高效，但均匀采样标量权重常导致帕累托前沿覆盖不均。本文旨在解决这一偏差问题，实现对帕累托前沿的均匀采样，以更好反映用户偏好多样性。

Method: 通过几何分析揭示标量权重变化时解在帕累托前沿上的非均匀遍历速度，建立弧长累积分布函数（CDF），并逆向该函数得到理想的权重采样策略。针对结构化问题推导闭式解；对于通用问题，采用迭代式CDF重建与权重采样。

Result: 理论上，SURF在满足条件时可线性收敛至不可避免的有限采样误差下界；实验上，在多目标强化学习、多目标游戏和大模型对齐任务中，相较于基线方法，SURF显著提升了帕累托前沿的均匀覆盖效果。

Conclusion: SURF是一种基于帕累托前沿感知的权重采样方法，能够有效克服传统标量法带来的覆盖不均问题。其理论保证和实证表现表明，该方法在多目标优化中具有高度实用性和优越性。

Abstract: Scalarization is widely used in multi-objective optimization owing to its simplicity and scalability. In many applications, the goal is to generate solutions that represent diverse user preferences, ideally with uniform coverage of the Pareto front (PF). However, uniformly sampling scalarization weights usually induces non-uniform coverage of the PF. We explain this mismatch through a geometric analysis of the scalarization path. As the scalarization weight varies, the corresponding solutions trace the PF with a generally non-uniform traversal speed. This speed induces an arc-length cumulative distribution function (CDF); inverting this CDF map yields a principled rule for selecting weights that produce uniform PF coverage. Building on this insight, we propose SURF (Sampling Uniformly along the PaReto Front). For structured problems, including bi-objective bandits, we derive closed-form expressions for this CDF map and the resulting PF-aware weight sampling rule. For general problems, SURF alternates between CDF reconstruction and weight sampling. Theoretically, we show that under provable conditions, SURF converges linearly to an unavoidable finite-sampling floor. Empirically, experiments on bandits, multi-objective-gymnasium, and multi-objective LLM alignment demonstrate that SURF efficiently achieves more uniform PF coverage than baselines.

</details>


### [239] [Dynamic Shapley Computation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20620)
*Xuan Yang,Hsi-Wen Chen,Ming-Syan Chen,Jian Pei*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: D-Shap 是一种动态数据估值框架，通过将 Shapley 值表示为玩家-任务矩阵，利用任务与玩家之间的局部性，实现高效更新。它支持快速任务添加和玩家变更，显著降低计算成本，同时保持高估值质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 Shapley 值计算方法在动态环境中效率低下，因每次变动需重新计算全部值，缺乏可复用性。本文旨在解决这一问题，提升数据估值在动态场景下的实用性。

Method: 将 Shapley 值建模为玩家-任务矩阵，利用任务依赖的局部性和相似任务的估值相似性，提出结构感知插值与局部块更新机制；引入自估值机制，无需预设任务即可从训练数据构建初始矩阵。

Result: 实验表明，D-Shap 在任务更新上仅需毫秒级时间，玩家更新成本降低达三个数量级，且估值质量接近全量重算水平。

Conclusion: D-Shap 通过结构化矩阵维护与局部性利用，实现了高效、可扩展的动态数据估值，在实际应用中具备显著优势。

Abstract: Shapley-based data valuation provides a principled way to quantify the contribution of training data, but its high computational cost makes it impractical in dynamic settings where tasks and training players evolve. Existing methods treat Shapley computation as a one-shot process and collapse contributions into aggregated scores, preventing reuse and requiring recomputation under any change. We introduce a new perspective that represents Shapley values as a player-by-task matrix and formulates dynamic valuation as a structured matrix maintenance problem. We exploit the fact that each task depends on a small subset of training players and that similar tasks yield similar valuations, leading to utility locality and coalition locality. Based on these insights, we propose D-Shap, a dynamic valuation framework that enables efficient updates by modifying only a small portion of the matrix: new task valuations are inferred via structure-aware interpolation, while updates induced by new players are confined to affected local matrix blocks. To eliminate the need for pre-specified evaluation tasks, we introduce self-valuation, which constructs the initial matrix directly from training data, supported by scalable subset reuse and coverage-aware anchor selection. Experiments across diverse models show that D-Shap performs task updates in milliseconds and reduces the cost of player updates by up to three orders of magnitude, while achieving valuation quality competitive with full recomputation.

</details>

By dissecting these relationships, we clarify the broader theoretical significance of the localization method and demonstrate its practical applicability across diverse machine learning tasks. Furthermore, we explore advanced extensions of the framework, such as adaptive kernels, hierarchical local models, and non-local models. Notably, we show that the Transformer -- a cornerstone of modern sequence modeling -- can be constructed using hierarchical local models, revealing the ability of the localization method to unify and generalize state-of-the-art architectures. ### [241] [Same Target, Different Basins: Hard vs. Soft Labels for Annotator Distributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20642)
*Mirerfan Gheibi,Gashin Ghazizadeh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究在标注者存在分歧时，使用硬标签传递（hard-label delivery）作为软标签训练的替代方案。提出两种方法：多轮法（multipass）和随机标签采样（SLS），在标注数据稀疏时表现优于软标签训练，尤其当经验目标分布远离完整标注者分布时；当有完整标注分布时，两种方法与软标签训练效果相当。实验表明SLS与软标签交叉熵优化相同期望目标，且硬标签传递收敛到更平坦的极小值区域，支持其在OOD检测中的优越性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当标注者存在分歧时，这种分歧可能反映的是认知不确定性而非简单的标签噪声。传统方法如合并投票或直接基于经验软标签分布训练可能无法充分捕捉这一不确定性。因此，探索硬标签传递作为一种更有效的替代方案，以更好地利用标注分歧信息。

Method: 采用两种硬标签传递方法：多轮法（multipass）通过循环处理观察到的投票并保持数据集大小不变；随机标签采样（SLS）在每个训练周期开始时为每个样本随机采样一个标签。同时引入确定性控制和打乱SLS作为对照实验，评估不同方法的有效性。

Result: 在CIFAR-10H上，当每样本标注数较少时，硬标签传递显著优于软标签训练，尤其是在经验目标分布偏离完整标注分布的情况下；当拥有完整标注分布时，硬标签方法与软标签训练性能相当。SLS与软标签交叉熵优化相同的期望目标，且硬标签方法收敛至更平坦的极小值区域，在SVHN和CIFAR-100上的OOD检测任务中表现出更强鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 当原始投票计数可用时，多轮法是一个强而实用的默认选择；当仅有少量标注时，随机标签采样（SLS）提供了一种轻量级但性能仍具竞争力的替代方案，且在完整标注分布下可达到与软标签训练相当的效果。

Abstract: When annotators disagree, that disagreement can reflect epistemic uncertainty rather than simple label noise. We study hard-label delivery as an alternative to the usual choices of collapsing votes to a single label or training directly on the empirical soft-label distribution. We focus on two primary hard-label methods: multipass, which cycles through observed votes while keeping the dataset size fixed, and stochastic label sampling (SLS), which samples one label per example at the start of each epoch. On CIFAR-10H, we find that when only a small number of annotations per example is available, hard-label delivery improves over soft-label training, with larger improvements where the sparse empirical target is farther from the full annotator distribution. When full annotator distributions are available, both hard-label methods match soft-label training. We use deterministic control as an ablation of multipass and shuffled SLS as a control that breaks the example-to-distribution match. We also show that SLS and soft-label cross-entropy optimize the same expected objective. Hard-label delivery also converges to flatter basins, with supporting descriptive evidence from OOD detection on SVHN and CIFAR-100. Overall, these results suggest that multipass is a strong practical default when raw vote counts are available, while SLS offers a lightweight alternative that remains competitive when only a few votes per example are available and matches soft-label training when full annotator distributions are available.

</details>


### [242] [AVSD: Adaptive-View Self-Distillation by Balancing Consensus and Teacher-Specific Privileged Signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20643)
*Duy Nguyen,Hanqi Xiao,Archiki Prasad,Zaid Khan,Anirban Das,Austin Zhang,Sambit Sahu,Hyunji Lee,Elias Stengel-Eskin,Mohit Bansal*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: AVSD是一种新型的自蒸馏方法，通过融合多个具有特权信息的视角，分离出跨视角的稳定共识信号与视角特异性残差信号，以解决传统自蒸馏中因教师使用学生无法访问的私有信息而导致的不对称问题。该方法在数学竞赛和代码生成任务上均显著优于现有基线模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统自蒸馏方法存在教师使用学生在推理时无法获取的特权信息，导致训练与推理不一致；同时，不同任务适合的特权信息类型不同，难以选择单一最优视图。因此需要一种能联合处理多视角信息并自动识别可靠更新方向的方法。

Method: 提出AVSD（Adaptive-View Self-Distillation），通过分解监督信号为跨视角共识部分和视角特异性残差部分，仅当残差信号与共识方向一致且比例适当时才加入更新，从而实现更稳健、自适应的训练。

Result: 在AIME24、AIME25、HMMT25等数学竞赛基准上，AVSD在Qwen3-8B和Qwen3-4B上分别取得平均3.1%和2.2%的Avg@8提升；在Codeforces和LiveCodeBench v6代码生成任务上，相较单视角自蒸馏提升2.4%。

Conclusion: AVSD通过动态整合多视角特权信息，有效缓解了自蒸馏中的信息不对称问题，提升了模型在复杂任务上的性能，尤其在需要精确推理的任务中表现出更强的鲁棒性和泛化能力。

Abstract: Self-distillation enables language models to learn on-policy from their own trajectories by using the same model as both student and teacher, with the teacher being conditioned on privileged information unavailable to the student. Such information can come in different types or views, such as solutions, demonstrations, feedback, or final answers. This setup provides dense token-level feedback without relying on a separate external model, but creates a fundamental asymmetry: the teacher may rely on view-specific information that the student cannot access at inference time. Moreover, the best type of privileged information is often task-dependent, making it difficult to choose a single teacher view. In this work, we address both these challenges jointly by introducing AVSD (Adaptive-View Self-Distillation), a novel method of self-distillation with multiple privileged-information views, which reconstructs token-level supervision by separating stable cross-view consensus from view-specific residual signals. AVSD identifies the consensus signal shared across views, which provides a reliable update direction, and then selectively adds the view-specific residual signal to adjust the update magnitude when it both aligns with the consensus direction and remains proportionate to the consensus signal. Experiments on math competition benchmarks (AIME24, AIME25, and HMMT25) show that AVSD consistently outperforms both single-view self-distillation baselines and GRPO, achieving average Avg@8 gains of 3.1% and 2.2% over the strongest baselines on Qwen3-8B and Qwen3-4B, respectively. Moreover, on code-generation benchmarks (Codeforces, LiveCodeBench v6) using Qwen3-8B, AVSD outperforms the single-view self-distillation baseline by 2.4% on average.

</details>


### [243] [Design for Manufacturing: A Manufacturability Knowledge-Integrated Reinforcement Learning Framework for Free-Form Pipe Routing in Aeroengines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20644)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前航空发动机管道布局设计与下游制造过程脱节，导致需大量试错迭代，效率低且难以保证可制造性。亟需一种集成设计与制造知识的智能化方法，提升复杂管道设计的自动化水平与制造可行性。

Method: 基于弗雷内坐标系建立管道路径的边界值问题，用曲率与扭转参数表示路径，通过三次埃尔米特插值生成连续路径；将制造知识（如最大曲率/扭转限制）作为约束嵌入优化过程；采用近端策略优化算法（PPO）结合随机探索与阶段引导奖励机制进行路径优化；最后通过统一映射公式将优化路径转化为六轴弯曲机的运动轨迹。

Result: FPRO生成的路径具有更高的几何平滑性，无碰撞，制造可行性强；相比基于笛卡尔坐标的传统方法及现有强化学习基线，在收敛速度、路径长度、终端对齐精度、障碍物避让和可制造性指标上均表现更优；真实制造测试显示数字设计与实物高度一致，验证了方法的实用性。

Conclusion: FPRO框架成功实现了航空发动机自由曲面管道设计与制造的深度融合，显著提升了设计效率与可制造性，具备良好的工程应用前景。

Abstract: Design for manufacturing plays a critical role in advanced aeroengine development, where complex components necessitate careful consideration of manufacturability. However, current practices in pipe routing remain largely decoupled from down-stream manufacturing, leading to labor-intensive, trial-and-error iterations to achieve manufacturable designs. To address this problem, this study proposes the Frenet-based pipe routing optimization (FPRO) framework, a manufacturability knowledge-integrated reinforcement learning approach for free-form pipe design in aeroengines. FPRO formulates the routing problem as a boundary value problem in the Frenet frame. In this framework, the pipe path is represented by curvature and torsion profiles, which are generated using cubic Hermite interpolation. To integrate design and manufacturing, domain-specific manufacturing knowledge is embedded as constraints on the permissible ranges of curvature and torsion. The path optimization is performed using the proximal policy optimization algorithm with stochastic exploration and a stage-guided reward mechanism. A unified mapping formulation then translates the optimized path into motion trajectories for the bending die, enabling direct fabrication on a six-axis free-bending machine. Experimental results demonstrate that FPRO consistently generates collision-free, manufacturable paths with smoother geometric profiles compared to Cartesian-based methods. It also achieves faster convergence and superior performance in terminal alignment, path length, obstacle avoidance, and manufacturability compared to state-of-the-art reinforcement learning baselines. Real-world validation confirms the close geometric correspondence between the manufactured pipe and its digital design, validating the practical feasibility of FPRO.

### [244] [LT2: Linear-Time Looped Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20670)
*Chunyuan Deng,Yizhe Zhang,Rui-Jie Zhu,Yuanyuan Xu,Jiarui Liu,T. S. Eugene Ng,Hanjie Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出LT2（Linear-Time Looped Transformers）系列架构，通过将二次复杂度的softmax注意力替换为亚二次、线性时间注意力，显著提升循环变压器的效率。研究了LT2-linear（线性注意力）、LT2-sparse（稀疏注意力）及其混合版本LT2-hybrid，发现循环机制与这些注意力形式具有独特协同效应：在线性注意力中实现迭代记忆优化，在稀疏注意力中逐步扩大有效感受野。理论分析与实验证明其在记忆回溯、状态跟踪和语言建模任务中的稳定优势。特别地，LT2-hybrid (GDN+DSA) 实现线性时间成本下的高性能，而LT2-hybrid (Full+GDN) 以少量全注意力层大幅提升性能与效率。还展示了将预训练的循环变压器转换为LT2-hybrid模型的方法，所提出的Ouro-hybrid-1.4B模型仅用约10亿词元训练即超越多数10亿参数工业级模型，并接近40亿参数模型表现，同时保持线性时间速度优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有循环变压器（LT）虽具强大能力，但与全注意力结合时仍存在二次计算复杂度，导致效率低下。亟需在不牺牲性能的前提下降低计算开销，推动小规模语言模型向高效、可扩展方向发展。

Method: 提出LT2系列架构，采用线性或稀疏注意力替代传统二次注意力；设计LT2-linear、LT2-sparse及两种混合变体（LT2-hybrid GDN+DSA 和 Full+GDN），利用循环机制实现注意力形式间的互补优化；引入模型转换方法，将预训练的LT模型转化为LT2-hybrid结构。

Result: LT2系列在多个任务中均表现出优于或相当的传统循环变压器性能，且计算效率显著提升。其中，LT2-hybrid (GDN+DSA) 达到线性时间成本下的高质量输出；LT2-hybrid (Full+GDN) 在极低全注意力比例下实现性能超越。转换后的Ouro-hybrid-1.4B模型在10亿词元训练下表现媲美40亿参数工业级模型，兼具高效与高质。

Conclusion: LT2架构通过融合线性与稀疏注意力并利用循环机制的协同效应，成功实现了高效与高性能的平衡，为构建可扩展的小型语言模型提供了清晰路径，显著推动了高效语言模型的发展。

Abstract: Looped Transformers (LT) have emerged as a powerful architecture by iterating their layers multiple times before decoding the final token. However, pairing them with full attention retains quadratic complexity, making them computationally expensive and slow. We introduce LT2 (Linear-Time Looped Transformers), a family of looped architectures that replace quadratic softmax attention with subquadratic, linear-time attention. We study two variants: LT2-linear with linear attention and LT2-sparse with sparse attention. We find that looping uniquely synergizes with these variants: it enables iterative memory refinement in linear attention and progressively expands the effective receptive field in sparse attention. We formalize these benefits theoretically and demonstrate consistent empirical gains across controlled recall, state-tracking, and language modeling tasks. We then explore LT2-hybrid, which combines different attention variants in a looped setting. Two variants are especially promising: LT2-hybrid (GDN+DSA), which interleaves linear and sparse attention to maximize efficiency and matches the standard looped transformer's quality at fully linear-time cost; and LT2-hybrid (Full+GDN), which interleaves GDN with a small fraction of full attention layers to maximize quality, surpassing the standard looped transformer in both performance and efficiency. We also show how to convert a pre-trained LT into an LT2-hybrid model. With about 1B tokens of training, our converted model, Ouro-hybrid-1.4B, outperforms industry-level 1B models and is competitive with industry-level 4B models while retaining the speed benefits of linear-time attention. Together, these results show a clear path toward making looped transformers more scalable and advancing efficient, capable small language models.

Motivation: 传统静态模型难以捕捉非平稳时间序列中的动态分布漂移；现有Mixture-of-Experts（MoE）方法受限于固定专家池和无记忆路由机制，无法有效应对突发的模式切换。

Method: 利用最大均值差异（MMD）检测分布变化，动态创建或移除异构专家以优化模型容量；设计带有循环状态和异常存储库的时间记忆路由器，实现上下文感知且稳定的专家选择，无需测试阶段更新。

Conclusion: Dynamic TMoE成功实现了模型架构的动态演化与时间连续性的协同学习，为非平稳时间序列预测提供了高效、自适应的新范式。

Abstract: Non-stationary time series forecasting is challenged by evolving distribution shifts that static models struggle to capture. While Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) architectures offer a promising paradigm for decoupling complex drift patterns, existing approaches are limited by fixed expert pools and memoryless routing, hampering their ability to adapt to abrupt regime shifts. To address this, we propose Dynamic TMoE, a framework that unifies architectural evolution with temporal continuity during learning phase. By detecting distribution shifts via Maximum Mean Discrepancy (MMD), we dynamically instantiate heterogeneous experts and prune redundant ones to optimize capacity. Additionally, a temporal memory router leverages recurrent states and an anomaly repository to ensure stable, context-aware expert selection without requiring test-time updates. Experiments on nine benchmarks demonstrate state-of-the-art performance, reducing MSE by 10.4% and MAE by 7.8%. Code is available at https://github.com/andone-07/Dynamic-TMoE.

<details>

Abstract: Random forests aggregate tree votes by simple majority, treating all trees as equally informative. We observe that the topological pattern along each tree's root-to-leaf decision path -- where and how often the dominant class label flips along it -- carries a signal of tree reliability that is exploitable for per-sample reweighting. The naive use of this signal is structurally confounded with the predicted class, so we propose a class-conditional ratio weighting that guarantees zero expected class bias by construction. On 30 binary classification benchmarks under a shared-forest, shared-split protocol with 30 repeats, the proposed method is the only one among four compared schemes -- RF, weighted RF, KNORA-Eliminate, KNORA-Union -- to yield a statistically significant accuracy improvement over RF (Wilcoxon p = 0.018), while the three alternatives all fail to do so (p > 0.5). It is also the only scheme without majority-recall regressions, with minority-recall regressions limited to 3/30 datasets -- a one-sided loss to which classical dynamic ensemble selection methods are susceptible. The gain is robust across forest sizes from 100 to 1000 trees.

<details>

Abstract: Generative verifiers have emerged as a promising paradigm for step-wise verification, but their verification behavior is often poorly calibrated: they may be under-critical and miss erroneous steps, or over-critical and reject correct reasoning. We refer to this tendency to be overly lenient or overly critical as verifier strictness. In this work, we study whether verifier strictness can be controlled through hidden-state intervention. We uncover a verification-specific hidden-state signal: in step-wise verification, a verifier's tendency to accept or reject a solution step is encoded near the boundary of the corresponding verification paragraph. Exploiting this signal, we show that hidden-state steering can directly modulate verifier strictness without fine-tuning. However, uniform steering induces a trade-off between error detection and correctness certification. To address this, we propose VerifySteer, which exploits latent correctness signals for sample-level routing and selectively intervenes on paragraph boundaries. Experiments on ProcessBench and Hard2Verify show that VerifySteer outperforms prompt optimization and activation steering baselines, and is competitive with self-consistency while requiring 4-7x less inference compute. VerifySteer is also complementary to verification fine-tuning, providing further gains on top of fine-tuned verifiers. The code is available at https://github.com/YefanZhou/VerifySteer.

### [249] [Correcting Stochastic Update Bias in Preconditioned Language Model Optimizers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20756)
*Nikhil Nayak,Julia White,Urchade Zaratiana,Kelton Zhang,Henrijs Princis,Dhruv Atreja,Henry Fawcett,Matthew Thomas,George Hurn-Maloney,Ash Lewis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种单批次偏差校正框架，以解决预条件优化器在语言模型训练中因有限样本导致的双重偏差问题：梯度与预条件矩阵来自同一小批量引起的耦合偏差，以及预条件矩阵逆或逆根因非线性运算引入的偏差。通过交叉拟合预条件估计和方差校正反演，该框架适用于AdamW、Sophia和Shampoo等优化器，在Qwen2.5-0.5B上分别降低0.15、0.07、0.11 nats的保留损失，且对混合质量预训练和下游指令微调效果为中性至正向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有预条件优化器通常将随机更新规则视为总体预条件下降的直接近似，但忽略了有限样本下的两种偏差：梯度与预条件估计的耦合偏差，以及预条件矩阵逆运算带来的非线性偏差。这些偏差影响优化性能，亟需校正。

Method: 提出单批次偏差校正框架：采用交叉拟合预条件（从独立微批次组中估计梯度和预条件）和方差校正反演（利用微批次变异性减去主导的delta方法偏差项），适用于对角动量、对角曲率及矩阵预条件方法。

Result: 在Qwen2.5-0.5B上，偏差校正使预训练损失分别降低0.15（AdamW）、0.07（Sophia）、0.11（Shampoo）nats；对混合质量预训练和下游任务表现均呈中性至正向影响。

Conclusion: 偏差校正是一种实用机制，可有效减少有限样本更新偏差，提升预条件优化器的性能。

Abstract: Preconditioned optimizers are central to language model training, but their stochastic update rules are usually treated as direct approximations to population preconditioned descent. We show that this view misses two finite-sample biases. First, the gradient and preconditioner are typically estimated from the same minibatch, introducing gradient--preconditioner coupling bias. Second, even when the preconditioner estimate is unbiased, its inverse or inverse-root is generally biased because inversion is nonlinear. We propose a single-batch bias-correction framework that addresses both effects: cross-fitted preconditioning estimates the numerator and preconditioner from independent microbatch groups, while variance-corrected inversion uses microbatch variability to subtract the leading delta-method bias term. The framework applies to diagonal moment, diagonal curvature, and matrix preconditioning methods, instantiated in AdamW, Sophia, and Shampoo. Bias correction reduces held-out pretraining loss on Qwen2.5-0.5B by $0.15$, $0.07$, and $0.11$ nats, respectively; the effects on mixed-quality pretraining and downstream instruction tuning are consistently neutral-to-positive. Together, these results establish bias correction as a practical mechanism for reducing finite-sample update bias and improving the performance of preconditioned optimizers.

### [250] [Most Transformer Modifications Still Do Not Transfer at 1-3B: A 2020-2026 Update to Narang et al. (2021) with Downstream Evaluation and a Noise Floor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20798)
*Yang Zhao,Jiahao Lu,Bin Huang,Guhua Zhang,Jie Zhou*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Transformer架构改进方法缺乏在现代大模型（1-3B参数）下的系统性验证，且传统以预训练困惑度为指标的评估方式已不适用。本文旨在通过严格的控制实验，重新审视这些新方法的真实有效性。

Method: 在1.2B和3B参数规模下，对20种后2021年提出的Transformer修改进行严格iso-data、iso-compute、iso-recipe控制实验；使用多种子基线噪声水平，以CLIMB-12作为主要下游评估指标，并考察跨规模训练稳定性。

Conclusion: 在1-3B规模下进行架构比较时，必须包含噪声基线报告、下游评估和跨规模稳定性测试，否则易误判模型改进效果。

Abstract: Narang et al. (2021) evaluated 40+ Transformer modifications at T5-base scale and concluded that most did not transfer. Five years later, the typical working regime has moved to 1-3B parameters, downstream evaluation has replaced pretraining perplexity, and a substantially different catalogue of modifications has emerged. We revisit their question by testing 20 post-2021 Transformer modifications at 1.2B and 3B under strict iso-data, iso-compute, iso-recipe control, with a multi-seed baseline noise floor and CLIMB-12 downstream evaluation as the primary metric. The central finding reproduces theirs at this curated set: most modifications do not transfer. Of the 20 modifications, only two clear Bonferroni correction at 1.2B; one of those two further fails to train stably at 3B under the shared recipe. We also find that the loss-downstream gap reported by Tay et al. (2023) enlarges several-fold for attention-output modifications: two significant failures converge to within 2-3% of baseline validation loss yet drop 6-16 CLIMB-points. We conclude that noise-floor reporting, downstream evaluation, and cross-scale stability testing are now prerequisites for architecture comparisons at 1-3B.

### [251] [Cumulative Meta-Learning from Active Learning Queries for Robustness to Spurious Correlations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20771)
*Kin Whye Chew,Jingxian Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CAML 是一种新的主动学习框架，通过利用查询样本元学习模型的先验（归纳偏置），以更好地区分核心特征与虚假相关性。它将每一轮主动学习视为一个元学习任务，通过累积式地更新归纳偏置，捕捉不同轮次间的序列依赖关系。相比传统方法仅更新似然项，CAML 通过引入交互项增强模型对关键特征的学习能力。实验表明，在多个存在虚假相关性的基准测试中，CAML 显著提升了少数群体的准确率，提升幅度最高达29.9%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实世界数据中的虚假相关性导致机器学习模型依赖无关模式，影响可靠性、泛化性和公平性。标准主动学习方法仅简单添加查询样本，无法有效强化模型对核心特征的识别，尤其在深度学习中易被大标签集稀释或过拟合。因此需要一种能持续优化模型归纳偏置的方法来应对这一挑战。

Method: 提出累积式主动元学习（CAML），将每轮主动学习视为元学习任务：当前标签集作为元训练数据，新查询批次作为元测试数据。通过维护并逐步优化累积的归纳偏置，捕捉主动学习轮次间的序列依赖关系，并引入交互项以建模早期元学习偏置与后期查询目标之间的耦合。

Result: CAML 在多个虚假相关性基准上显著提升少数群体准确率：在 Dominoes 上提升 27.8%，Waterbirds 上提升 29.9%，SpuCo 上提升 14.3%，CivilComments 上提升 24.0%。表明其在增强模型鲁棒性与公平性方面具有显著优势。

Conclusion: CAML 通过累积式元学习机制，有效缓解了虚假相关性带来的模型偏差问题，提升了模型在复杂现实场景下的泛化能力与公平性。该方法为解决主动学习中的误导性模式依赖提供了新思路。

Abstract: Spurious correlations in real-world datasets cause machine learning models to rely on irrelevant patterns, undermining reliability, generalization, and fairness. Active learning offers a promising way to address this failure mode by querying informative samples that distinguish core features from spurious ones. However, standard active-learning methods simply append queried examples to the labeled set, effectively updating only the likelihood term. In deep learning regimes, the influence of these informative samples can be diluted by the larger labeled set and memorized by overparameterized models. We propose Cumulative Active Meta-Learning (CAML), an active-learning framework that uses queried examples to meta-learn the prior, or inductive bias, governing how the model adapts. CAML casts each active-learning round as a meta-learning task: the current labeled set serves as meta-train data for adaptation, while the newly queried batch serves as meta-test data for evaluating generalization. Unlike conventional meta-learning, which treats tasks as independent and identically distributed, CAML exploits the sequential dependence between active-learning rounds by maintaining a cumulative inductive bias that is progressively refined. Theoretically, we show that this cumulative formulation introduces interaction terms that couple earlier meta-learned inductive biases with later query-induced objectives, capturing dependencies absent from standard meta-learning. Empirically, CAML improves minority-group accuracy across spurious-correlation benchmarks and acquisition strategies, with gains of up to 27.8% on Dominoes, 29.9% on Waterbirds, 14.3% on SpuCo, and 24.0% on CivilComments.

Method: 提出 Tunable MAGMAX 框架，利用偏好向量动态控制模型合并时从各任务向量中选取的元素数量，并基于少量目标环境数据与训练数据自动构建偏好向量，实现无手动干预的性能调控。

Abstract: Continual learning (CL) aims to train models sequentially on multiple tasks while mitigating catastrophic forgetting of previously learned knowledge. Recent advances in large pre-trained models (LPMs) and model merging techniques, such as MAGMAX, have demonstrated effective CL performance by combining task-specific parameters. However, existing methods primarily focus on average performance across all tasks and do not adequately address how to construct models accommodating different deployment environments or varying user preferences. This paper proposes a model merging framework, termed Tunable MAGMAX, which enables preference-aware control of task-specific performance in CL.
